### [1] [Anomalous suppression of quantum chaos between two integrable limits](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05506)
*Roopayan Ghosh,Henry Davenport,Frank Schindler*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文发现，具有时间反演对称性的非可积多体系统——相互作用Su-Schrieffer-Heeger模型——的平均能级间距比明显低于高斯正交系综（GOE）的混沌预测值，挑战了非可积性必然导致完全混沌谱的常规认识。通过精确对角化和半解析论证，作者将此反常归因于多体带态的非完全杂化，并展示了该机制在打破手征和反演对称性下的鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 挑战“非可积系统必然呈现高斯正交系综（GOE）混沌谱统计”这一传统认识，揭示存在一类非可积多体系统，其谱统计显著偏离GOE预测。

Method: 采用精确对角化（exact diagonalization）数值方法，辅以半解析（semi-analytical）论证，分析相互作用Su-Schrieffer-Heeger模型的能级统计；并扩展模型以检验机制在打破手征对称性（chiral symmetry）和反演对称性（inversion symmetry）下的鲁棒性。

Result: 该模型的平均能级间距比$\langle r\rangle$明显低于GOE预测值约0.535，且该偏差在深非可积区域持续存在。谱异常源于多体带态（many-body band states）的非完全杂化，这一机制削弱了能级排斥（level repulsion）但未恢复可积性。打破手征和反演对称性后该机制依然稳健。

Conclusion: 非可积性并不必然导致完全混沌的谱统计；由非相互作用能带结构继承而来的不完全杂化会重塑谱结构，弱化能级排斥，从而产生偏离GOE的统计行为。

Abstract: Level statistics in non-integrable quantum many-body systems with time reversal symmetry are expected to follow the Gaussian Orthogonal Ensemble (GOE), a hallmark of quantum chaos. However, we show that the interacting Su-Schrieffer-Heeger model exhibits a clear suppression of the mean level-spacing ratio $\langle r\rangle$ from the GOE value $\approx 0.535$, persisting deep in the nonintegrable regime. This challenges the conventional association between non-integrability and fully chaotic spectral statistics. Using exact diagonalization supported by semi-analytical arguments, we trace this anomaly to incomplete hybridization of many-body band states inherited from the noninteracting band structure. The resulting restructuring of the spectrum weakens level repulsion without restoring integrability. We show the robustness of this mechanism in extensions of the model which break chiral and inversion symmetry.

</details>


### [2] [Complete local expansion of the availability function in random sequential adsorption of aligned squares at low density: Termination at fourth order](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05634)
*F. Tolea,M. Tolea*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该论文推导了定向正方形随机顺序吸附（RSA）中可用性函数 α(q) 的低覆盖率展开，至覆盖度 q 的四阶。展开在四阶精确终止，并通过几何容斥原理和数值模拟验证了系数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解低覆盖率下定向正方形随机顺序吸附（random sequential adsorption, RSA）过程中可用空间减少的机制，即通过几何重叠分析来刻画排除区域（exclusion regions）对新增颗粒吸附可能性的影响。

Method: 采用基于排除区域几何重叠的容斥展开（inclusion-exclusion expansion），系统枚举所有几何上允许的多体构型，推导可用性函数 α(q) 的低覆盖率展开至四阶。进一步通过在离散格点上的数值模拟验证展开系数的准确性。

Result: 展开在四阶精确终止，因为最多四个已沉积的正方形可以同时与一个试探插入位置的排除区域重叠。通过枚举所有几何允许的构型获得展开系数，数值模拟结果与理论系数在统计误差内一致。

Conclusion: 对于定向正方形的 RSA 过程，可用性函数 α(q) 的低覆盖率展开具有有限阶终止性，系数可由容斥原理精确确定，且数值模拟支持该理论结果的正确性。

Abstract: We consider random sequential adsorption (RSA) of aligned squares and derive the low-coverage expansion of the availability function alpha(q), the fraction of positions accessible to an additional square, up to fourth order in the coverage q. At low coverage, the reduction of available space can be understood in terms of geometric overlap between exclusion regions created by previously deposited squares. A single square blocks a finite area; pairs of squares may have overlapping exclusion zones, reducing the total blocked area; similarly, three and four squares can share a common overlap region, leading to higher-order corrections. These contributions can be systematically accounted for through an inclusion-exclusion expansion based on the geometry of overlapping exclusion regions, with alternating signs dictated by inclusion-exclusion. The expansion terminates exactly at fourth order, since no more than four deposited squares can simultaneously overlap the exclusion region of a trial insertion. The coefficients are obtained by explicit enumeration of all such geometrically admissible configurations and are further confirmed by numerical simulations on a discrete lattice, showing agreement within statistical uncertainty.

</details>


### [3] [Quantum Density of States and Integer Partitions: A Semiclassical Approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06146)
*M. V. N. Murthy,Matthias Brack*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该综述探讨了半经典方法(semi-classical methods)如何同时描述物理中的多体系统和解析数论(analytic number theory)中的整数分拆(integer partitions)，重点揭示了统计力学(statistical mechanics)与数分拆之间的深层联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管统计力学与数论看似截然不同，但两者分别处理能量在粒子间的分布与整数被拆分为其他整数的方式，其基本问题在数学结构上具有高度相似性。作者旨在通过半经典方法(特别是周期轨道理论)架起两个领域之间的桥梁。

Method: 从单粒子量子态密度(level density)出发，通过半经典迹公式(semiclassical trace formula)建立态密度与经典周期轨道(periodic orbits)之间的联系，再推广到多粒子系统。利用态密度的平均(光滑)部分在离散整数自变量处再现渐近数分拆(asymptotic number partition)行为；对于特殊的分立平方分拆(distinct square partitions)，则用毕达哥拉斯三元数(Pythagorean number triples)表征的少数周期轨道解释其显著振荡。

Result: 态密度的平均部分可以在整数自变量处重现渐近数分拆；在分立平方分拆情形中，周期轨道理论通过少量轨道即可准确再现明显的振荡结构。此外，还针对素数的整数分拆(包括无限制和分立两种情况)给出了若干新结果。

Conclusion: 半经典方法能够有效统一处理统计力学与整数分拆中的渐近行为与振荡特征。特别地，分立平方分拆中规则振荡的存在性(尽管渐近趋于零)可能与费马定理(Fermat's theorem)相关，值得进一步探讨。

Abstract: In this review we discuss semi-classical methods that are traditionally used to describe many-body systems in physics, but may also be used to describe partitions of integers in analytic number theory. Specifically, we explore the connection between the methods of statistical mechanics and number partitions. Though the two fields appear very different, their fundamental issues bear a close resemblance. In the former case it is the distribution of a given amount of energy among the particles in an ensemble at a given temperature with well defined properties, while in the latter case it is the way an integer is partitioned into other integers, with or without restrictions. We begin with a discussion of the single-particle quantum density of states, also called the level density, in which we illustrate the connection between the density of states and the classical periodic orbits through the semiclassical trace formula. This is then extended to many particle systems. We show that the asymptotic number partition is reproduced by the average (smooth) part of the level density at discrete integer values of the argument. In the especially interesting case of distinct square partitions, pronounced oscillations are well reproduced by the periodic orbit theory in terms of a few orbits characterised by Pythagorean number triples. We speculate on the connection to Fermat's theorem as to why such regular oscillations (though vanishing asymptotically) exist only in this special case. Finally, we discuss some new results for integer partitions of primes, both unrestricted and distinct.

</details>


### [4] [Modern view of activated rate processes: unidirectional fluxes at equilibrium, correlation functions, and splitting probabilities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05672)
*Alexander M. Berezhkovskii,Kevin Song,Dmitrii E. Makarov*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文基于克拉默斯（Kramers）80多年前提出的布朗粒子逃逸势垒模型，从多个视角严格论证了如何将连续动力学映射为离散态化学动力学，指出基于势垒顶位置进行状态划分的朴素方法不可行，而应考虑轨迹历史，从而构建反应物与产物系综，并在条件转移概率定义的速率与时间演化算子（time-evolution operator）的弛豫模式两种视角下实现自洽描述。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 克拉默斯模型虽已被核物理、生物物理和化学物理领域广泛采用，但从化学动力学角度看，如何将连续动力学严格映射为离散态的化学动力学（chemical kinetics）仍有待澄清。近期进展促使作者对该映射提供一种严格方法，并解释克拉默斯理论为何有效以及如何从多个视角加以理解。

Method: 将系统平衡系综划分为对应反应物（reactant）与产物（product）的两个子系综，并考虑子系综之间的通量（fluxes）。关键在于：基于相对于势垒顶（barrier top）位置的朴素分割无法得到物理上合理的映射，而应考虑轨迹历史。在此基础上构建的反应物与产物系综，可从两个互补视角——基于条件转移概率定义的速率（rate）以及基于时间演化算子弛豫模式（relaxation modes）——提供内部自洽的问题描述。

Result: 论文指出，仅依据位置（相对于势垒顶）划分反应物与产物状态是不足的，必须引入轨迹历史信息才能得到物理上成立的映射。由此构建的反应物与产物系综在两种不同理论视角下均能给出自洽的描述。

Conclusion: 该视角论文（Perspective）为克拉默斯理论从连续动力学到离散态化学动力学的映射提供了严格框架，揭示了该理论有效性的深层原因，并统一了传统速率定义与时间演化算子弛豫模式两种分析视角。

Abstract: More than 80 years ago Kramers published a paper calculating how fast a Brownian particle escapes from a potential well over an activation barrier. Since then Kramers' model has been widely adopted by nuclear physics, biophysics and chemical physics communities as a description of activated barrier crossing. From a chemical kinetics perspective, Kramers' theory provides a mapping from continuous dynamics to discrete-state chemical kinetics. Motivated by recent developments, this Perspective provides a rigorous way of performing such a mapping, explaining why and how Kramers' theory works from several points of view. Specifically, we consider transitions of a Brownian particle between two potential wells corresponding to the ``reactant'' and the ``product'' of a chemical reaction. A central unifying idea is to divide the equilibrium ensemble of possible states of the system into two sub-ensembles corresponding to the reactant and product states and then to consider fluxes between these sub-ensembles. Importantly, naive separation based on the location measured relative to the barrier top does not result in a mapping that is physically tenable, and instead the past of the trajectory should be considered. Thus constructed reactant and product ensembles provide an internally consistent description of the problem when also viewed from two different perspectives: one based on the definition of the rate as a conditional transition probability per unit time and the other based on the relaxation modes of the time-evolution operator governing the dynamics.

</details>


### [5] [The Ramsey community number as a renormalization-group crossing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05954)
*Alexei Vazquez*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文在金刚石分形层级晶格上证明，拉姆齐社区数（Ramsey community number）$r_k$ 是一个精确的重整化群（renormalization-group）穿越量，给出了其闭式解，并发现了一个精确的社区有序相（community-ordered phase）：最优划分的社区数 $q_{\rm opt}\sim\sqrt{n}$ 随网络规模增长，且该层次结构通过一系列一级相变（first-order transitions）逐层热力学有序化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 拉姆齐社区数 $r_k$ 定义为在贝叶斯检测规则（Bayesian detection rule）下，网络用社区（communities）描述优于无社区描述的最小规模。本文旨在阐明该量的精确重整化群（renormalization-group）性质，并探索其背后的热力学有序行为。

Method: 在金刚石分形层级晶格（diamond hierarchical lattice）上，建立块模型充分统计量（block-model sufficient statistics）的线性映射（特征值为 $\{bs,b\}$），分析度校正证据密度（degree-corrected evidence density）向社区固定点（community fixed point）$\ln K$ 的流动，并推导 $r_k(b,s;q)$ 的闭式解。同时，将赖夏特–博恩霍尔特社区哈密顿量（Reichardt–Bornholdt community Hamiltonian）置于该晶格上，研究其基态与相变行为。

Result: $r_k$ 是运行证据（running evidence）越过检测阈值（detection threshold）的生成代（generation）；度校正（degree correction）可使检测提前两个代次；给出了整个参数族 $r_k(b,s;q)$ 的闭式解。在铁磁临界温度（ferromagnetic critical temperature）以下，两个枢纽（hubs）锁定于相反社区，形成持续到 $n\to\infty$ 的交错有序（staggered order）。最优划分的社区数 $q_{\rm opt}\sim\sqrt{n}$ 随网络增长，且通过一系列一级相变（first-order transitions）逐层有序化，每个稳定层级的温度按 $1/\ln q$ 下降。

Conclusion: 该系统中的涌现划分（emergent partition）同时满足可检测性（detectable）、最优性（optimal）和热力学有序性（thermodynamically ordered）。每一稳定层级均持续到 $n\to\infty$，表明社区结构可在无限大系统中保持有序。

Abstract: The Ramsey community number $r_k$ is the smallest size at which a network is better described by communities than by none, under a Bayesian detection rule. On the diamond hierarchical lattice we show that $r_k$ is an exact renormalization-group crossing: the block-model sufficient statistics obey a linear map with eigenvalues $\{bs,b\}$, the degree-corrected evidence density flows to $\ln K$ at a community fixed point, and $r_k$ is the generation at which the running evidence clears the detection threshold. Degree correction advances detection by two generations. We derive $r_k(b,s;q)$ in closed form for the whole family. Finally, placing on the lattice the Reichardt--Bornholdt community Hamiltonian -- whose ground state is the partition itself -- we find an exact community-ordered phase: below the ferromagnetic critical temperature the two hubs lock into opposite communities for any resolution $γ>0$, a staggered order that persists as $n\to\infty$. Allowing each nested sub-community its own label, the optimal partition is a hierarchy of $q_{\rm opt}\sim\sqrt{n}$ communities, so the number of Potts states that best describes the network grows with the network. This hierarchy orders thermally level by level, through a cascade of first-order transitions whose temperatures fall as $1/\ln q$, so every stable level persists as $n\to\infty$: the emergent partition is detectable, optimal, and thermodynamically ordered.

</details>


### [6] [Identifying Non-Ideal Reaction-Diffusion Systems Unable to Maintain Diffusion Out-of-Equilibrium](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06030)
*Francesco Avanzini,Timur Aslyamov,Massimiliano Esposito*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文发展了一种基于动力学势（kinetic potential，作为李雅普诺夫函数）的通用方法，用于判断在非理想反应-扩散系统（non-ideal reaction-diffusion systems）中，当受到自主均匀化学恒化器（chemostats）驱动时，扩散是否必然达到平衡。该方法推广了先前工作（J. Chem. Phys. 161, 174108 (2024)）的结果，放宽了部分假设，证明当化学反应网络满足伪细致平衡（pseudo-detailed balanced）或复平衡（complex balanced）时，扩散均会平衡，且两类网络对反应通量的不同约束源于其不同的化学计量性质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在判断非理想反应-扩散系统在开放驱动下是否必然达到扩散平衡时存在局限性，需要更普适的理论框架。作者旨在推广先前结果，并揭示不同网络类型对平衡条件的影响机制。

Method: 构造一个作为李雅普诺夫函数（Lyapunov function）的动力学势（kinetic potential），以此判断扩散必然平衡的充分条件。该方法适用于受自主均匀化学恒化器（chemostats）驱动的非理想反应-扩散系统（non-ideal reaction-diffusion systems）。

Result: 证明了在两类化学反应网络下扩散均会平衡：一类是伪细致平衡（pseudo-detailed balanced）网络，其反应通量受反应物与产物的化学计量数共同控制；另一类是复平衡（complex balanced）网络，其反应通量仅受反应物种类的化学计量数控制。两类网络对反应通量的不同约束源于其不同的化学计量性质。

Conclusion: 提出的动力学势方法可统一判断非理想反应-扩散系统在恒化器驱动下的扩散平衡条件。伪细致平衡与复平衡网络在反应通量约束上的差异，从根本上由化学计量性质决定。

Abstract: We develop a general method, based on the construction of a kinetic potential acting as a Lyapunov function, to establish when diffusion necessarily equilibrates in non-ideal reaction-diffusion systems, under arbitrary driving by autonomous homogeneous chemostats. Using this method, we generalize the results of J. Chem. Phys. 161, 174108 (2024) by relaxing some of the underlying assumptions. Specifically, we show that diffusion equilibrates in reaction-diffusion systems whose chemical reaction network is either pseudo-detailed balanced, with reaction fluxes controlled by the stoichiometry of reactants and products, or complex balanced, with reaction fluxes controlled only by the stoichiometry of the reactants. The different constraints on the reaction fluxes are shown to originate from the distinct stoichiometric properties of the two classes of networks.

</details>


### [7] [Conditional Residence Times and Sequential Transition Dynamics of an Overdamped Dimere](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06110)
*Dhruv Agrawal,W. L. Reenbohn*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究了在热涨落和弱周期力作用下，过阻尼二聚体（overdamped dimer）在双稳势阱（bistable potential）中的完成动力学（completion dynamics）。利用条件驻留时间（Conditional Residence Time, CRT）量化两个单体先后跨越势垒（barrier）之间的延迟，发现CRT的分布由滞后单体的逃逸时间与外驱周期之间的竞争决定，并且平均CRT随驱动频率呈非单调变化，从而将耦合系统中的跃迁启动与完成区分为两个独立过程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究多关注耦合系统中单个或同步的势垒穿越行为，但两个单体先后完成穿越之间的延迟动力学尚缺乏定量刻画。本文旨在区分跃迁的启动（initiation）与完成（completion），并引入CRT作为测量工具来研究这一延迟过程。

Method: 构建一个过阻尼二聚体在双稳势阱中的动力学模型，系统受热涨落（thermal fluctuations）和弱周期力（weak periodic force）驱动。两个单体初始位于同一势阱中，先由靠近势垒的单体完成首次跳跃，随后利用条件驻留时间（CRT）量化第二个单体等待并完成跨越的延迟时间。根据不同时间窗口（立即、第一周期、后续周期）对CRT分布进行分析。

Result: CRT分布呈现出由滞后单体的逃逸时间（escape time）与外驱动周期（time period of the external drive）之间的竞争所决定的定性不同的区域。弱耦合（weak coupling）条件下延迟效应最强，完成过程会分散到多个强迫周期中。改变驱动频率时，滞后单体在特定周期内完成跃迁的概率在三个时间窗口之间重新分配，导致平均CRT随频率呈非单调（non-monotonic）变化。

Conclusion: 耦合系统中跃迁的启动与完成是两个分离的过程。CRT是量化耦合随机系统（coupled stochastic systems）中顺序势垒穿越动力学的有效度量。

Abstract: We investigate the completion dynamics of an overdamped dimer moving in a bistable potential under thermal fluctuations and a weak periodic force. Both monomers start in one of the two wells separated by a barrier. The transition is initiated when the monomer closer to the barrier makes a jump across it. The completion dynamics refers to the next part of the dynamics where the second monomer has to wait for some time before it can follow up. We use the Conditional Residence Time (CRT) to study the delay between the successive barrier crossing of the two monomers. The CRT distributions highlight qualitatively different regimes formed by the competition between the escape times of the lagging monomer and the time period of the external drive. The effect is strongest in the weak coupling regime where the delayed completion is spread across multiple forcing cycles. By partitioning this process into three windows, i.e. the immediate, first cycle and later cycles, we show that the probability that the lagging monomer will make a transition in the said cycle is redistributed among these pathways as we change the frequency of the drive. This leads to a non-monotonic dependence of the mean CRT on the frequency of the drive. Our results demonstrate that transition initiation and completion in a coupled system are two separate processes and establish CRT as a useful measure to quantify the sequential barrier crossing dynamics in coupled stochastic systems.

</details>


### [8] [Hidden Entropy Production at Mechanical Stall: Exact Reconstruction in a Reciprocal Brownian Motor](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06131)
*Mesfin Mesfin Taye*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该论文证明，在互易布朗马达（reciprocal Brownian motor）中，可以通过仅观测机械锁定坐标（mechanically stalled coordinate）的测量数据，精确重建隐藏在其后的熵产生（entropy production）。作者引入一个最小可解析的朗之万马达模型（Langevin motor），其中观测平移坐标与隐藏内转子通过单一周期性势能互易耦合，并基于力–扭矩互易性与平移对称性推导出局部流恒等式，从而闭合隐藏的热力学账目。Harada–Sasa热（heat）等于观测坐标的正电流平方耗散，信息流修正项严格为零。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法通常需要分离时间尺度或观测所有自由度才能重构隐藏的熵产生；该工作旨在探索在互易耦合系统中，是否可以仅利用单一观测坐标的测量数据来精确重建隐藏的热力学量，而不依赖时间尺度分离。

Method: 构造了一个最小、可解析求解的朗之万马达模型，其中观测平移坐标$x$与隐藏内转子$\theta$通过单一周期性势能$V(x-\ell\theta)$互易耦合，使得内部扭矩$\tau_{\rm int}=-\ell F_x$恒成立。利用力–扭矩互易性（force–torque reciprocity）与平移对称性推导局部流恒等式（local current identity），该恒等式将隐藏自由度的概率流与观测自由度的量直接关联，从而闭合隐藏热力学账目。最终，基于该恒等式证明Harada–Sasa关系。

Result: 证明了在互易布朗马达中，隐藏于机械锁定坐标后的熵产生可以通过仅对该坐标的测量数据精确重建，无需时间尺度分离。发现Maruyama–Sasa热与Harada–Sasa热在该互易类中完全相等，且Harada–Sasa热等于观测坐标的正电流平方耗散（positive current-square dissipation），而信息流修正项（information-flow correction）严格为零。

Conclusion: 该工作揭示了一个新的互易布朗马达类，其中隐藏热力学量可仅由观测坐标的轨迹数据精确推断。关键创新在于不需要时间尺度分离，且Harada–Sasa关系中的信息流修正项为零，这为实验上仅通过有限观测数据推断系统热力学提供了理论基础。

Abstract: We show that in a reciprocal Brownian motor the entropy production hidden behind a mechanically stalled coordinate can be reconstructed exactly from measurements of that coordinate alone. We introduce a minimal, analytically solvable Langevin motor in which an observed translational coordinate is coupled reciprocally to a hidden internal rotor: a single periodic potential $V(x-\ellθ)$ generates both the force on the observed coordinate and the reaction torque on the hidden one, so that $τ_{\rm int}=-\ell F_x$ holds identically. Force--torque reciprocity together with translational symmetry produces a local current identity that closes the hidden thermodynamic bookkeeping. From it we prove that the Harada--Sasa heat measured through the observed coordinate equals the positive current-square dissipation of that coordinate, with the information-flow correction vanishing identically. eciprocal class. ries in that it requires no separation of time scales.

</details>


### [9] [Thermodynamic phase transitions in lattice spin systems with severe kinetic constraints: Numerical simulation results](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06205)
*Ruifeng Liu,Jianwen Zhou,Yejia Chen,Jiahang Chen,Hai-Jun Zhou*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文通过大规模数值模拟，研究了二维正方晶格和三维立方晶格上具有超参数 K=1 的 Fredrickson-Andersen 模型中未冻结子系统的热力学相变。发现未冻结子系统的巨连通分量在临界初始填充密度 ρ_c 处崩塌（正方晶格 ρ_c=0.2475，立方晶格 ρ_c=0.2809），该相变属于常规格点逾渗（site percolation）的普适类；同时观察到立方晶格的基态在 ρ^*=0.1423 处经历连续晶体-玻璃相变，而正方晶格的基态在任意正 ρ 下长程序即被破坏。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在严重约束动力学晶格自旋系统（如 Fredrickson-Andersen 模型）中，部分格点可能因动力学约束而永久冻结，剩余未冻结子系统的热力学行为尚待阐明。本研究旨在通过数值模拟揭示该未冻结子系统的相变特性及其与格点逾渗的关联。

Method: 采用大规模数值模拟方法，对二维正方晶格和三维立方晶格上的 Fredrickson-Andersen 模型（超参数 K=1）进行模拟研究。从随机初始构型出发，分析未冻结子系统的巨连通分量随初始填充密度 ρ 的变化，并通过有限尺寸标度（finite-size scaling）等方法判定相变临界点及普适类。

Result: 未冻结子系统的巨连通分量在临界密度 ρ_c 处发生崩塌，正方晶格 ρ_c=0.2475，立方晶格 ρ_c=0.2809，该相变与常规格点逾渗属于同一普适类。立方晶格的基态在 ρ^*=0.1423 处呈现连续的晶体-玻璃相变；正方晶格的基态中，只要初始填充密度 ρ>0，长程晶序即被破坏。

Conclusion: 严重约束下的未冻结子系统在二维和三维晶格中均呈现出与格点逾渗同普适类的几何相变，且其基态行为随空间维度不同而显著差异：三维中存在晶体-玻璃相变，二维中长程晶序对任意正密度均不稳定。

Abstract: The Fredrickson-Andersen model with hyperparameter $K=1$ is a severely constrained kinetic lattice spin system, such that any site is temporarily blocked from changing its packing state (empty or occupied) if there is one or more occupied nearest neighbors. Starting from a completely random initial configuration with a fraction $ρ$ of sites being occupied, some of the sites may be permanently frozen to their initial state under this severe kinetic constraint. The remaining sites can switch states at least occasionally, and they form the unfrozen subsystem associated with the given initial configuration. In the present work we investigate thermodynamic phase transitions in such unfrozen subsystems of the two-dimensional square lattice and the three-dimensional cubic lattice by extensive numerical simulations. We demonstrate that the giant connected component of the unfrozen subsystem collapses at certain critical value $ρ_{c}$ of initial packing density, with $ρ_c = 0.2475$ for the square lattice and $ρ_c = 0.2809$ for the cubic lattice. This phase transition belongs to the same universality class of the conventional site percolation. We also observe that the ground states (densest packing configurations) experience a continuous crystal-to-glass phase transition at the critical value $ρ^* = 0.1423$ of initial packing density for the cubic lattice. For the two-dimensional square lattice we argue that long-range crystalline order is destroyed in the ground states as long as the initial packing density $ρ$ is positive.

</details>


### [10] [Robust q-negative Multifractal Detrended Cross-Correlation Coefficient](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06324)
*Thiago B. Murari,José Fernando F. Mendes,Hernane B. B. Pereira,Marcelo A. Moret*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文针对多重分形去趋势交叉相关系数在负波动阶数下的数值不稳定性问题，提出了一种有符号的多重分形去趋势交叉相关系数（Signed Multifractal Detrended Cross-Correlation Coefficient, ρ_SMFDCCA），该系数通过局部归一化去趋势相关和正则化波动振幅，在正负q值下均严格有界于[-1,1]，无需额外校正，并应用于股票指数和温度记录以揭示尺度与振幅依赖的交叉相关结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的多重分形去趋势交叉相关系数（multifractal detrended cross-correlation coefficient, ρ_q(n)）在应用于负波动阶数（negative fluctuation orders）时受到数值不稳定性（numerical instabilities）、无界值（unbounded values）和解释困难（interpretational difficulties）的困扰，亟需一种稳健且可解释的替代方案。

Method: 提出一种基于振幅条件（amplitude-conditioned）的有符号多重分形去趋势交叉相关系数 ρ_SMFDCCA，核心思路是利用局部归一化去趋势相关（locally normalized detrended correlations）和正则化波动振幅（regularized fluctuation amplitudes）来构造可观测量，从而保留局部相互作用的符号并确保结果严格有界。

Result: 使用独立分数高斯噪声（independent fractional Gaussian noise）验证表明，该方法无虚假交叉相关（spurious cross-correlations），且数值稳定。实际应用显示，该系数能解析交叉相关随时间尺度（temporal scale）和波动振幅（fluctuation amplitude）的联合演化，揭示出股票市场指数在大波动期间更强的同步性（stronger synchronization）以及温度记录中异质的耦合模式（heterogeneous coupling patterns）。

Conclusion: 所提出的有符号多重分形去趋势交叉相关系数消除了此前方法所需的校正步骤，在正负q值下均保持严格有界，为研究尺度依赖的交叉相互作用提供了一种数值稳定、无需额外处理的可靠工具。

Abstract: The multifractal detrended cross-correlation coefficient $ρ_q(n)$ is widely used to investigate scale-dependent interactions, but its application to negative fluctuation orders is affected by numerical instabilities, unbounded values, and interpretational difficulties. We propose a Signed Multifractal Detrended Cross-Correlation Coefficient, $ρ_{\mathrm{SMFDCCA}}(n,q)$, an amplitude-conditioned correlation observable for multifractal detrended analysis, based on locally normalized detrended correlations and regularized fluctuation amplitudes. The proposed coefficient preserves the sign of local interactions, remains strictly bounded within $[-1,1]$ for both positive and negative values of $q$, and eliminates the corrective procedures required by previous approaches. Validation using independent fractional Gaussian noise confirms the absence of spurious cross-correlations and the numerical stability of the method. Applications demonstrate that the proposed observable resolves how cross-correlations evolve jointly with temporal scale and fluctuation amplitude, revealing scale- and amplitude-dependent correlation structures, including stronger synchronization during large fluctuations in stock-market indices and heterogeneous coupling patterns in temperature records.

</details>


### [11] [Static vacancies as parametrized conformal defects in the critical $J_1$--$J_2$ transverse-field Ising chain](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06511)
*R. L. Silva,R. C. Silva,R. J. C. Lopes,A. R. Pereira*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文利用密度矩阵重整化群（DMRG）方法，研究横场伊辛链（transverse-field Ising chain）临界线上两个静态非磁性空位（vacancy）之间的相互作用。结果显示，沿整个量子临界线，空位间相互作用呈代数衰减（algebraic decay），衰减指数α接近普适卡西米尔值（Casimir value）1，并随次近邻耦合J₂有微弱但系统的依赖；自旋关联函数跨越空位的透射比（transmission ratio）随J₂单调增长，而Affleck-Ludwig边界熵（boundary entropy）保持较小且近似常数。三个观测量随J₂光滑单调变化，构成一个由J₂控制的单参数部分透射共形缺陷族（conformal defect family）。整个临界线借助体自旋关联函数指数η=1/4精确定位。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有研究考察了能隙相（gapped regime）中空位-空位相互作用呈指数衰减的行为，但沿量子临界线（quantum critical line）上该相互作用的性质尚不清楚。本文旨在填补这一空白，系统研究临界区域中空位相互作用的标度行为。

Method: 采用密度矩阵重整化群（density-matrix renormalization-group, DMRG）方法，对最多含N=300个格点的开放链进行数值计算。临界线通过体自旋关联函数指数η=1/4（伊辛普适类（Ising universality class）的有序参量指数）进行定位。

Result: 沿临界线，空位间相互作用呈代数衰减 |Δ_b(r)|∼r^{-α}，衰减指数α接近卡西米尔值（Casimir value）1，并存在弱但系统的J₂依赖，在J₂/J₁∈[0.1,1.0]范围内满足α_∞ ≃ 1.070 + 0.091(J₂/J₁)。自旋关联透射比T_∞(J₂)从0.11单调增长至0.33。Affleck-Ludwig边界熵log g_∞ ≈ −0.073，远高于伊辛固定边界条件（fixed-BC）值−ln√2，接近自由边界值。

Conclusion: 三个观测量（衰减指数α、透射比T_∞、边界熵log g_∞）随J₂光滑单调变化，构成一个由次近邻耦合J₂控制的单参数部分透射共形缺陷族（conformal defect family）。该结果将空位相互作用的研究从能隙相推广至临界区域，揭示了临界线上代数衰减的普适行为。

Abstract: We revisit the problem of two static nonmagnetic vacancies in the transverse-field Ising chain with first- and second-neighbor couplings $J_1$ and $J_2$, now on the critical line, using density-matrix renormalization-group (DMRG) calculations in open chains of up to $N=300$ sites. In contrast to the gapped regime studied previously, where the vacancy-vacancy interaction decays exponentially, along the entire quantum critical line the interaction becomes algebraic, $|Δ_b(r)|\sim r^{-α}$, with $α$ close to the universal Casimir value of unity and a weak but systematic dependence on the second-neighbor coupling, $α_\infty \simeq 1.070 + 0.091\, J_2/J_1)$ across $J_2/J_1\in[0.1,1.0]$. The transmission ratio of the spin correlator across a vacancy approaches a $J_2$-dependent plateau $T_\infty(J_2)$ that grows from $0.11$ to $0.33$ over the same range, and the Affleck-Ludwig boundary entropy is small and approximately constant, $\log g_\infty \approx -0.073$, well above the Ising fixed-BC value $-\ln\sqrt{2}$ and close to the free-boundary value. The three observables vary smoothly and monotonically with $J_2$, consistent with a one-parameter family of partially transmissive conformal defects controlled by $J_2$. Throughout, the critical line is located using the bulk spin-correlator exponent $η=1/4$, the order-parameter exponent of the Ising universality class, which provides a robust criterion in this open geometry.

</details>

### [12] [Magnetotransport of tomographic electrons in a Corbino disk](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05540)
*Nitay Ben-Shachar,Johannes Hofmann*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文研究发现，在Corbino圆盘中的断层扫描输运（tomographic transport）会诱导近电极的超弹道边界层，产生增强的滑移速度，从而参数化提升二次磁阻系数。该系数随磁场变化呈现三种不同输运机制，其中断层扫描区的磁阻对温度和密度的反常依赖可能解释近期实验中观察到的电子粘滞性（electron viscosity）反常标度行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了揭示在低温至中等温度下清洁电子气中因泡利阻塞（Pauli blocking）导致的费米面奇宇称模（odd-parity modes）异常长寿命所引发的“断层扫描输运”现象在受限几何结构中的具体表现，以及其对磁阻（magnetoresistance）系数的影响。

Method: 理论分析Corbino圆盘几何中的断层扫描流动，研究电极附近超弹道输运（superballistic transport）和增强滑移速度（slip velocity）的形成机制，分析磁阻系数随磁场变化的三种不同输运区域。

Result: 断层扫描流动在Corbino圆盘中产生扩展边界层，该边界层具有超弹道输运和增强的滑移速度，导致二次磁阻系数产生参数化增强，且该增强程度显式依赖于电极曲率（electrode curvature）。磁阻系数随磁场强度呈现三个截然不同的区域：弱场下的断层扫描区、中等场下的流体动力学区（hydrodynamic regime）以及强场下的常规欧姆区（Ohmic regime）。断层扫描区的磁阻对温度和密度呈现反常依赖。

Conclusion: 断层扫描区磁阻的反常温度和密度依赖关系可能解释近期实验中观测到的电子粘滞性反常标度行为，且通过器件几何结构可控制磁阻增强的强度。

Abstract: In clean electron gases at low-to-moderate temperatures, odd-parity modes of the Fermi surface are anomalously long-lived due to Pauli blocking, giving rise to ``tomographic transport'' that is not captured by a hydrodynamic model. Here we show that tomographic flow in a Corbino disk induces an extended boundary layer near electrodes with superballistic transport and enhanced slip velocity, which leads to a parametric enhancement of the quadratic magnetoresistance coefficient. The enhancement depends explicitly on the electrode curvature, allowing its strength to be controlled by the device geometry. The magnetoresistance coefficient reveals three distinct regimes as a function of magnetic field: a tomographic regime at weak fields; a hydrodynamic regime at intermediate fields, reached when the cyclotron radius becomes comparable to a large odd-mode mean free path; and a conventional Ohmic regime at large fields, reached when the cyclotron radius becomes comparable to the short even-mode mean free path. The tomographic regime is characterized by an anomalous dependence of the magnetoresistance on temperature and density, which may account for recent experimentally observed anomalous scaling of the electron viscosity.

</details>


### [13] [Effect of pressure on the magnetic properties of (Co$_{0.5}$Fe$_{0.5}$)$_5$GeTe$_2$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05548)
*Tamás Prok,Zoltán Kovács-Krausz,Harvey Stanfield,Bing Zhao,Michael Leonárd Morgan,Bálint Fülöp,Marcos H. D. Guimarães,Ivan J. Vera-Marun,Saroj Prasad Dash,Szabolcs Csonka,Péter Makk,Endre Tóvári*

TL;DR: 本文通过磁阻测量研究反铁磁（antiferromagnetic）(Co₀.₅Fe₀.₅)₅GeTe₂在不同压力下的各向异性与层间交换场，发现2 GPa压力下交换耦合增强50%，并指出观测到的尖锐磁滞跃迁源于层数的奇偶效应（even-odd effect），而非铁磁相共存。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 钴掺杂Fe₅GeTe₂具有随Co浓度变化的丰富磁相图，其中(Co₀.₅Fe₀.₅)₅GeTe₂的磁序性质尤为引人关注，因为它可能同时表现出铁磁序（ferromagnetic order）、A型反铁磁序（A-type antiferromagnetic order）或两者共存。需要澄清其磁序本质。

Method: 在系列压力下对反铁磁(Co₀.₅Fe₀.₅)₅GeTe₂进行磁阻（magnetoresistance）测量，并利用双子格模型（two-sublattice model）提取各向异性场和层间交换场。

Result: 2 GPa压力下，层间交换（interlayer exchange）增大50%，表明磁性质对层间距（interlayer distance）高度敏感；另发现反铁磁态内的尖锐磁滞跃迁（hysteretic transitions）可通过线性链模型（linear chain model）定性描述。

Conclusion: 上述尖锐磁滞跃迁更可能源于层数的奇偶效应，而非铁磁相共存，从而对(Co₀.₅Fe₀.₅)₅GeTe₂的磁序本质给出了新的解释。

Abstract: Cobalt-doped Fe$_5$GeTe$_2$ possesses a rich magnetic phase diagram as a function of Co concentration. The nature of magnetic order in (Co$_{0.5}$Fe$_{0.5}$)$_5$GeTe$_2$ is especially interesting, as it has been shown to exhibit ferromagnetic order, A-type antiferromagnetic (AFM) order, or potentially both at the same time. Here we present magnetoresistance measurements on antiferromagnetic (Co$_{0.5}$Fe$_{0.5}$)$_5$GeTe$_2$ at a series of pressures and extract the anisotropy and interlayer exchange fields using the two-sublattice model. We show a 50 % increase of the interlayer exchange at 2 GPa, highlighting the sensitivity of magnetic properties to interlayer distance. In addition, we find that the sharp hysteretic transitions observed within the AFM state can be qualitatively described by a linear chain model, which suggests an even-odd effect as a function of layer number instead of a coexisting ferromagnetic phase.

### [14] [Equivalence between the Axion Invariant and the $S_4$ Symmetry Indicator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05719)
*Mengyao Zhang*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文建立了三维S₄对称轴子绝缘体中轴子不变量（axion invariant）与S₄对称性指标（symmetry indicator）z₂之间的等价关系，通过S₄缝纫矩阵（sewing matrix）重新表述磁电极化率2P₃=θ/π，并将其化简为从布里渊区到SU(2)的映射度模2，最终证明该模2度与S₄本征值导出的对称性指标z₂一致。这一结果弥合了轴子响应的拓扑场论描述与对称性指标拓扑能带理论之间的差距，并将已知的反幺正对称性（如CₙT）下的响应-指标等价性推广到幺正的、定向反转的旋转反演对称性S₄。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究已在反幺正对称性（antiunitary symmetry，如CₙT）框架下建立了拓扑响应与对称性指标之间的等价关系，但在幺正（unitary）、定向反转（orientation-reversing）的旋转反演对称性（rotoinversion symmetry）S₄下，轴子不变量与对称性指标之间的联系尚不明确。本文旨在填补这一理论空白，统一轴子响应的拓扑场论描述与对称性指标分类。

Method: 从磁电极化率（magnetoelectric polarizability）的Chern-Simons表达式出发，将2P₃=θ/π重新表述为S₄缝纫矩阵（S₄ sewing matrix）的形式。通过稳定约化（stable reduction）将系统简化为行列式为1的两能带块，进而将不变量表达为从布里渊区（Brillouin zone）到SU(2)的映射度（degree of a map）。随后在四个S₄不变动量（S₄-invariant momenta）处利用S₄本征值计算该映射度模2，证明其与对称性指标z₂一致。最后构建最小紧束缚模型（minimal tight-binding model）进行数值验证。

Result: 证明了在三维Chern数为零的S₄对称轴子绝缘体中，轴子不变量2P₃与对称性指标z₂完全等价。紧束缚模型验证了这一对应关系。该结果将响应-指标等价性从反幺正对称性（如CₙT）成功推广至幺正的定向反转旋转反演对称性S₄。

Conclusion: 本文建立的等价关系弥合了轴子响应的拓扑场论（topological field theory）描述与对称性指标（symmetry indicators）拓扑能带理论（topological band theory）分类之间的理论鸿沟。该工作为统一理解不同对称性框架下的拓扑响应提供了重要理论基础，并拓展了对称性指标在预测拓扑材料响应性质中的应用范围。

Abstract: The equivalence between the axion invariant and the $S_4$ symmetry indicator is established for three-dimensional $S_4$-symmetric axion insulators with vanishing three-dimensional Chern numbers. Starting from the Chern-Simons expression for the magnetoelectric polarizability, $2P_3=θ/π$ is rewritten in terms of the $S_4$ sewing matrix. After stable reduction to determinant-one two-band blocks, the invariant is expressed as the degree of a map from the Brillouin zone to $SU(2)$. The degree modulo two is then evaluated from the $S_4$ eigenvalues at the four $S_4$-invariant momenta and is shown to coincide with the symmetry indicator $z_2$. A minimal tight-binding model verifies the correspondence between $2P_3$ and $z_2$. The result closes a gap between the topological-field-theory description of the axion response and the topological-band-theory classification by symmetry indicators. It also extends the known response-indicator equivalence from antiunitary settings such as $C_nT$ symmetry to the unitary, orientation-reversing rotoinversion symmetry $S_4$.

</details>


### [15] [Engineering nonlinear magnon scattering in artificial spin ice via vertex dipolar control](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05797)
*Waleed I. Waseer,Peng Yan*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过微磁学模拟，识别出尖端曲率（edge curvature）是人工自旋冰（ASI）中一种独立于岛足迹（footprint）的几何设计参数，能够在不改变晶格密度和岛体积的前提下调控非线性磁子散射（magnon scattering），实现从整数谐波到次谐波（subharmonic）谱的转变，并揭示了曲率局域化非线性的角度依赖特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统人工自旋冰的几何控制参数（如岛长度、宽度和纵横比）会同时改变岛足迹、偶极间距和形状各向异性，导致非线性响应（nonlinear response）无法与线性谱和晶格密度独立调控。因此需要寻找一种能解耦这些约束的设计自由度。

Method: 采用微磁学模拟（micromagnetic simulation）方法，对强微波驱动下的kagome型人工自旋冰体系进行研究，系统扫描不同尖端曲率与驱动参数空间，分析谐波产生与次谐波阈值行为。

Result: 尖锐尖端岛主要产生整数谐波（integer harmonics），而哑铃形尖端通过将退磁场和交换场（exchange field）集中在岛末端，在不改变岛体积或晶格间距的前提下，促成向次谐波富集谱的转变。识别出由尖端曲率控制的次谐波产生连续阈值。第二谐波振幅的角度依赖性在尖锐与哑铃几何结构之间发生反转，可作为曲率局域化非线性（curvature localized nonlinearity）的实验可检测特征。

Conclusion: 尖端曲率是一种保足迹（footprint preserving）的设计参数，可用于工程化调控人工自旋冰中的非线性磁子散射，对可重构磁子器件（reconfigurable magnonic devices）具有重要应用意义。

Abstract: Artificial spin ice (ASI), composed of geometrically frustrated arrays of interacting nanoislands, provides a versatile platform for reprogrammable magnonic functionality. However, the commonly used geometric control parameters such as island length, width, and aspect ratio simultaneously modify the island footprint, inter island dipolar spacing, and shape anisotropy, making it difficult to tune the nonlinear response independently of the linear spectrum and lattice density. Using micromagnetic simulations of kagome ASI under strong microwave drive, we identify edge curvature as a geometric degree of freedom that separates nonlinear magnon scattering from the island footprint. Sharp tipped islands predominantly generate integer harmonics, whereas dumbbell shaped tips produce a transition toward subharmonic rich spectra by concentrating demagnetizing and exchange fields near the island ends without changing the overall island volume or lattice spacing. By mapping the curvature and drive parameter space, we identify a continuous threshold for subharmonic onset controlled by tip curvature. We further show that the angular dependence of the second harmonic amplitude reverses between sharp and dumbbell geometries, providing an experimentally accessible signature of curvature localized nonlinearity. Width and leg length asymmetry can also modify harmonic amplitudes, but they do not remove the intrinsic trade off between footprint and coupling. These results establish tip curvature as a footprint preserving design parameter for engineering nonlinear magnon scattering in ASI, with implications for reconfigurable magnonic devices.

### [16] [Floquet polaritons in optically driven materials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05857)
*Tsan Huang,Teng Xiao,Jiahua Duan,Haoliang Qian,Zhiyuan Sun*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个基于有效线性光学磁化率（effective linear optical susceptibility）来描述弗洛凯极化激元（Floquet polaritons）的实用框架，并通过石墨烯、六方氮化硼和层状超导体三个实例验证了该方法，展示了泵浦光通过非线性光学效应诱导出的弗洛凯极化激元能带及其非厄米特性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代泵浦-探测实验中，泵浦光脉冲会显著改变材料中极化激元（polaritons）的性质，使其转变为弗洛凯极化激元（Floquet polaritons），但缺乏一个实用的理论框架来描述这种由光驱动的准粒子态。

Method: 提出一个实用框架，以材料的线性和非线性光学性质为基础来描述弗洛凯极化激元；核心量是有效线性光学磁化率，该磁化率通过非线性光学磁化率（nonlinear optical susceptibilities）而包含泵浦光的贡献。

Result: 在石墨烯中，红外泵浦通过三阶光学非线性（third-order optical nonlinearity）诱导出弗洛凯等离激元能带（Floquet plasmon bands）；在等离激元能带交叉附近，参量不稳定性（parametric instability）导致平带（flat bands）、不稳定模和奇异点（exceptional points），与非厄米系统（non-Hermitian systems）高度相似。在六方氮化硼中，中红外激光泵浦通过声子非线性（phononic nonlinearity）诱导出弗洛凯声子极化激元能带。在层状超导体中，太赫兹泵浦通过约瑟夫森型光学非线性（Josephson-type optical nonlinearity）诱导出弗洛凯约瑟夫森等离激元（Floquet Josephson plasmons），表现为探测脉冲太赫兹反射率中的新峰。

Conclusion: 该框架为描述弗洛凯极化激元提供了一种普遍可行的方法，揭示了泵浦光通过材料的各类光学非线性可诱导出丰富的弗洛凯极化激元能带结构，并呈现出非厄米系统中的奇异性。

Abstract: Polaritons are coupled collective modes of light and matter in quantum materials. In modern pump-probe experiments, a pump light pulse may dramatically alter the properties of the polaritons, rendering them Floquet polaritons that can be detected by a probe pulse. We present a practical framework to describe Floquet polaritons in terms of the linear and nonlinear optical properties of the material. The central quantity that yields the spectra of Floquet polaritons is an effective linear optical susceptibility contributed by the pump through nonlinear optical susceptibilities. We apply this method to graphene and show that via its third-order optical nonlinearity, infrared pump leads to Floquet plasmon bands. Notably, near plasmonic band crossings, parametric instability leads to flat bands with unstable modes and exceptional points that closely resemble those of non-Hermitian systems. As a second example, we show that in hexagonal boron nitride pumped by mid-infrared laser, the pump induces Floquet phonon polariton bands via phononic nonlinearity, which can be detected with either far-field or near-field optical technique. Finally, in layered superconductors pumped by THz light polarized along the out-of-plane direction, the Josephson-type optical nonlinearity leads to Floquet Josephson plasmons, which manifest as new peaks in the THz reflectivity of a probe pulse.

</details>


### [17] [Machine learning prediction of the convergence criterion for a topological invariant of finite non-Hermitian chains](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05900)
*Raghav Chaturvedi,Viktor Könye,Ewelina M. Hankiewicz*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文研究了非厄米有限链中基于极分解的拓扑不变量所需的裁剪长度（crop-length）的确定方法，指出该长度由物理衰变（局域化）长度控制，并利用随机森林回归（random-forest regression）实现了跨模型、跨相图的准确预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在有限非厄米链（non-Hermitian chains）中，基于极分解（polar-decomposition）的拓扑不变量需要选择一个合适的裁剪长度参数，该参数通常凭经验选取，尤其在拓扑相变（topological phase transitions）附近有限尺寸效应最强时影响显著。本文旨在建立裁剪长度的物理基础，使其选择不再依赖经验。

Method: 首先通过近邻和纯长程跳跃的Hatano-Nelson型链（Hatano-Nelson-type chains）分析裁剪长度与局域化长度（localization length）的标量倍数关系；对于更一般的模型，利用特征多项式（characteristic polynomial）的多通道根结构（multichannel root structure）进行分析。采用随机森林回归（random-forest regression）捕捉有限尺寸和近边界修正，同时保留衰变长度解释。

Result: 对于近邻和纯长程跳跃模型，裁剪长度主要由单个局域化长度的标量倍数近似；对于更一般的模型，则受特征多项式多通道根结构控制。随机森林回归在保留衰变长度解释的同时，能准确捕捉有限尺寸和边界修正。训练后的预测器能够泛化到未见过的哈密顿量（Hamiltonians）和复基能量（complex base energies），准确再现全相图中的裁剪长度。

Conclusion: 这些结果提供了一种实用且具有物理可解释性的裁剪长度选择方法，从而决定了实空间不变量（real-space invariant）何时能可靠地捕获有限非厄米链的拓扑性质。此外，从纯净近邻跳跃链学到的预测在中等程度跳跃无序（hopping disorder）下保持稳定。

Abstract: A topological invariant based on polar-decomposition of matrices correctly captures the topology of finite non-Hermitian chains exhibiting the non-Hermitian skin effect, provided that an appropriate crop-length parameter is chosen. This parameter, which sets the cutoff used in the calculation of the invariant, is usually chosen empirically and becomes especially important near topological phase transitions, where finite-size effects are strongest. Here we show that the required crop-length is controlled by physical decay (localization) lengths. For nearest-neighbor and pure longer-range hopping Hatano-Nelson-type chains, the crop-length is set mainly by a single localization length and is well approximated by a scalar multiple of that length. For more general longer-range hopping models, it is governed instead by a multichannel root structure of the characteristic polynomial. Random-forest regression captures finite-size and near-boundary corrections while preserving this decay-length interpretation. Trained on one set of Hamiltonians, the predictor accurately generalizes to unseen Hamiltonians and complex base energies, reproducing crop-lengths across full phase diagrams. We further show that the predictions learned from clean nearest-neighbor hopping chains remain stable under moderate hopping disorder. These results provide a practical and physically interpretable way to choose the crop-length, which in turn determines when the real-space invariant can reliably capture the topology of finite non-Hermitian chains.

### [18] [Interfacial Noncollinear Filtering of Spin Hall Currents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05912)
*Dan-Yang Han,Zi-An Wang,Hong-Liang Chen,Bo Li,Wen-Jian Lu,Yu-Ping Sun,Liang Liu,Shu-Hui Zhang,Ding-Fu Shao*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文指出实际器件中自旋电流的极化并非仅由体块对称性决定，而是体块与界面响应的协同结果；建立了发射自旋电流（emitted spin current）作为体块-界面混合响应的理论，提出界面非共线滤波（interfacial noncollinear filtering）机制，使传统高对称性自旋霍尔（spin Hall）材料也能产生非常规自旋极化电流。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 挑战传统观点——自旋霍尔电流（spin Hall current）的极化完全由晶体对称性固定，以解释为何低对称性自旋源（spin source）并非实际器件中产生非常规自旋极化的唯一途径，并回应界面效应在自旋输运中的关键作用。

Method: 建立了发射自旋电流作为体块-界面混合响应的理论框架，提出界面非共线滤波机制：低对称性界面自旋-轨道场（interfacial spin-orbit field）与动量分辨的自旋极化非共线，施加自旋依赖的透射，从而将隐藏的动量分辨自旋极化分量转化为可观测的非常规发射自旋电流。通过旋转对称的最小模型和真实高对称性狄拉克半金属（Dirac-semimetal）模型进行验证。

Result: 传统自旋霍尔源在界面自旋-轨道场选择性透射其隐藏体块自旋霍尔织构（bulk spin Hall texture）时，能够发射显著的面外自旋电流（out-of-plane spin current）。自旋电流极化是体块与界面响应协同作用的结果。

Conclusion: 提供了一种在不依赖固有低对称性体块晶体或外部对称性破缺方案（external symmetry-breaking scheme）的情况下，对CMOS兼容的高效自旋霍尔材料中自旋电流极化进行重编程的策略。

Abstract: Spin Hall currents generated in nonmagnetic materials are conventionally regarded as bulk responses whose polarization is fixed by crystal symmetry. This view has motivated the search for intrinsically low-symmetry spin sources when unconventional spin polarizations are required. Here we point out that, in realistic heterostructures, the device-relevant quantity is not the fully symmetry-averaged bulk spin Hall current, but the emitted spin current transmitted across the interface. We therefore establish emitted spin currents as bulk-interface hybrid responses and propose interfacial noncollinear filtering as a mechanism to bypass the bulk-symmetry constraint. A low-symmetry interfacial spin-orbit field, generally noncollinear with the momentum-resolved spin polarization of the incident spin Hall current, imposes spin-dependent transmission and converts hidden momentum-resolved spin-polarization components into an observable unconventional emitted spin current. Using both a rotationally symmetric minimal model and a realistic high-symmetry Dirac-semimetal model, we show that conventional spin Hall sources can emit sizable out-of-plane spin currents when their hidden bulk spin Hall textures are selectively transmitted by the interfacial spin-orbit field. Our results reveal that spin-current polarization emerges from the cooperative action of bulk and interfacial responses, providing a strategy for reprogramming spin-current polarization in high-efficiency, CMOS-compatible spin Hall materials without relying on intrinsically low-symmetry bulk crystals or external symmetry-breaking schemes.

### [19] [Layer-selective chirality switch in bilayer graphene intercalated by Janus monolayers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06159)

Method: 采用第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）分析电子结构；构建紧束缚模型（tight-binding model）描述近距诱导的Rashba自旋-轨道耦合；结合Rashba-Edelstein电荷-自旋转换（Rashba-Edelstein charge-to-spin conversion）计算验证自旋电流方向的可控性。

Abstract: We predict that intercalating bilayer graphene with nonmagnetic WSSe or magnetic MnSSe Janus monolayers induces a layer-selective switch of the in-plane Rashba spin texture, resulting in opposite spin current directions in the top and bottom graphene layers. First-principles calculations reveal that both Janus monolayers decouple the two graphene layers while simultaneously inducing opposite signs of the proximity-induced Rashba spin-orbit coupling in each. Tight-binding modeling of the proximitized layers, combined with Rashba-Edelstein charge-to-spin conversion calculations, confirms that the spin current direction can be independently controlled by gating the top or bottom graphene layer. ### [20] [Uncertainty relations for arbitrary currents in coherent transport](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06190)

TL;DR: 该论文推导了适用于相干、强耦合、非平衡线性系统中任意流（currents）的热力学与动力学不确定关系（thermodynamic and kinetic uncertainty relations），利用输运统计特性（特别是涨落定理，fluctuation theorems）识别出决定单个散射事件精度代价的相关熵产生（entropy production）与活性（activity），所得界限包含高阶涨落且在远离平衡态时仍然有效。通过在常规和超导混合结构中的示例，展示了其预测能力和适用范围优于现有表述。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有热力学与动力学不确定关系在相干、强耦合或远离平衡态的线性系统中存在适用性局限，需要构建更普遍的理论框架来描述任意流（currents）的精度-代价权衡（precision-cost trade-off）。

Method: 利用输运统计特性（transport statistics），尤其借助涨落定理（fluctuation theorems），识别出在单个散射事件（scattering events）层面决定精度代价的关键物理量——熵产生（entropy production）与活性（activity）。

Result: 推导出的不确定关系界限包含高阶涨落（higher-order fluctuations），且在远离平衡态（far from equilibrium）时仍然有效。在常规和超导混合结构中的数值示例表明，其预测能力和适用范围（predictiveness and validity range）均超过了现有表述。

Conclusion: 该工作为相干、强耦合线性系统中的精度-代价权衡提供了更一般性的理论描述，拓宽了不确定关系在非平衡输运（non-equilibrium transport）中的适用范围。

Abstract: We derive thermodynamic and kinetic uncertainty relations valid for arbitrary currents in coherent, strongly coupled, linear systems out of equilibrium. Exploiting properties of the transport statistics, in particular fluctuation theorems, we identify the relevant entropy production and activity that determine the cost of precision at the level of individual scattering events. The resulting bounds include higher-order fluctuations and remain valid far from equilibrium. We illustrate our results in normal and superconducting hybrid structures, and show that their predictiveness and validity range exceeds existing formulations.

### [21] [Classical Reversible Computation by Quantum Coherence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06219)
*Daniel Loss*

TL;DR: 本文提出基于自旋量子点阵列（spin quantum-dot array）的经典可逆逻辑实现方案，利用相干自旋动力学（coherent spin dynamics）和幺正旋转（unitary rotation）替代不可逆开关，以iToffoli门为通用构建模块，在4K温区实现低于朗道尔标度（Landauer scale）的极低能耗，同时该半导体硬件兼具量子计算与经典可逆逻辑的双重用途。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 数据中心与AI应用带来的能源需求激增，重新激发了人们对可逆计算（reversible computation）的兴趣——若信息可被取消计算（uncomputed），则逻辑运算不必在每一步都耗散热量。传统绝热CMOS虽然通过减缓电荷运动降低能耗，但仍然受限于晶体管的阈值物理（threshold physics）瓶颈。

Method: 提出在锗/硅（Ge/Si）空穴自旋量子点阵列中通过各向异性交换（anisotropic exchange）和直流电压脉冲（DC voltage pulses）驱动iToffoli门，实现经典可逆逻辑。同一种自旋同时承担存储、传输和计算功能，用幺正旋转（unitary rotation）替代不可逆开关，但在算法层面不使用量子叠加（superposition）。

Result: 仿真采用实验参数复现了Toffoli真值表，并得到可测试的错误景观（error landscape）。毫伏级脉冲作用于飞法级栅极（femtofarad gates），使门能耗低于4K温区的朗道尔标度（Landauer scale），较室温CMOS Toffoli门（含/不含4K冷却开销）低约五到八个数量级。

Conclusion: 该方案表明，同一套半导体硬件具有双重用途：当使用量子叠加时支持量子算法，否则支持经典可逆逻辑。自旋比特的穿梭（shuttling）无需测量即可传输比特，因此逻辑与数据移动在读出头之前始终保持可逆性。

Abstract: Rising energy demand from data-centre and AI applications has renewed interest in reversible computation, where logic need not dissipate heat at every step if information is uncomputed. Implementations have so far been classical: adiabatic CMOS reduces dissipation by slowing charge motion but is still limited by the threshold physics of transistors. Here we propose classical reversible logic implemented by coherent spin dynamics in a spin quantum-dot array, with inputs and outputs in classical basis states and no algorithmic use of superposition. The same spin stores, transports, and computes, with unitary rotation replacing irreversible switching. The universal building block is an iToffoli gate driven by DC voltage pulses and anisotropic exchange in Ge/Si hole spins. Simulations with experimental parameters reproduce the Toffoli truth table and yield a testable error landscape. Because shuttling transports the bit without measurement, logic and data movement remain reversible until readout. Millivolt pulses on femtofarad gates yield a gate energy below the 4~K Landauer scale, about five (eight) orders of magnitude below a room-temperature CMOS Toffoli with (without) 4 K cooling overhead. The same semiconductor hardware is therefore dual-use, supporting quantum algorithms when superposition is used and classical reversible logic otherwise.

</details>


### [22] [Local spin magnetization in itinerant non-collinear magnets: The local spin Berry curvature](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06253)
*Doru Sticlet,Frédéric Piéchon*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于热力学（thermodynamics）的局域自旋磁化定义方法，通过系统对外部微扰磁场的响应而非平衡自旋密度来定义磁化强度。该理论在共线磁体中与传统方法一致，但在非共线磁体中产生定性及定量差异，其中自旋相干性（spin coherence）通过类似贝里曲率（Berry curvature）的贡献导致磁化分布改变，并产生可观测后果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统方法中，巡游磁体（itinerant magnets）的局域自旋磁化强度由平衡局域自旋密度（equilibrium local spin density）决定。本文旨在提出一种替代的热力学定义，以揭示非共线磁体中传统方法未能捕捉的效应。

Method: 从热力学角度出发，将局域自旋磁化强度定义为系统对无穷小外磁场的响应。通过比较该定义与传统平衡自旋密度定义在共线磁体与非共线磁体中的预测差异，并引入类似轨道磁化（orbital magnetization）中贝里曲率（Berry curvature）的贡献来描述能级本征态（energy eigenstates）的场致形变效应。

Result: 对于共线磁体（collinear magnets），两种理论的预测一致；但对于非共线磁体（non-collinear magnets），传统方法与新热力学方法在定性及定量上均存在差异。热力学方法中，自旋相干性（spin coherences）通过场致能级形变决定了不同的局域自旋磁化分布。该效应由类似贝里曲率的贡献所捕捉，并产生若干可观测的后果。

Conclusion: 提出了一种基于热力学的局域自旋磁化定义，其与非共线磁体中的传统定义存在本质差异，揭示出自旋相干性与场致能级形变的重要作用。该理论框架为理解巡游磁体中的磁化行为提供了新的视角，并预测了若干可实验检验的效应。

Abstract: Conventionally, the local spin magnetization in itinerant magnets is determined from the equilibrium local spin density. Here, we propose a thermodynamic approach in which the local spin magnetization is defined from the response of the system to an infinitesimal external magnetic field. The predictions of the two theories are identical for collinear magnets, but differ qualitatively and quantitatively for non-collinear magnets. In the present thermodynamic approach, the spin coherences determine an alternative distribution of local spin magnetization due to the field-induced deformation of the energy eigenstates. This effect is captured by a Berry-curvature-like contribution reminiscent of orbital magnetization and has several distinct observable consequences. We explore the differences between the conventional and thermodynamic approaches in several test cases.

</details>


### [23] [Composite-Fermion Study of Cavity-Modified Fractional Quantum Hall Excitation Gaps](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06298)
*Dalin Boriçi,Nicolas Regnault,Cristiano Ciuti*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文在复合费米子（composite-fermion）框架下研究了腔调控吸引性电子-电子相互作用如何改变分数量子霍尔态（fractional quantum Hall states）的激发能隙，发现输运能隙被一致增强，而磁激子（magnetoroton）谱则对相互作用范围呈现更丰富的依赖性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究腔调控的吸引性电子-电子相互作用对分数量子霍尔态激发能隙的影响机制，特别是输运能隙和中性磁激子激发谱在不同相互作用条件下的行为。

Method: 在复合费米子框架内，考虑自旋极化的最低朗道能级（lowest-Landau-level）模型，腔模具有空间均匀的真空场梯度（vacuum-field gradient）和由长距离截断（long-distance cutoff）控制的有限相互作用范围，计算了Laughlin $ν=1/3$ 和 $ν=1/5$ 态的中性磁激子激发谱和带电激发能隙，并进行了有限尺寸标度（finite-size scaling）分析。

Result: 输运能隙被腔诱导相互作用一致增强，其增强幅度与电子数的平方和真空场梯度的四次方成标度关系；高波矢磁激子能隙在所有相互作用范围内均被增强，其行为与带电激发能隙紧密相关。

Conclusion: 腔调控相互作用能有效调节分数量子霍尔态的激发特性，但磁激子谱对相互作用范围表现出更复杂的依赖性，这表明中性激发与带电激发对腔相互作用具有不同的响应机制。

Abstract: We investigate how cavity-mediated attractive electron-electron interactions modify the excitation gaps of fractional quantum Hall states within the composite-fermion framework. We compute both the neutral magnetoroton excitation spectrum and the charged excitation gap relevant to transport experiments for the Laughlin $ν=1/3$ and $ν=1/5$ states. We consider a spin-polarized lowest-Landau-level model in which the interaction is mediated by a cavity mode with a spatially uniform vacuum-field gradient and a finite interaction range controlled by a long-distance cutoff. Finite-size scaling reveals that the transport gap is consistently enhanced by the cavity-induced interaction, with the gap enhancement scaling quadratically with the electron number and with the fourth power of the vacuum-field gradient. By contrast, the magnetoroton spectrum exhibits a richer dependence on the interaction range. The high-$k$ magnetoroton gap is enhanced for all interaction ranges considered, consistent with its close connection to the charged excitation gap, even with the long-range character of the interaction.

### [24] [From Valley Filtering to Superconducting Diode Effect in Spin-Orbit Coupled Graphene Junctions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06303)

Result: 发现自旋-轨道耦合石墨烯单结中的谷过滤和非对称边缘输运特性；在短结约瑟夫森结中，边缘输运的局域化性质导致高磁通下存在残余超电流，并观测到强非互易输运引发的约瑟夫森二极管效应。

Abstract: We study the transport properties of proximitized graphene, which can acquire a spin-orbit coupling by the proximity effect with a substrate. We focus on the ballistic and zero temperature limits, making use of a tight-binding procedure based on the KWANT Python package. We first find key results on valley-filtering properties and asymmetric edge transport in spin-orbit coupled graphene single junctions, and then move to the analysis of the superconducting transport in a graphene Josephson junction, in the short junction limit. We study the relative contribution of edge modes for different edge terminations and some degree of edge disorder, and also analyze the magnetic interference pattern that arises when threading the junction with a perpendicular magnetic field. We find residual supercurrent at high magnetic fluxes, due to the localized nature of transport in the junction, and a strong non-reciprocal transport that leads to a significant Josephson diode effect.

Method: 采用全局积累栅极加单层耗尽细栅极的器件架构替代传统的多层重叠栅极结构；通过精心设计栅极与二维空穴气（2DHG）之间的电容，实现基于射频（RF）的单次自旋读出（single-shot spin readout）和两个单自旋量子比特的相干控制（coherent control）。

Abstract: Hole spin qubits in undoped Ge/SiGe quantum well structures have advanced rapidly in performance and scalability. Here we present fabrication and measurements of Ge/SiGe spin qubit devices with a global accumulation gate and single-layer depletion fine gates, which substantially reduce fabrication complexity.   <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 实验结果展示了界面电荷相关效应的影响，并为利用界面工程（interfacial engineering）调控石墨烯基莫尔系统（moiré system）中的关联态提供了新途径。

Abstract: Interaction between different two dimensional materials can give rise to many exotic physical phenomena which are rarely observed in intrinsic materials. Recently, several theoretical and experimental works have revealed that magnetic proximity effect between pristine graphene and magnetic substrates can lead to the emergence of quantum anomalous Hall states and quantum spin Hall states. However, interplay between correlated states in graphene-based systems and magnetic materials has seldom been studied. Here we perform the transport measurement at ultrahigh magnetic field of twisted double bilayer graphene (TDBG) on CrOCl (COC) substrate, which is an antiferromagnetic material. Instead of a magnetic-exchange effect on graphene, we observe an enhanced correlated insulating state at half-filling factor of TDBG as a result of the charge-transfer process between TDBG and COC. The temperature and magnetic field dependence of this enhanced state are further studied. Our results demonstrate the influence of charge-related effect at the interface, and shed a light on a new route for manipulating the correlated states in graphene-based moiré systems using interfacial engineering.

### [27] [Half state at $ν_{tot}$ = -1/2 and its transition in Decoupled Twisted Double Bilayer Graphene](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06547)
*Ning Ma,Kenji Watanabe,Takashi Taniguchi,Mitali Banerjee*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过解耦双层扭转型双层石墨烯（decoupled twisted double bilayer graphene, TDBG）中的磁输运测量，首次实验观察到半填充态（ν = 1/2）在零位移场下表现为双组分（two-component）Halperin-Laughlin (Ψ331) 态，并通过调节位移场实现了向单组分（one-component）非阿贝尔态（Pfaffian态）的连续转变，揭示了双层量子霍尔系统中半填充基态的起源与可调性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 双层量子霍尔系统中 ν = 1/2 分数量子霍尔态（fractional quantum Hall state）的起源（双组分Halperin态 vs 单组分Pfaffian态）已争论数十年，亟需实验手段来区分并调控这两种可能的基态。

Method: 采用解耦双层扭转型双层石墨烯（TDBG）作为双层量子霍尔平台，进行磁输运（magnetotransport）测量，通过调控位移场（displacement field, D field）观测不同填充因子下的分数量子霍尔态及其转变行为。

Result: 在 ν_tot = -1/2 处，零位移场下观测到半填充态，与双组分Halperin-Laughlin (Ψ331) 态的理论预言一致；通过增大位移场，该半填充态从双组分态连续转变为单组分非阿贝尔态。

Conclusion: 实验证实TDBG中半填充态的性质可通过位移场灵活调控，为理解双层量子霍尔系统中半填充因子的基态（ground states）起源提供了关键实验证据和可调谐平台。

Abstract: The origin of the fractional state at $ν$ = 1/2 observed in double-layer quantum Hall systems has been under debate for decades. Because of the variation of bilayer charge distribution and interlayer tunneling strength, the half-filling state can be attributed to a two-component(2C) or a one-component(1C) origin, which corresponds to Halperin state and Pffafian state, respectively. Here we report the magnetotransport measurement in decoupled twisted double bilayer graphene(TDBG), which has been proved to be a promising platform for double quantum Hall system. Fractional quantum hall states in both odd and even denominator fillings are observed. We also found that the half-filling state occurs at zero displacement field at $ν_{tot}$ = -1/2, which is theoretically consistent with two-component Halperin-Laughlin (Ψ331) state. Moreover, we report the transition from two-component state at zero D field to one-component non-Abelian state by tunning displacement field. Our observation of the half filling state and its transition from 2C to 1C state provides the tunability of decoupled twisted double bilayer graphene and shed light on the understanding of the ground states at half-filling factor in the double quantum Hall system.

### [28] [2D Transport in an in-plane magnetic field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06561)
*Aryaman Babbar,Sankar Das Sarma*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出利用平行面内磁场（in-plane magnetic field）通过自旋极化（spin polarization）改变屏蔽效应（screening），从而区分二维金属-绝缘体转变（2D metal-insulator transition）两种竞争机制——Wigner结晶（Wigner crystallization）与Anderson局域化（Anderson localization），并基于两项最新实验给出了定量理论预言。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实验中观测到的密度调控型二维金属-绝缘体转变存在两种可能的物理机制（Wigner结晶或Anderson局域化），传统的输运测量难以直接区分二者，需要一种能够明确辨别这两种竞争场景的理论方案。

Method: 利用平行面内磁场诱导自旋极化，降低电子态密度（density of states）进而减弱屏蔽效应；通过分析屏蔽效应对两种转变临界密度（critical density）的不同影响——Anderson局域化的临界密度因屏蔽减弱而升高，而Wigner结晶则受此影响较小——构建了区分两种机制的一般性理论框架。

Result: 基于两项近期实验（Z. Ge等人, arXiv:2510.12009; T. Han等人, arXiv:2604.00113）给出了自旋极化效应在转变密度上的定量数值结果；指出了临界密度变化方向依赖于主导散射机制：长程带电杂质（long-ranged charged impurities）散射下临界密度升高，短程缺陷（short-ranged defects）散射下临界密度可能降低。

Conclusion: 两种场景的差异源自自旋极化是主导屏蔽效应（提升临界密度）还是主导费米面（Fermi surface）效应（抑制临界密度），这一判据为实验区分二维金属-绝缘体转变的微观机制提供了明确的定量预测。

Abstract: A parallel in-plane magnetic field could, in principle, distinguish between two competing physical scenarios for the experimentally observed density-tuned 2D metal-insulator transition (where decreasing the carrier density leads to a crossover from an effective metal to an effective insulator): Wigner crystallization or Anderson localization. Since the main scattering mechanism in 2D doped semiconductors arises from screened random charged impurities and screening in turn depends on the electronic density of states, the in-plane magnetic field could distinguish between the two by decreasing screening through spin polarization and this enhances the effective critical density for Anderson localization compared with Wigner crystallization. We give the general theory and provide results for the quantitative magnitudes of the spin polarization effect on the transition density by focusing on two recent experiments [Z. Ge, et al, arXiv:2510.12009, T. Han, et al, arXiv:2604.00113], noting that the critical density may actually decrease if the dominant scattering is by short-ranged defects instead of long-ranged charged impurities. The difference between the two cases arises from whether spin polarization dominates screening (enhanced critical density) or the Fermi surface (suppressed critical density).

</details>

### [29] [High-Accuracy Semi-Analytical Method for Solving the Problem of Electromagnetic Wave Scattering by Arbitrary Ensembles of Parallel Circular Cylinders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06517)
*V. V. Ternovski,M. I. Tribelsky*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 提出了一种用于任意数量平行、无限长、均匀、非重叠正圆柱体构成的二维电磁波散射问题的数值求解方法，通过柱谐函数解析展开、Graf加法定理处理多重散射，并结合条件数监控与扩展精度运算实现可控精度的数值验证解，并以三个铝纳米柱构成的亚波长团簇为例进行了散射特性分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决由任意数量、任意半径与复介电常数的平行无限长圆柱体构成的二维电磁波散射问题，特别是针对亚波长密堆积构型下多重散射（multiple scattering）的数值求解与精度验证需求。

Method: 采用柱谐函数（cylindrical harmonics）对电磁场进行解析展开，利用Graf加法定理（Graf's addition theorem）将多重散射效应归入展开系数的线性方程组，通过条件数监控（condition number monitoring）和必要时采用扩展精度算术（extended-precision arithmetic）进行数值求解，并辅以多阶段收敛验证（multistage verification of convergence）。

Result: 实现了在广泛参数范围内（包括亚波长密堆积配置）具有可控精度的数值验证解；以三个相同铝纳米柱（nanocylinders/nanowires）构成的亚波长团簇为例，计算并分析了散射截面（scattering cross section）、吸收截面（absorption cross section）、消光截面（extinction cross section）及散射指示图（scattering indicatrix），并构建了坡印廷矢量场（Poynting vector field）流线图，展示了团簇内圆柱间的能量通量再分布及表面附近的局域场增强区域。

Conclusion: 所提方法能够为任意圆柱构型的二维电磁散射问题提供数值验证解，且精度可控，适用于包括亚波长密堆积在内的复杂场景，并为纳米光学等领域的能量分布与场增强研究提供了分析工具。

Abstract: A method is proposed for solving the two-dimensional problem of electromagnetic wave scattering by a cluster of an arbitrary number of parallel, infinitely long, homogeneous, non-overlapping right circular cylinders. The cylinders may have arbitrary radii and complex permittivities, and their axes, while remaining parallel, may occupy arbitrary positions in the transverse plane. The solution is constructed using an analytical expansion of the electromagnetic field in cylindrical harmonics. Multiple scattering is taken into account by Graf's addition theorem, which leads to a system of linear equations for the expansion coefficients. This system is solved numerically with condition number monitoring and, when necessary, extended-precision arithmetic, followed by a multistage verification of convergence. The method provides numerically verified solutions with controlled accuracy over a wide range of parameters, including densely packed subwavelength configurations. As an example, scattering of a normally incident, linearly polarized monochromatic plane wave by a subwavelength cluster of three identical aluminum nanocylinders (nanowires) is studied. The scattering, absorption, and extinction cross sections, as well as the scattering indicatrix, are computed and analyzed. Streamlines of the Poynting vector field are constructed, demonstrating redistribution of the energy flux between the cylinders of the cluster and the formation of localized regions of field enhancement near their surfaces.

</details>


### [30] [Separation of Homogeneous and Inhomogeneous Broadening using Two-Dimensional Coherent Spectroscopy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05564)
*Adam Alfrey,Cole Tait,Joshua R. Hendrickson,Steven T. Cundiff*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文证明了二维相干光谱（2DCS）能够有效减少光谱线宽中均匀展宽（homogeneous dephasing）与非均匀展宽（inhomogeneous broadening）的简并性，相比一维Voigt拟合，可分离出更可靠、相关性更低的线宽参数。以hBN封装的MoSe₂在8K下的激子共振为例，2DCS结合联合不确定度加权拟合，显著缩小了参数置信区间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 光学光谱线宽中均匀去相干（homogeneous dephasing）与非均匀展宽（inhomogeneous broadening）的贡献难以独立分离；一维Voigt拟合中高斯与洛伦兹宽度高度相关，导致两者均无法被可靠确定。

Method: 利用二维相干光谱（2DCS）提供正交的光谱切片（对角线（diagonal）与交叉对角线（cross-diagonal）），分别对均匀和非均匀展宽过程具有互补灵敏度；采用联合不确定度加权拟合（joint uncertainty-weighted fit）映射完整的χ²(σ,γ)景观（landscape），量化参数协方差（parameter covariance）。

Result: 在hBN封装的MoSe₂于8K的激子共振测量中，与线性Voigt分析相比，2DCS产生了更紧凑的置信区域（confidence regions）和显著降低的参数相关性，从而实现了激子线宽贡献的可靠分离。

Conclusion: 二维相干光谱（2DCS）能够有效降低均匀与非均匀展宽参数之间的简并性，为从光学光谱中可靠分离微观耗散（dissipation）与无序（disorder）机制提供了一种更优的分析方法。

Abstract: Separating the contributions of homogeneous dephasing from inhomogeneous broadening in spectral linewidths is essential for connecting optical spectra to microscopic dissipation and disorder mechanisms. Voigt fits to one-dimensional spectra, such as photoluminescence, yield strongly correlated Gaussian and Lorentzian widths, so that neither width can be determined independently with confidence. We quantitatively show that two-dimensional coherent spectroscopy (2DCS) reduces this degeneracy by providing orthogonal spectral slices, diagonal and cross-diagonal, with complementary sensitivity to homogeneous and inhomogeneous broadening processes. As a demonstration, we measure the exciton resonance in hBN-encapsulated MoSe$_2$ at 8 K. A joint uncertainty-weighted fit maps the full $χ^2(σ,γ)$ landscape to quantify parameter covariance. Compared with linear Voigt analysis, 2DCS yields more compact confidence regions and markedly reduced parameter correlation, enabling reliable separation of the contributions to the excitonic linewidth.

### [31] [Exact flat bands in a 3D photonic crystal](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05942)
*Kin Hung Fung,Yan-Long Chen,C. T. Chan,Qinghua Guo*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文展示了一种三维金属偶极子腔网络（属于空间群224号）中存在精确标量（scalar）扇区，它承载了精确的平带（flat band）。通过对称性设计，该矢量（vectorial）光子晶体中实现了原本在紧束缚模型中才有的标量式平带。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 光子平带工程面临根本困难：麦克斯韦方程组是矢量的，横波条件（transversality）阻碍了产生相消干涉平带所需的局域标量基。因此，寻找在真实矢量系统中实现平带的对称性设计方案是一个重要挑战。

Method: 作者构造了一个三维金属偶极子腔网络（dipolar cavity network），通过波导通道连接，构成一个完全矢量的光子晶体（空间群No. 224）。通过对称性分析，发现该矢量系统中的十二带问题包含一个自适应的径向偶极子轴，其投影精确等价于同一网络的标量四带紧束缚哈密顿量；并通过微波尺度的耦合偶极子计算验证了该标量-矢量对偶性。

Result: 该三维金属网络中存在一个精确的标量扇区，承载了精确的平带。计算证实了标量-矢量对偶性（scalar-vectorial duality），即在矢量麦克斯韦系统中可以实现原本只在标量紧束缚模型中存在的平带。

Conclusion: 该工作提供了一个基于对称性的设计规则（symmetry-based design rule），用于在倒易矢量介质（reciprocal vector media）中实现标量式的平带，为光子平带的工程化开辟了新路径。

Abstract: Photonic flat bands are hard to engineer because Maxwell's equations are vectorial: transversality obstructs the localized scalar-like bases that generate destructive-interference flat bands in tight-binding models. We show that a three-dimensional metallic network of dipolar cavities joined by waveguide channels--a fully vectorial photonic crystal belonging to space group No. 224--hosts an exact scalar sector, carrying exact flat bands. The twelve-band vector problem contains one self-adaptive radial dipole axis per site whose projection is exactly the scalar four-band Hamiltonian of the same network. A microwave-scale coupled-dipole calculation confirms this scalar-vectorial duality. The result is a symmetry-based design rule for scalar-like flat bands in reciprocal vector media.

</details>


### [32] [Engineering Disordered Many-particle Plasmonic Nanoclusters for Wafer-scale Uniform and Giant Electromagnetic Field Enhancement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06003)
*Minjun Kim,Vasanthan Devaraj,Hyeon-Seok Seo,Seongjae Eom,Jeong-Su Lee,Donghan Lee,Min Yong Jeon,Thomas Zentgraf,Jong-Min Lee*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文提出一种受统计力学启发的多体等离子体架构，通过向连续极限（N>>1）移动来统计平均局部几何变化，从而解耦光学性能与微观无序。采用无光刻/刻蚀的多步脱润湿策略制造晶圆级纳米簇，在较大间隙下实现超越优化少体系统的高集体增强，SERS增强因子接近4×10⁸，重现性RSD约10%。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出一种受统计力学（statistical mechanics）启发的多体等离子体架构（many-body plasmonic architecture），通过向连续极限（continuum limit, N>>1）移动使局部几何变化被统计平均。实现方式为无光刻和刻蚀的多步脱润湿（multi-step dewetting）策略，在大颗粒之间引入大量小卫星纳米颗粒，构建鲁棒的多体系统。

Result: 该设计在单个间隙较大的情况下，实现了超越优化少体系统的高集体增强。优化条件下，表面增强拉曼散射（SERS）增强因子接近4×10⁸，重现性RSD约10%。

Conclusion: 该可扩展、低成本的概念为传感、光谱学和量子技术等领域建立了一条通向可重现的晶圆级纳米光子学平台的实用路径。

Abstract: Scalable plasmonic technologies face a critical trade-off: few-body architectures offer high enhancement but are sensitive to fabrication flaws, while scalable methods like solid-state dewetting yield large, low-enhancement gaps. We introduce a paradigm shift using a many-body plasmonic architecture inspired by statistical mechanics. By moving toward the continuum limit (N>>1), local geometric variations are statistically averaged out, effectively decoupling optical performance from microscopic disorder. We implement this concept via a lithography- and etching-free, multi-step dewetting strategy, creating wafer-scale nanoclusters. This process strategically forms a robust many-body system by introducing numerous small satellite nanoparticles between larger particles. Crucially, this design achieves a high collective enhancement that surpasses even optimized few-body systems, despite having larger individual gaps. Under optimized conditions, these substrates exhibit a surface-enhanced Raman scattering enhancement factor approaching 4 x 108 with unprecedented reproducibility (RSD of ~10%). This scalable, low-cost concept establishes a practical route toward reproducible wafer-scale nanophotonic platforms for sensing, spectroscopy, and quantum technologies.

### [33] [Terahertz-driven four-wave mixing at glass surfaces: Probing vibrational resonances and structural regimes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06417)
*Mathias Hedegaard Kristensen,Jérôme Degert,Theo Guillaume,Emmanuel Abraham,Laetitia Dalstein,Eric Freysz*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文展示太赫兹驱动四波混频（terahertz-driven four-wave mixing, FWM）可直接探测玻璃等无序材料（disordered materials）的低频振动模与结构演化。对PbO-硅酸盐玻璃系列的研究表明，该技术可分辨玻色峰（Boson-peak）集体激发与Pb-O/Si-O网络伸缩模，并在44 mol% PbO附近观测到中程尺度的孤对电子（lone-pair）重排信号，这些信息无法通过线性红外、拉曼和太赫兹时域光谱获取。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 玻璃等无序材料的结构动力学非常复杂，传统光谱技术难以直接探测其低频振动模和结构演化。因此需要一种能够提供直接、深度受限且体灵敏（bulk-sensitive）的非线性光谱方法。

Method: 采用太赫兹驱动四波混频（terahertz-driven four-wave mixing, FWM）技术，对PbO-硅酸盐玻璃（20-54 mol% PbO）进行测量，系统追踪该系列玻璃的低频振动模与结构演化。

Result: 成功分辨出集体玻色峰激发（Boson-peak excitations）与Pb-O/Si-O网络伸缩模（stretching modes）；主导振动频率随PbO含量增加而蓝移（blueshift），反映了Pb²⁺从硅酸盐修饰体（silicate-modifier）向网络形成体（network-former）的演化。在44 mol% PbO附近观测到FWM信号的显著增强，对应中程Pb-Pb关联的出现；面内/面外FWM强度比（I_SS/I_PS）追踪了χ⁽³⁾张量各向异性，后者与Pb²⁺孤对电子空间关联相关。两个可观测量均在44 mol% PbO处呈现非单调峰值，而该组成下NMR未发现Pb-O局域配位变化，且Pb-O-Pb自由氧连接可忽略，表明中程结构发生了独立的孤对电子集体重排。

Conclusion: 太赫兹驱动FWM是一种体灵敏、近表面深度受限（~50 nm）的非线性光谱技术，能够探测线性红外、拉曼和太赫兹时域光谱无法触及的振动和电子结构指纹信息，为研究无序材料中的中程结构演化提供了新工具。

Abstract: Disordered materials such as glasses exhibit complex structural dynamics that are challenging to probe with conventional spectroscopies. We demonstrate that terahertz-driven four-wave mixing (FWM) at glass surfaces provides direct access to low-frequency vibrational modes and structural evolution in amorphous solids. Applied to a compositional series of PbO-silicate glasses (20-54 mol% PbO), this technique resolves distinct contributions from collective Boson-peak excitations and Pb-O / Si-O network stretching modes, and tracks their systematic evolution across structurally distinct compositional regimes. The dominant vibrational frequency blueshifts with PbO content, reflecting the progressive evolution of the Pb$^{2+}$ network role from silicate-modifier to ward network-former. A pronounced enhancement of the FWM signal near 44 mol% PbO coincides with the emergence of medium-range Pb-Pb correlations, while in-plane-to-out-of-plane FWM intensity ratio ($I_{\rm SS}/I_{\rm PS}$) tracks $χ^{(3)}$ tensor anisotropy tied to Pb$^{2+}$ lone-pair spatial correlations. The non-monotonic peak in both observables at 44 mol% PbO - a composition where NMR finds no change in local Pb-O coordination and Pb-O-Pb free-oxide linkages are negligible - provides direct evidence that a collective lone-pair reorganization occurs in the medium-range structure independently of nearest-neighbor bonding. These results establish terahertz-driven FWM as a bulk-sensitive, near-surface depth-confined ($\sim$50 nm) nonlinear spectroscopy sensitive to vibrational and electronic structural fingerprints inaccessible to linear infrared, Raman, and terahertz time-domain probes.

### [34] [Alleviating the Hubble Tension with Smooth Sign-Switching Dark Energy: Full CMB Constraints with DESI and PantheonPlus](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05044)
*Mariam Bouhmadi-López,Hsu-Wen Chiang,Beñat Ibarra-Uriondo*

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了符号切换暗能量（sign-switching dark energy）的ECDM模型，发展了在暗能量状态方程参数发散时依然保持良定义的扰动方程形式化方法，并利用多种宇宙学观测数据检验了该模型，结果表明该类模型与当前精度宇宙学观测完全兼容，同时能够缓解哈勃张力（Hubble tension）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 发展了ECDM模型——暗能量密度从负值逐渐过渡到正值的平滑实现——的扰动方程一致形式化方法，确保在暗能量状态方程参数在过渡期间发散时依然保持良定义（well behaved）。利用Planck 2018、ACT DR6和SPT-3G的宇宙微波背景（cosmic microwave background）测量、DESI DR2的重子声学振荡（baryon acoustic oscillation）测量、Pantheon+的Ia型超新星距离以及SH0ES的局域哈勃常数测量等综合宇宙学观测数据对模型进行检验。

Conclusion: 符号切换暗能量类模型为宇宙晚期动力学提供了有说服力的修正方案，在不违背现有观测数据的前提下有效缓解了哈勃张力，是标准宇宙学模型的一个可行替代或扩展。

Abstract: Sign-switching dark energy has recently been proposed as a minimal modification of the late-time expansion history aimed at alleviating tensions within the standard cosmological model. In this work, we investigate ECDM, a smooth realisation of this scenario, with the dark energy density gradually transitioning from a negative to a positive value. We develop a consistent formulation of the perturbation equations that remains well behaved even when the dark energy equation-of-state parameter diverges during the transition. We confront the model with a comprehensive set of cosmological observations, including cosmic microwave background measurements from Planck 2018, ACT DR6 and SPT-3G, baryon acoustic oscillation measurements from DESI DR2, Type Ia supernova distances from Pantheon+, and local Hubble constant measurement of SH0ES. The inclusion of perturbations allows us to assess the impact of the model on structure growth and CMB anisotropies, providing a more thorough test of sign-switching dark energy. Our results show that this class of models is fully compatible with current precision cosmological observations while alleviating the Hubble tension and providing a compelling modification of the late-time dynamics of the Universe.

### [35] [A Novel Implementation of Self-Interacting Dark Matter in AREPO](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05504)
*Oliver Zier,Xuejian Shen,Vinh Tran,Martin Rosenlyst,Mark Vogelsberger,Rongrong Liu*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文在移动网格代码AREPO-2中提出了一种新的蒙特卡洛自相互作用暗物质（SIDM）数值实现，通过专用的暗物质邻居搜索树和成对通信方案，在保持计算效率和可扩展性的同时，支持速度依赖截面和非弹性相互作用，并通过一系列理想化和宇宙学测试验证了其性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自相互作用暗物质（SIDM）通过碰撞热输运影响暗物质晕结构，可能解决结构形成中的若干小尺度疑难，如矮星系核区密度分布等问题。现有的SIDM数值实现（如AREPO-1版本）在效率和可扩展性方面存在不足，需要发展更高效的实现方案。

Method: 基于蒙特卡洛（Monte-Carlo）方法在移动网格（moving-mesh）代码AREPO-2中实现SIDM。核心创新在于建立一个专用的暗物质邻居搜索树（DM-only neighbour-search tree），将散射求解器与引力求解器解耦，保留AREPO-2的分层时间积分（hierarchical time integration）机制。引入MPI任务间的成对通信方案（pairwise communication scheme），支持在单个时间步内追踪多次散射事件，同时保证动量、能量守恒和并行一致性。采用每对时间步判据（per-pair timestep criterion）减少不必要的限制。实现原生支持速度依赖截面（velocity-dependent cross-sections）和非弹性相互作用（inelastic interactions），并设计了紧凑接口以便扩展其他SIDM物理过程。

Result: 通过一系列理想化测试和宇宙学测试（包括孤立核坍缩模拟和含重子/不含重子的宇宙学盒子）完成了实现验证。除引力热坍缩晚期阶段外，SIDM模拟相比对应的冷暗物质（CDM）运行仅带来适度额外计算开销，且显著快于AREPO-1中之前的SIDM实现。

Conclusion: 本文提出的AREPO-2 SIDM实现兼具效率、可扩展性和可扩展性，能够支持更丰富的暗物质物理模型，为未来利用SIDM解释小尺度结构疑难提供了可靠的数值工具。

Abstract: Self-interacting dark matter (SIDM) influences halo structure through collisional heat transport and may solve several small-scale puzzles in structure formation. SIDM creates thermalized cores in low-mass haloes, which may account for the observed cored dwarf galaxies. During late-time gravothermal core collapse, SIDM can produce dense low-mass DM haloes and substructures detected through perturbations to cold stellar streams and strong gravitational lenses. In this work, we present a new Monte-Carlo SIDM implementation in the moving-mesh code AREPO-2, designed for efficiency, scalability, and extensibility. The central feature of the implementation is a dedicated DM-only neighbour-search tree that decouples the scattering solver from gravity. This preserves compatibility with the hierarchical time integration used by AREPO-2 while leaving the optimized gravity solver unconstrained. A pairwise communication scheme between MPI tasks allows tracking multiple scattering events in a single timestep while conserving momentum and energy and maintaining parallel consistency by construction. This is complemented by a per-pair timestep criterion that significantly reduces unnecessary timestep restrictions. The implementation natively supports velocity-dependent cross-sections and inelastic interactions, while a compact interface is designed for additional SIDM physics to be implemented without knowledge of the parallelization layer. We validate the implementation for isotropic, elastic scattering using a suite of idealized and cosmological tests. We assess performance and scalability in isolated core-collapse simulations and in cosmological boxes, both DM-only and with baryons. Except during the late stages of gravothermal collapse, SIDM simulations incur only modest overhead relative to the corresponding CDM runs and are substantially faster than the previous SIDM implementation in AREPO-1.

</details>
