### [36] [Searching for charged Higgs bosons in top decays via the $t^*b$ channel](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05499)
*Saiyad Ashanujjaman,Guglielmo Coloretti,Andreas Crivellin,Benjamin Fuks,Yeonsu Heo*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究通过重解释ATLAS对双轻子事件的基准测量，对来自奇异顶夸克衰变$t\to H^\pm b$并随后衰变$H^\pm\to t^*b$（含有虚顶夸克的离壳道）所产生的$t\bar t b\bar b$末态进行约束，给出了对分支比乘积${\rm Br}(t\to H^\pm b)\times{\rm Br}(H^\pm\to t^*b)$在110–165 GeV带电希格斯质量范围内的模型无关上限（1.9%–2.9%），并将其应用于多种二希格斯双态模型，证明该重解释方法是对传统寻找轻带电希格斯粒子和非标准顶夸克衰变的互补探针。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有对带电希格斯玻色子（charged Higgs boson，$H^\pm$）的搜索主要集中于较重质量（末态含在壳顶夸克）以及$H^\pm\to \tau\nu$、$cs$、$cb$等衰变模式，而质量低于顶夸克的轻带电希格斯通过离壳通道（off-shell channel）$H^\pm\to t^*b$衰变这一关键区域几乎未被约束，尽管由于大顶汤川耦合（top Yukawa coupling）该道在低于顶夸克阈值时可能成为主导衰变模式。

Method: 从奇异顶夸克衰变$t\to H^\pm b$出发，$H^\pm$进一步通过$H^\pm\to t^*b$离壳衰变，从而在顶夸克对（$t\bar t$）产生和衰变中形成$t\bar t b\bar b$类末态；作者通过对近期ATLAS合作组在双轻子事件（dileptonic events）中的基准测量（fiducial measurements）进行重解释（reinterpretation），导出对分支比乘积的约束，并在多种二希格斯双态模型（two-Higgs-doublet model, 2HDM）框架下进行解读。

Result: 在带电希格斯质量110–165 GeV范围内，获得对${\rm Br}(t\to H^\pm b)\times{\rm Br}(H^\pm\to t^*b)$的模型无关上限为1.9%–2.9%。在规范$Z_2$对称模型中传统搜索仍占主导，但在上行型对齐极限（up-type aligned limit）中，该重解释方法在靠近顶夸克阈值时具有竞争力；在顶亲和（top-philic）情形下提供了直接的相关约束；在顶特异二希格斯双态模型（top-specific 2HDM）中，进一步排除了传统搜索未覆盖的低$\tan\beta$区域。

Conclusion: 研究表明，$t\bar t$产生伴随额外$b$喷注（$b$-jets）的末态可以作为轻质量带电希格斯玻色子和非标准顶夸克衰变的一种互补探针，并激励LHC合作组开展专门分析。

Abstract: Rare top-quark decays offer a sensitive probe of charged Higgs bosons with masses below the top mass, owing to the large $t\bar t$ production rate at the LHC and the distinctive final states involving leptons and $b$-jets. While existing searches target the $H^\pm\to τν$, $cs$, and $cb$ modes, the decay $H^\pm\to tb$ has been studied only for heavier charged Higgs bosons with an on-shell top quark in the final state. The low-mass off-shell channel $H^\pm\to t^*b$ therefore remains essentially unconstrained, even though it can become the dominant decay mode below the top-quark threshold owing to the large top Yukawa coupling. We study charged-Higgs production from the rare top decay $t\to H^\pm b$, followed by the decay $H^\pm\to t^*b$. Top-antitop production and decay hence give rise to a $t\bar t b\bar b$-like final state, which we constrain by reinterpreting recent ATLAS fiducial measurements in dileptonic events. We obtain model-independent limits of 1.9%-2.9% on the product of branching ratios ${\rm Br}(t\to H^\pm b)\times{\rm Br}(H^\pm\to t^*b)$ for charged-Higgs masses between 110 and 165 GeV, and interpret these bounds in several two-Higgs-doublet scenarios. While dedicated searches for conventional charged-Higgs decays dominate for canonical $Z_2$-symmetric models, the $t^*b$ reinterpretation becomes competitive near the top-quark threshold in the up-type aligned limit and provides relevant direct constraint in a top-philic scenario. In the top-specific Two-Higgs-Doublet Model, it additionally excludes a low-$\tanβ$ region not covered by conventional searches. These results thus establish $t\bar t$ production with additional $b$-jets as a complementary probe of light charged Higgs bosons and nonstandard top-quark decays, and motivate dedicated analyses by the LHC collaborations.

</details>


### [37] [Precision Study of Semileptonic and Non-Leptonic $B_c$ Decays to $η_c$ and P Wave Charmonia](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05527)
*Aritra Biswas,Soumitra Nandi,Shantanu Sahoo*

TL;DR: 基于NRQCD理论框架，利用实验数据（而非额外模型输入）约束B_c介子到P波粲偶素（P wave charmonium）的跃迁形状因子，给出半轻子分支比、轻子普适性比率以及非轻子衰变和产生过程的预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: B_c介子衰变到P波粲偶素态（如χ_c0, χ_c1, h_c）的相关形状因子此前缺乏精确的实验约束，现有理论预测依赖较多模型输入。本文旨在利用已有辐射衰变实验数据直接提取波函数导数，从而减少模型依赖性，提高预测可靠性。

Method: 跃迁形状因子的解析表达式取自非相对论量子色动力学（NRQCD），但其归一化和形状由实验数据直接约束，不引入额外模型依赖参数。具体而言，利用χ_c0、χ_c1和h_c的辐射衰变数据，提取其在原点的径向波函数导数，从而更新B_c → (χ_c0, χ_c1, h_c)的形状因子。

Result: 给出了三个半轻子分支比的具体数值预测，以及轻子普适性比率（lepton flavour universality ratios）：R(χ_c0)=0.185(3)、R(χ_c1)=0.147(26)和R(h_c)=0.068(2)。同时提供了选定的非轻子B_c衰变以及正负电子对撞和Z玻色子衰变中P波粲偶素产生过程的预测结果。

Abstract: We analyse semileptonic and non-leptonic decays of the $B_c$ meson into P wave charmonium states. The analytic expressions for the transition form factors are taken from NRQCD, while their normalisations and shapes are constrained directly using experimental data, without introducing any additional model-dependent inputs. Using radiative decay data of $χ_{c0}$, $χ_{c1}$, and $h_c$, we extract the derivatives of their radial wave functions at the origin and update the $B_c \to (χ_{c0}, χ_{c1}, h_c)$ form factors. We present predictions for the semileptonic branching fractions, the lepton flavour universality ratios $R(χ_{c0})=0.185(3)$, $R(χ_{c1})=0.147(26)$, and $R(h_c)=0.068(2)$, as well as selected non-leptonic $B_c$ decays and P-wave charmonium production in $e^+e^-$ annihilation and $Z$-boson decays.

### [38] [Separating energy scales in hadron scattering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05990)
*S. M. Troshin,N. E. Tyurin*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文讨论了软强子散射（soft hadron scattering）中的能量尺度分离可能性，识别了两个关键尺度：一个对应总截面开始增长的区域，另一个对应渐近区域（asymptotic region）；后者对幺正性效应（unitarity effects）最为敏感，前者则主要受多粒子产生导致的初始波吸收特征影响；从阴影散射（shadow scattering）向反射散射（reflective scattering）的转变建立了这两个能量尺度之间的关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究软强子散射中不同能量尺度的分离可能性，以理解总截面增长与渐近行为背后的物理机制。

Method: 通过分析两个能量尺度——总截面增长起始尺度与渐近区域尺度——各自对幺正性效应和多粒子产生吸收效应的敏感性差异，并考察从阴影散射到反射散射的转变过程。

Result: 发现渐近区域尺度对幺正性效应更敏感，而总截面增长区域尺度主要受多粒子产生的初始波吸收特征影响；阴影散射向反射散射的转变将这两个尺度联系起来。

Conclusion: 软强子散射中存在两个可分离的能量尺度，且阴影-反射散射转变提供了二者之间的定量关系。

Abstract: We discuss energy scales in soft hadron scattering and possibility of their separation: the one relevant to the region where the total cross-sections increase begins and another one related to the asymptotic region. The latter scale is most sensitive to the unitarity effects and former one -- to the gross features of absorption of the initial wave due to multiparticle production. Transition from the shadow to reflective scattering sets a relation between the two energy scales.

Main category: hep-ph

Method: 基于C++库ggxy实现，双圈虚部振幅（two-loop virtual amplitudes）采用不同运动学区域（kinematic regions）的解析近似（analytical approximations），其余部分精确计算；支持自由修改输入参数（顶夸克质量及其重整化方案、外部Z玻色子/希格斯玻色子质量），并已与Powheg接口以实现与部分子簇射（parton shower）的匹配。

Abstract: We present the C++ library ggxy, which can be used for the fast and flexible calculation of partonic and hadronic cross sections to gluon-initiated top-mediated processes such as $gg\to HH$, as well as the newly derived processes $gg\to ZH$ and $gg\to ZZ$, at NLO QCD including full top-quark mass dependence. The two-loop virtual amplitudes are implemented using analytical approximations in different kinematic regions, while all other parts of the calculation are exact. This implementation allows to freely modify all input parameters, such as the top-quark mass and its renormalization scheme and the masses of the external $Z$/Higgs bosons. In addition, ggxy has been interfaced to Powheg, which allows the matching to parton showers.

### [40] [Understanding the near-threshold structures in $e^+e^- $ annihilation from a unified $N \bar N$-interaction perspective](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06168)
*Teng Ji,Ulf-G. Meißner*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了电子-正电子对撞中接近核子-反核子（N̅N）阈值的截面结构，提出这些结构可以统一解释为N̅N末态相互作用（final-state interaction）的体现，而非各通道独立的窄共振。基于手征有效场论（chiral EFT）描述的强N̅N相互作用，并结合慢变短距离电磁产生源，该模型同时对五个非重子末态通道的近阈值截面给出了自洽描述。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在e⁺e⁻ → p̅p、e⁺e⁻ → n̅n以及其他非重子末态的反应截面中，观察到接近核子-反核子（N̅N）阈值的类共振结构。这些结构的共同起源尚不明确，本文旨在检验它们是否能够被统一的N̅N末态相互作用所解释，而无需引入各通道独立的新共振态。

Method: 采用手征有效场论（chiral EFT）描述耦合的³S₁-³D₁系统的强N̅N相互作用，参数由低能N̅N散射数据约束固定。在此相互作用下，通过拟合慢变化的短距离电磁产生源来描述p̅p和n̅n截面；进而将得到的N̅N产生振幅作为输入，应用于五个非弹性强子通道。

Result: 模型成功同时描述了e⁺e⁻ → p̅p、e⁺e⁻ → n̅n及其他非重子末态通道的近阈值截面。结果显示，观测到的截面结构可以一致地归因于同一套N̅N动力学（dynamics），无需引入各通道独立的额外窄共振（narrow resonances）。

Conclusion: 近阈值截面中出现的结构并非来自多个互不相关的共振态，而很可能是由共同的N̅N末态相互作用导致的动力学效应。这一结论强调了强相互作用中末态效应在解释对撞截面实验特征时的重要性。

Abstract: Near-threshold structures have been observed in the cross sections for $e^+e^- \to p \bar p$, $e^+e^- \to n \bar n$ and several non-baryonic final states in the vicinity of the $N \bar N$ thresholds. We investigate whether these structures can be understood as manifestations of a common $N \bar N$ final-state interaction. The strong $N \bar N$ interaction is taken from the chiral EFT description of the coupled ${}^3S_1$-${}^3D_1$ system constrained by low-energy $N \bar N$ scattering data. With this interaction fixed, the $p \bar p$ and $n \bar n$ cross sections are described by fitting only short-distance electromagnetic production sources, which are assumed to vary slowly over the near-threshold region. The resulting $N \bar N$ production amplitudes are then used as input for five inelastic hadronic channels. A simultaneous description of the near-threshold cross sections is obtained, indicating that the observed structures can be consistently interpreted as consequences of the same underlying $N \bar N$ dynamics, without introducing separate narrow resonances in individual channels.

### [41] [Predictions for $b$-baryon lifetimes at NNLO-QCD](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06538)
*Alexander Lenz,Maria Laura Piscopo,Aleksey V. Rusov*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文在重夸克展开（HQE）框架下，首次引入自由b夸克衰变的次次领头阶（NNLO）QCD修正和维度五贡献的完整次领头阶（NLO）QCD修正，给出了b重子总衰变率、寿命比以及以B⁰_d介子寿命归一化的寿命的最新预测，显著降低了理论不确定性，并与实验数据取得了极好的一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期及即将开展的实验进展需要更精确的理论预测。b重子（b-baryon）的衰变率和寿命比是检验重夸克展开（heavy quark expansion, HQE）框架的重要观测量，但此前理论计算中尚未包含完整的次次领头阶（next-to-next-to-leading-order, NNLO）QCD修正及维度五（dimension-five）贡献的完整次领头阶（next-to-leading-order, NLO）QCD修正，导致理论不确定性较大。

Method: 在HQE框架内，首次纳入自由b夸克衰变的NNLO QCD修正，以降低总衰变率的理论不确定性；同时首次包含维度五贡献的完整NLO QCD修正，以改进寿命比的预测精度。

Result: NNLO QCD修正显著降低了总衰变率的理论不确定性；维度五贡献的NLO QCD修正虽对总衰变率影响较小，但导致寿命比出现显著偏移，从而改善了HQE预测与实验数据的一致性。最终，总衰变率和寿命比的HQE预测与当前实验测量结果在引用的不确定度范围内表现出极好的一致性。

Conclusion: HQE框架在包含高阶QCD修正后，能够为b重子衰变率和寿命比提供与实验高度一致的精确理论预测，验证了HQE在该领域的有效性。

Abstract: Motivated by recent and forthcoming experimental progress, we provide updated predictions for the total decay rates of $b$-baryons, their lifetime ratios and their lifetimes normalised to that of the $B^0_d$ meson within the framework of the heavy quark expansion (HQE). We include, for the first time, next-to-next-to-leading-order QCD corrections to the free $b$-quark decay, which significantly reduce the theoretical uncertainties in the total decay rates. In addition, we also include, for the first time, the complete next-to-leading-order QCD corrections to the dimension-five contributions. While these corrections have only a minor effect on the total decay rates, they induce a sizeable shift in the lifetime ratios, improving the agreement between HQE predictions and experimental data. Overall, we find excellent agreement between the HQE predictions and current experimental measurements for both total decay rates and lifetime ratios within the quoted uncertainties.

### [42] [A Quantitative Framework of Nonperturbative QCD from Topological Vacuum with Application to Parton Structures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06060)
*Wei-Yang Liu*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本论文发展了一个基于QCD真空拓扑结构的定量框架，将红外胶子构型建模为瞬子（instanton）与反瞬子（anti-instanton）的液体系综，从而同时捕捉迹反常、轴反常（axial anomaly）及手征对称性破缺（chiral symmetry breaking），并分别以统计系综和有效场论（EFT）两种形式构建。该框架被嵌入光前（light-front）和横动量依赖（TMD）因子化，计算了部分子可观测量、软函数（soft functions）、强子形状因子及高扭度（higher-twist）关联，应用于强子质量与自旋分解、近阈值夸克偶素产生及强CP问题，展示了真空结构在强子物理中的定量重要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非微扰QCD长期以来缺乏一个既能提供物理图像又具备定量预测能力的统一框架。本文旨在基于QCD真空的拓扑结构，发展一套能够同时解释迹反常、轴反常和手征对称性破缺等核心非微扰现象的物理图像，并将其与部分子层次的可观测现象系统性地联系起来。

Method: 通过积掉紫外自由度，将红外胶子构型建模为瞬子与反瞬子组成的液体系综。框架有两种等价的表述方式：一是构建由瞬子作用和狄拉克行列式（Dirac determinant）定义权重的统计系综；二是将行列式重写为有效夸克相互作用，从而构建有效场论（EFT）。该EFT被进一步在光前（light-front）量子化下重新表述，显式构造光前波函数（light-front wave functions）并在线性因子化下计算部分子可观测量；同时将该框架嵌入横动量依赖（TMD）因子化，通过计算软函数（soft functions）建立快度演化的真空起源。

Result: 成功计算了标量、赝标量和能量-动量张量（EMT）形状因子，以及高扭度色力（higher-twist color force）和多胶子关联函数。这些结果被应用于强子质量与自旋分解、近阈值夸克偶素产生以及强CP问题。论文表明QCD真空在从低到中等分辨率的强子结构描述中提供了定量上关键的贡献，桥接了非微扰真空物理与部分子唯象学。

Conclusion: 本工作建立的基于瞬子液体系综的框架成功地将拓扑真空结构与部分子层次的可观测物理系统性地联系起来，证明了QCD真空在强子结构描述中具有定量重要性，为从低到中等分辨率下的强子物理提供了统一且可计算的理论工具。

Abstract: This dissertation develops a quantitative framework that provides a physical picture for non-perturbative QCD based on the topological structure of the QCD vacuum. By integrating out the ultraviolet degrees of freedom, the infrared gluon configurations are modeled as a liquid ensemble of instantons and anti-instantons, which induce effective interactions among quarks. This framework captures the origin of trace and axial anomalies through the infrared distributions of QCD and dynamically breaks chiral symmetry. More specifically, this framework can be formulated in two ways: in one, we construct a statistical ensemble with weights defined by the instanton action and Dirac determinant, while in the other we formulate an effective field theory (EFT) by rewriting the determinant as effective quark interactions. By reformulating the EFT on the light front, we explicitly construct the light-front wave functions and calculate various parton observables in linear factorization. We further embed the framework into transverse momentum dependent factorization and establish a vacuum origin for rapidity evolution by computing the soft functions. We also extend this approach to various form factors in light hadrons, including scalar, pseudoscalar, and energy-momentum tensor (EMT), as well as higher-twist color force and multigluon correlations, with applications to hadron mass and spin decomposition, near-threshold quarkonium production, and strong CP problem, highlighting the importance of the vacuum origin in hadron structures. Overall, this work demonstrates that the QCD vacuum provides a quantitatively crucial description of hadronic structure from low to moderate resolution, bridging nonperturbative vacuum physics with partonic phenomenology.

</details>


### [43] [Polyakov Loops Tame Phase Transitions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06203)
*Lisa Biermann,Joydeep Chakrabortty,Christoph Englert*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文估计了Polyakov圈（Polyakov loop）对电弱相变（electroweak phase transition）的影响，发现Polyakov圈会减弱热贡献，从而软化电弱相变、改变泡泡动力学（bubble dynamics）、成核（nucleation）及相关引力波谱（gravitational-wave spectrum）；该非微扰效应使一级相变（first-order PT）相比二级相变（second-order PT）或平滑过渡（smooth cross-over）更不受青睐，且该特征对费米子和玻色子贡献具有普适性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 电弱相变是早期宇宙的重要物理过程，但传统微扰理论忽略了Polyakov圈这一非微扰（non-perturbative）贡献。本文旨在定量评估Polyakov圈对电弱相变及其可观测后果（如引力波信号）的具体影响。

Method: 通过将Polyakov圈这一非微扰贡献纳入微扰框架（perturbative approaches），构建包含Polyakov圈的热有效势（thermal effective potential），并分析其如何改变相变的级次与动力学特征。

Result: Polyakov圈倾向于压制热贡献，从而软化电弱相变，并改变泡泡动力学、成核过程及相关引力波谱。包含该非微扰贡献后，一级相变比二级相变或平滑过渡更不被热有效势所支持，且该效应在费米子与玻色子贡献中均成立。

Conclusion: Polyakov圈对电弱相变具有普适性的软化作用，表明在微扰计算中必须纳入这一非微扰效应，否则可能高估一级相变的发生概率及相应的引力波信号强度。

Abstract: We estimate the impact of Polyakov loop (PL) contributions on electroweak phase transitions (PTs). We show that the PL, which is unavoidable in thermal gauge field theory, tends to tame thermal contributions, thereby softening electroweak PTs and affecting bubble dynamics, nucleation, and the related gravitational-wave spectrum. Including this non-perturbative contribution in perturbative approaches results in a thermal effective potential that disfavours first-order PTs over either second-order PTs or smooth cross-overs. This feature is universal for both fermionic and bosonic contributions to the effective potential.

</details>


### [44] [Interplay of CPT-Violating and CPT-Conserving Lorentz Invariance Violation at DUNE](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06513)
*Priyankush Deka,Arnab Sarker,Moon Moon Devi,Sushant K. Raut*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了中微子振荡中的洛伦兹不变性破缺（LIV）效应，重点关注CPT破缺与CPT守恒的标准模型扩展（SME）系数之间的相互作用。发现对角LIV系数中 $a_{ee}$ 和 $a_{ττ}$ 占主导，非对角项中 $a_{eμ}$ 和 $a_{eτ}$ 贡献最显著，而对应的 $c_{αβ}$ 系数影响较小。以DUNE为代表的长基线实验表明，LIV会以参数特定方式改变CP破坏灵敏度，某些LIV系数可将显著性从 $5\sigma$ 压低至 $3\sigma$ 以下，且 $a_{αβ}$ 与 $c_{αβ}$ 的简并效应进一步恶化了CP破坏的提取能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 中微子振荡实验是检验洛伦兹不变性破缺（Lorentz invariance violation, LIV）的重要平台，同时CP破坏的精确测量是理解宇宙物质-反物质不对称的关键。本文旨在系统研究CPT破缺与CPT守恒的SME系数（$a_{αβ}$ 与 $c_{αβ}$）在中微子振荡中的联合效应，评估它们对即将开展的长基线实验（如DUNE）中CP破坏发现潜力的影响。

Method: 本研究基于标准模型扩展（Standard Model Extension, SME）框架，在理论上分类讨论对角与非对角的LIV系数（$a_{αβ}$ 和 $c_{αβ}$）的贡献大小。以DUNE（Deep Underground Neutrino Experiment）作为代表性长基线实验，通过数值分析检验LIV参数对CP破坏敏感性的影响，包括参数间的相关性、新相位的依赖性以及 $a_{αβ}$ 与 $c_{αβ}$ 之间的简并效应（degeneracies）。

Result: 在对角LIV系数中，$a_{ee}$ 和 $a_{ττ}$ 贡献占主导；非对角LIV系数中，$a_{eμ}$ 和 $a_{eτ}$ 贡献最为显著，而相应的 $c_{αβ}$ 系数仅产生次主导效应。$a_{ee}$、$a_{ττ}$、$a_{eμ}$ 和 $a_{eτ}$ 的存在会将CP破坏显著性从原本的 $5\sigma$ 压低至 $3\sigma$ 以下（覆盖 $δ_{\rm CP}$ 的很大范围）。$c_{αβ}$ 项的独立影响同样导致抑制，但与 $a_{αβ}$ 联合时会引入参数简并，进一步恶化CP破坏敏感度，使其普遍低于 $5\sigma$。

Conclusion: 洛伦兹不变性破缺（LIV）效应会显著削弱长基线中微子实验中CP破坏的发现潜力，特别是 $a_{ee}$、$a_{ττ}$、$a_{eμ}$ 和 $a_{eτ}$ 等主要系数以及 $a_{αβ}$ 与 $c_{αβ}$ 之间的简并效应，将导致CP破坏显著性系统性下降。因此，在即将开展的长基线实验（如DUNE）的精确振荡研究中，必须将LIV效应纳入考虑，以避免对CP破坏信号产生误判。

Abstract: We present a study of Lorentz invariance violation (LIV) in neutrino oscillations, with primary emphasis on the interplay between CPT-violating and CPT-conserving Standard Model Extension (SME) coefficients. We find that $a_{ee}$ and $a_{ττ}$ dominate among the diagonal LIV coefficients, whereas $a_{eμ}$ and $a_{eτ}$ provide the most significant off-diagonal contributions. In contrast, the corresponding $c_{αβ}$ coefficients have comparatively sub-leading effects. Taking DUNE as a representative long-baseline experiment, we show that the sensitivity to CP violation is modified by LIV in a parameter-specific manner. We find correlations between off-diagonal LIV parameters, and non-trivial dependence on the new phases. In absence of LIV, DUNE is expected to establish CP violation at $5σ$ for a limited fraction of $δ_{CP}$ values. We find that the presence of $a_{ee}$, $a_{ττ}$, $a_{eμ}$ and $a_{eτ}$ weakens the CP discovery potential, reducing the achievable significance to below $3σ$ over a substantial fraction of $δ_{\rm CP}$. The independent impact of $c_{αβ}$ terms also results in suppression, but in combination with $a_{αβ}$, they introduce degeneracies, complicating the extraction of $δ_{CP}$. This generally results in a deterioration of CP violation sensitivities below $5σ$. These findings emphasize the importance of incorporating LIV effects in precision oscillation studies at upcoming long-baseline experiments.

### [45] [Boson-fermion meromorphic open-string vertex algebras and their canonically twisted modules](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05817)
*Qixuan Fang,Yi-Zhi Huang,Fei Qi*

Main category: math.QA

TL;DR: 本文从带有非退化对称双线性型的有限维向量空间出发，构造了一个 $\frac{\mathbb{Z}}{2}$-分次亚纯开弦顶点代数（$\frac{\mathbb{Z}}{2}$-graded meromorphic open-string vertex algebra）及其规范扭曲模（canonically twisted module），该代数是自由玻色-费米顶点算子超代数（free boson-fermion vertex operator superalgebra）的非交换推广，并通过推广的 Wick 定理（Wick's theorem）完成了构造，作为从旋流形（spin manifolds）构造 Dirac 型算子（Dirac-like operators）的代数部分。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在先前关于纯玻色和纯费米情形的工作（[H1]、[FQ]、[Q3]）基础上，本文旨在构造一种同时包含玻色子和费米子场且具有非交换推广的 $\frac{\mathbb{Z}}{2}$-分次代数结构，为从旋流形构造 Dirac 型算子提供代数基础。

Method: 从带有非退化对称双线性型的有限维向量空间出发，通过玻色子和费米子生成场的适当非交换推广来生成代数；保持产生算符与湮灭算符之间的超交换关系，但不对产生算符之间施加任何关系；利用推广的 Wick 定理给出两个玻色-费米生成场的正规乘积（normal-ordered product）之积的公式，进而构造出 $\frac{\mathbb{Z}}{2}$-分次亚纯开弦顶点代数及其规范扭曲模。

Result: 成功构造了 $\frac{\mathbb{Z}}{2}$-分次亚纯开弦顶点代数及其规范扭曲模；证明了在该非交换情形下推广的 Wick 定理成立；正规乘积（normal-ordering）依然保持良好定义；产生算符与湮灭算符之间的超交换关系与纯玻色和纯费米情形一致。

Conclusion: 本文的构造是从旋流形构造 Dirac 型算子的代数部分；该工作将早期纯玻色和纯费米情形下的结果推广到了同时包含玻色子和费米子的非交换情形。

Abstract: We construct a $\frac{\mathbb{Z}}{2}$-graded meromorphic open-string vertex algebra from a finite-dimensional vector space with a nondegenerate symmetric bilinear form, together with its canonically twisted module. This algebra is generated by suitable noncommutative generalizations of bosonic and fermionic fields and is a noncommutative generalization of the free boson-fermion vertex operator superalgebra. Similarly to the purely bosonic and purely fermionic cases in the early works by the second author in [H1], by Fiordalisi and the third author in [FQ], and by the third author in [Q3], the usual super-commutatitive relations between creation and annihilation operators still hold while no relations exist among creation operators. In particular, normal-ordering remains well-defined. As in [H1], [FQ], and [Q3], we prove a generalized Wick's theorem in this case, which gives a formula for a product of two normal ordered products of bosonic and fermionic generating fields. Using this generalized Wick's theorem, we construct the $\frac{\mathbb{Z}}{2}$-graded meromorphic open-string vertex algebra and its canonically twisted module in this case. The construction in this paper is the algebraic part of our construction of suitable Dirac-like operators from spin manifolds.

### [46] [Constraints on Yukawa-type New Forces from the Lamb Shift in Muonic Hydrogen and Deuterium](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05917)
*Chung-Chien Huang,Li-Bang Wang*

Main category: physics.atom-ph

TL;DR: 本文发展了一个解析框架，利用氢和氘的兰姆移位（Lamb shift）约束汤川型（Yukawa-type）第五力（fifth-force）相互作用。通过将六维坐标空间积分转化为一维动量空间卷积，并结合原子核电荷分布的形状因子（form factor），该框架从最新光谱数据导出了耦合常数α在力程λ∈[10⁻⁴, 10⁶] fm范围内的约束，并识别出λ∼10⁵ fm处的共振型抵消（resonance-like cancellation）导致的约束发散。结果表明该类新力引起的跃迁频移远低于当前光谱分辨率，光谱精度是探测此类相互作用的主要瓶颈。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有对汤川型第五力（Yukawa-type fifth-force）相互作用的约束方法往往需要引入近似处理，且未能系统利用原子光谱中的兰姆移位（Lamb shift）数据。本文旨在开发一个无需近似的解析框架，通过精确计算氢和氘的兰姆移位来约束这类长程相互作用，并评估当前光谱实验精度的敏感性限制。

Method: 将原本六重积分的坐标空间能量移位转化为一维动量空间卷积（momentum-space convolution），将原子形状因子（atomic form factor）与汤川势（Yukawa potential）直接结合，从而无需近似即可纳入经验核电荷分布。该方法利用氢和氘的最新光谱数据，在力程λ∈[10⁻⁴, 10⁶] fm范围内对耦合常数α进行约束。

Result: 在λ∼10⁵ fm处，2s和2p轨道的移位之间出现共振型抵消（resonance-like cancellation），导致能量移位消失、耦合常数α的约束发散，标志着吸引力与排斥力之间的过渡。约束结果独立于核电荷分布模型。所有新力引起的跃迁频移均远低于当前光谱分辨率。

Conclusion: 该框架提供了一种无需近似且模型无关的方式，利用兰姆移位约束汤川型第五力。光谱实验精度是探测此类新相互作用的主要瓶颈（primary bottleneck）；随着未来光谱精度的提升，该方法有望给出更严格的约束。

Abstract: We develop an analytical framework to constrain Yukawa-type fifth-force interactions using the Lamb shift in hydrogen and deuterium. The sixfold coordinate-space integral for the energy shift is transformed into a one-dimensional momentum-space convolution of the atomic form factor and the Yukawa potential, eliminating the need for approximations. This formulation directly incorporates empirical nuclear charge distributions through their form factors, making the implementation of experimental results straightforward. Applying this method to the latest hydrogen and deuterium spectroscopy data, we derive constraints on the coupling constant $α$ in the interaction range $λ\in [10^{-4}, 10^{6}]$~fm. A resonance-like cancellation between the $2s$ and $2p$ orbital shifts is identified at a critical range $λ\sim 10^{5}$~fm, where the energy shift vanishes and the constraint on $α$ diverges, marking a transition between attractive and repulsive regimes. The constraints are shown to be independent of the nuclear charge distribution model. Our results indicate that the transition frequency shifts induced by such new forces lie well below current spectroscopic resolution, establishing spectroscopic precision as the primary bottleneck for probing these interactions.

</details>

### [47] [Lund--Regge Geometry and Integrability of a Generalized Konno--Oono System](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05681)
*Jose Luis Diaz Palencia,Enrique G. Reyes*

Main category: nlin.SI

TL;DR: 本文扩展了经典曲面理论与偏微分方程之间的联系，聚焦于Chern–Tenenblat意义下的伪球型方程（pseudo-spherical type equations）及由Lund–Regge系统推广得到的曲面浸入$S^3$模型。以广义Konno–Oono系统为核心应用，通过构建含参过定线性问题、Riccati伪势展开等技术，证明了存在无穷多个非平凡局部守恒律（local conservation laws），从而证明其可积性；此外还分析了一类行波解，并展示了其生成浸入$S^3$曲面的能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在厘清经典曲面理论与偏微分方程（partial differential equations）之间的深层关联，特别是针对伪球型方程和Lund–Regge系统所启发的非平凡推广，希望通过严格的积分性（integrability）分析，为这类方程提供系统的理论框架。

Method: 采用含参数过定线性问题（parameter-dependent overdetermined linear problem）构造；运用Riccati伪势展开（Riccati pseudo-potential expansion）分析；引入立体投影坐标（stereographic coordinates）处理全方程流形；构造特殊代表元（special representatives）；通过水平上同调（horizontal cohomology）直接证明非平凡性。

Result: 成功建立了广义Konno–Oono系统的无穷多个非平凡局部守恒律，从而确认其可积性；获得了一类行波解（travelling wave solutions），这些解可用于生成浸入$S^3$的曲面，其高斯曲率（Gaussian curvature）周期性变号，平均曲率（mean curvature）为非零周期函数；在极限情形下得到局部全等于广义Clifford环面（generalized Clifford tori）的曲面。

Conclusion: 通过综合运用多种解析与几何工具，论文系统地揭示了广义Konno–Oono系统的可积结构，为曲面浸入$S^3$的几何构造提供了新的解析途径。

Abstract: We extend recent work on the relation between classical surface theory and partial differential equations, focusing on equations of pseudo-spherical type in the sense of Chern--Tenenblat and on a non-trivial generalization motivated by the Lund--Regge system describing surfaces immersed in $S^3$. As our main application, we study a generalized Konno--Oono system with three dependent variables introduced in a previous paper by one of the authors. We construct an associated parameter-dependent overdetermined linear problem and {\em we establish the existence of infinitely many non-trivial local conservation laws}, hence, integrability. The latter is the most technically demanding part of this paper: it requires a refined analysis of a Riccati pseudo-potential expansion, the use of stereographic coordinates at the full equation manifold level, the construction of special representatives, and a direct proof of non-triviality in horizontal cohomology. We also analyse an illustrative class of travelling wave solutions and show that they can be used to generate surfaces immersed in $S^3$ whose Gaussian curvature changes sign periodically, while their mean curvature are non-vanishing periodic functions. In a limit case, we obtain surfaces that are locally congruent to generalized Clifford tori.

</details>


### [48] [Asymptotic analysis of N-elliptic localized solutions for the Fokas--Lenells equation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06409)
*Wang Tang,Guo-Fu Yu*

Main category: nlin.SI

TL;DR: 本文研究了Foka-Lenells方程的N-椭圆局域解（N-elliptic localized solutions）。基于Lax对，利用Weierstrass椭圆函数构造椭圆函数解及基本解矩阵；通过N重达布-巴克伦变换（N-fold Darboux-Backlund transformation）导出N-椭圆局域解；借助由sigma函数表示的柯西行列式（Cauchy determinant），系统分析了所得解沿传播方向及方向间的渐近行为，并建立了这些解的对称性质。

Abstract: This paper investigates the N-elliptic localized solutions of the Foka-Lenells equation. The N-elliptic localized solutions are further derived via the N-fold Darboux-Backlund transformation. ### [49] [Universal self-similar evolution of two-dimensional Bose-Einstein condensates in the acoustic regime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06062)
*Guillaume Costa,Sergey Nazarenko,Giorgio Krstulovic*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文通过数值模拟二维Gross-Pitaevskii方程及其对应的波动力学方程，研究了玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（Bose-Einstein condensate）在非平衡驱动下湍流级联的非稳态演化，发现自相似解兼具第一类和第二类自相似性的特征，并确定了传播前缘动力学由通用常数β控制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在非平衡驱动下，玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体会产生非线性相互作用的密度波，引发湍流级联（turbulent cascade）并将能量向小尺度传递。本文旨在研究二维Gross-Pitaevskii方程（Gross-Pitaevskii equation, GPE）的非稳态演化，以揭示此类系统中自相似解的结构和动力学特性。

Method: 对二维Gross-Pitaevskii方程及其对应的波动力学方程（Wave Kinetic Equation）进行数值模拟，通过对比两种方法的解来识别自相似解。

Result: 识别出适用于原子及极化激元玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体的自相似解，这些解同时表现出第一类自相似性（first kind self-similarity）和第二类自相似性（second kind self-similarity）的特征。传播前缘的动力学具有普适性，受无量纲通用常数β控制，且通过数值计算确定了β的值。

Conclusion: 二维GPE中非平衡驱动的湍流级联存在兼具两类自相似特性的自相似解，其传播前缘的演化由通用常数β唯一刻画，表明该动力学行为具有普适性。

Abstract: When driven out of equilibrium, a Bose-Einstein condensate develops nonlinearly interacting density waves that trigger a turbulent cascade, transferring energy toward small scales. In this article, we investigate the nonstationary evolution of solutions to the two-dimensional Gross-Pitaevskii equation. Through numerical simulations of both the GPE and the corresponding Wave Kinetic Equation, we identify self-similar solutions relevant to atomic and polariton Bose-Einstein Condensates. These solutions exhibit characteristics of both first and second kind self-similarity. In particular, we show that the dynamics of the propagating front is universal, governed by a dimensionless universal constant $β$, which we determine numerically.

### [50] [Self-Bound Droplets of Ultracold Dipolar Molecules under Tunable Double Microwave Shielding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06130)
*Roger Melero,Jordi Boronat,Ferran Mazzanti*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用基态路径积分蒙特卡洛方法（Ground-State Path Integral Monte Carlo method）对系统进行数值模拟，通过改变椭圆度角ξ来系统分析基态结构与相行为。

Result: 圆极化情形（ξ=0）下系统呈现气相；当|ξ|超过约3°的阈值后，观测到单个或多个自束缚液滴（self-bound droplets）；随ξ增大，液滴迅速变得紧密结合，并形成超流阵列（superfluid array）；在正ξ区域结果与实验数据吻合良好，负ξ区域存在适度差异但符合分子间势的预期对称性。

Conclusion: 双微波屏蔽势的椭圆度角ξ是实现极性分子从气相到液滴相乃至超流阵列的调控关键参数，理论与实验在正ξ区域一致，负ξ区域的差异源于分子间相互作用的对称性特征。

Abstract: We use the Ground-State Path Integral Monte Carlo method to study a Bose-Einstein condensate of strongly interacting NaCs polar molecules under the action of a fully anisotropic double microwave shielding potential characterized by a linear and an elliptical polarization field. In particular, we analyze the ground state of the system and its structure as a function of the ellipticity angle $ξ$. While for the circularly polarized case ($ξ=0$) a gas phase is realized, one or more self-bound droplets are observed for small $|ξ|$'s above a threshold value near $3^\circ$. With increasing $ξ$, the observed droplets rapidly become tightly bound and are estimated to form a superfluid array. Our results compare favorably to the experimental observations in [Zhang et al., Nature \textbf{651}, 601 (2026)] for positive $ξ$, while moderate differences show up for $ξ<0$ where our simulations conform to the expected symmetries of the intermolecular potential.

</details>


### [51] [Chiral Graviton Modes in Non-Abelian lattice Fractional Quantum Hall states](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06267)
*Zeno Bacciconi,Min Long,Hernan Xavier,Hongyu Lu,Marcello Dalmonte,Zi Yang Meng*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文通过多种数值模拟方法，在玻色子Harper-Hofstadter模型（bosonic Harper-Hofstadter model）实现的非阿贝尔晶格分数量子霍尔态（non-Abelian lattice fractional quantum Hall state）中，首次展示了长寿命手征引力子模（chiral graviton mode）的存在，该信号可通过几何淬火（geometric quenches）在小型开放液滴中观测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 合成量子物质（synthetic quantum matter）为实现超越传统电子材料限制的分数量子霍尔效应（fractional quantum Hall effect）提供了高度可调谐的途径，但以往理论研究主要集中于基态性质（ground state properties），尚不清楚此类平台能否揭示分数量子霍尔态的关键激发特性（excitation properties）。

Method: 结合完整精确对角化（full exact diagonalization）、能带投影精确对角化（band-projected exact diagonalization）与矩阵乘积态模拟（matrix-product-state simulations），在单位填充因子（unity filling factor）的玻色子Harper-Hofstadter模型中，通过手征三体关联函数（chiral 3-body correlators）探测非阿贝尔晶格态上的激发模。

Result: 首次在晶格非阿贝尔态上证明存在长寿命手征引力子模（chiral graviton mode），该引力子信号与拓扑扇区（topological sector）无关；而其他中性模如磁旋子模（magnetoroton）和中性费米子模（neutral fermion）在目前可实现的体积下分辨率较低。

Conclusion: 该手征引力子模可通过几何淬火（geometric quenches）在小型开放液滴中直接观测，其实现条件与当前冷原子实验（cold-atom experiments）直接相关，为在合成量子平台上研究分数量子霍尔态的非平庸激发提供了可行途径。

Abstract: Synthetic quantum matter provides a highly tunable route to fractional quantum Hall physics beyond the constraints of conventional electronic materials. However, previous theoretical studies have mostly focused on their ground state properties. It remains unclear to what extent such platforms could reveal key excitation properties of fractional quantum Hall states. Here, we study charge-neutral collective excitations in a non-abelian lattice fractional quantum Hall state realized in the bosonic Harper-Hofstadter model at unity filling factior, realizing a Moore-Read ground state. Combining full exact diagonalization, band-projected exact diagonalization, and matrix-product-state simulations, we demonstrate the existence of a long-lived chiral graviton mode, probed by chiral 3-body correlators, for the first time on lattice non-Abelian states. The graviton signal is topological sector-independent and could be observed via geometric quenches in small open droplets directly relevant to current cold-atom experiments, while other neutral modes, such as the magnetoroton and neutral fermion, are less resolved at presently achievable volumes.

### [52] [Free Multiplicative Convolution and Erlang Moments in Monitored Quantum Transport](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05693)
*Joon Hyung Lee*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 该论文研究了受监测Haar乘积矩阵$B_L$的传输本征值分布，证明了经验本征值分布收敛于$ν_c^{\boxtimes L}$，并在自由小损失极限下通过$S_{μ_τ}(z)=\exp(τ/(1+z))$给出了极限律，导出了显式的Erlang型矩和谱性质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解受监测Haar乘积$B_L=(PS_L)(PS_{L-1})\cdots(PS_1)$的传输本征值（transmission eigenvalues）的渐近行为，揭示其与自由概率论（free probability）和小损失极限（small-loss limit）的联系。

Method: 采用自由概率论中的加性卷积（additive convolution）和乘法卷积框架，证明经验本征值分布收敛于$ν_c^{\boxtimes L}$，其中$ν_c=(1-c)δ_1+cδ_0$；随后取自由小损失极限，通过Lagrange反演（Lagrange inversion）推导显式矩，并分析谱分支点（branch point）等性质。

Result: 极限律由$S_{μ_τ}(z)=\exp(τ/(1+z))$刻画，矩为Erlang型分布；谱中原子质量$μ_τ(\{1\})=(1-τ)_+$，实分支点为$τ\mathrm{e}^{1-τ}$；对角线缩放$L\simτN$、$c=1/N$给出了定量收敛问题，低阶矩检验支持该结果。

Conclusion: 自由小损失极限下得到了传输本征值分布的闭合形式解，解释了Beenakker递推中出现的多项式，并为量子混沌和散射理论中的谱问题提供了新的分析工具。

Abstract: We study the transmission eigenvalues of monitored Haar products \[
  B_L=(PS_L)(PS_{L-1})\cdots(PS_1), \] where the $S_i$ are independent Haar unitaries and $P$ is a deterministic projection. For fixed $L$, we prove that the empirical eigenvalue distribution of $B_L^\dagger B_L$ converges to $ν_c^{\boxtimes L}$, where $ν_c=(1-c)δ_1+cδ_0$. We then take the free small-loss limit and identify the limiting law by \[
  S_{μ_τ}(z)=\exp\left(\fracτ{1+z}\right). \] Lagrange inversion gives explicit Erlang-type moments, explaining the polynomials appearing in Beenakker's recursion. We also record spectral consequences, including the atom $μ_τ(\{1\})=(1-τ)_+$ and the real branch point $τ\mathrm{e}^{1-τ}$, and formulate the diagonal scaling $L\simτN$, $c=1/N$, as a quantitative convergence problem supported by low-order moment checks.

### [53] [Attractor Flow Versus Hesse Flow in Wall-Crossing Structures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05433)
*Qiang Wang*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该论文将 Dieter Van den Bleeken 论文中的物理讨论置于 Kontsevich 和 Soibelman 的壁-crossing结构（wall-crossing structure）框架下，通过比较 Hesse 流（Hesse flow）与吸引子流（attractor flow）在复可积系统基空间上的关系，并引入对偶 Hesse 流（dual Hesse flow）和对偶吸引子流（dual attractor flow），展示了在 $\mathbb{Z}$-仿射结构（$\mathbb{Z}$-affine structure）旋转下这些流之间的相互转化关系，暗示了其在镜像对称（Mirror Symmetry）中的可能应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将 Van den Bleeken 论文中的物理讨论重新置于 Kontsevich 和 Soibelman 提出的壁-crossing结构（wall-crossing structure）数学框架中，并探索 Hesse 流与吸引子流之间的关系及其在镜像对称（Mirror Symmetry）中的潜在应用。

Method: 首先比较了 Van den Bleeken 论文中给出的 Hesse 流（Hesse flow）与复可积系统（complex integrable system）基空间上的吸引子流（attractor flow），证明两者均可在壁-crossing结构（wall-crossing structure）的形式体系中适用。随后引入了对偶 Hesse 流（dual Hesse flow）和对偶吸引子流（dual attractor flow）的概念。

Result: 在 $\mathbb{Z}$-仿射结构（$\mathbb{Z}$-affine structure）的旋转下，Hesse 流可转化为对偶吸引子流（dual attractor flow），而吸引子流可转化为对偶 Hesse 流（dual Hesse flow）。

Conclusion: 这些转化关系暗示了该框架可能在镜像对称（Mirror Symmetry）中具有应用价值。

Abstract: We recast the physics discussions in the paper of Dieter Van den Bleeken \cite{svan2012bps} within the context of wall-crossing structure à la Kontsevich and Soibelman \cite{kontsevich2014wall}. In particular, we compare the Hesse flow given in \cite{svan2012bps} and the attractor flow on the base of the complex integrable system, and show that both can be used in the formalism of wall-crossing structure. We also propose the notions of dual Hesse flow and dual attractor flow, and show that under the rotation of the $\mathbb{Z}$-affine structure, the Hesse flow can be transformed into the dual attractor flow, while the attractor flow into the dual Hesse flow. This suggests its possible use in Mirror Symmetry.

</details>


### [54] [Measurement-Access Risk Frontiers for Autonomous Scientific Control](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05696)
*Bo Peng*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出“物理可及决策”（PADM）框架，形式化定义了一条测量-访问风险前沿，揭示自主科学中存在“无免费自主性极限”：仅靠计算无法消除决策不确定性，必须通过扩展物理访问、容忍扰动或限制部署来弥补记录缺失的目标成分。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自主科学（autonomous science）的规模化不仅受限于算法、计算或数据量，更受限于平台在执行行动前所能暴露的物理记录（physical records），因此需要形式化刻画物理可及性对决策风险的约束。

Method: 提出物理可及决策（physically accessible decision-making, PADM）框架，构造一条测量-访问风险前沿（measurement-access risk frontier），即在成本、带宽、延迟、扰动、存储和执行约束下，对可实现的记录最小化贝叶斯最优目标风险（Bayes-optimal target risk）。

Result: 推导出无免费自主性极限（no-free-autonomy limit）：自动化无法仅通过计算压缩决策不确定性；最优控制器无法移除记录中缺失的目标成分；缩小该差距需要扩展访问、审计、容忍扰动、降低速度或限制部署。在受监控反馈中，仅含位移信息的控制器仍暴露于隐藏切换力，而有限带宽线索可在行动前恢复部分缺失投影。通过包含1000目标应力面板的化学感知候选排名审计等实验提供了可重复验证。

Conclusion: PADM框架能够在部署前识别出针对特定目标的审计价值与残余的预言机缺口（oracle gaps），为自主系统的物理访问设计提供理论指导。

Abstract: Rapidly scaling autonomous science is limited not only by algorithms, compute or data volume, but by which physical records a platform exposes before action. We formulate physically accessible decision-making (PADM) and a measurement-access risk frontier: the Bayes-optimal target risk minimized over records realizable under cost, bandwidth, latency, disturbance, memory and actuation constraints. The frontier gives a no-free-autonomy limit: automation cannot collapse decision uncertainty by computation alone; an optimal controller cannot remove target components absent from its record, and closing that gap requires expanded access, auditing, tolerated disturbance, slower operation or restricted deployment. In monitored feedback, displacement-only control remains exposed to a hidden switching force, whereas a finite-bandwidth cue recovers part of the missing projection before action. A chemistry-aware candidate-ranking audit with a 1000-target stress panel, Gaussian sensing, hidden-regime decisions and cost-aware/thermodynamic channel selection provide reproducible checks. PADM identifies target-specific audit value and residual oracle gaps before deployment.

</details>

Result: 证明了对于所有非零耦合常数，所有谱带均存在层级结构；该结构可应用于详细描述Kohmoto蝴蝶（Kohmoto butterfly）的结构特征。

Conclusion: 所揭示的谱带层级结构为理解Kohmoto模型提供了重要框架，并为后续工作中解决斯图米安哈密顿量的干十马提尼问题（dry ten Martini problem）提供了关键步骤。

Abstract: We study the Kohmoto model, a family of discrete Schrödinger operators with Sturmian potentials depending on a frequency and a coupling constant. We prove that, for all non-vanishing coupling constants, all spectral bands admit a hierarchical structure. This structure offers a variety of applications, including a detailed description of the Kohmoto butterfly and a central step towards the resolution of the dry ten Martini problem for Sturmian Hamiltonians, which we carry out in a subsequent work.

### [56] [Two fluid CFL strange quark stars with scalar dark matter: critical mass and mass gap implications](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05972)
*J. Sedaghat,G. H. Bordbar,M. Haghighat,S. M. Zebarjad*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文在双流体框架下，利用微扰QCD研究了存在标量玻色子暗物质时色-味锁定（CFL）相奇异夸克星（SQS）的结构。发现最大引力质量对暗物质质量呈非单调依赖，且暗物质的加入使得双流体CFL奇异夸克星构型能够在与GW170817潮汐形变约束定性兼容的同时，复现低质量间隙区（如GW190814次组分）的观测性质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准单流体模型中的紧凑星构型难以同时满足来自GW170817的潮汐形变（tidal deformability）约束和低质量间隙（lower mass-gap）区域（如GW190814的次组分）的观测性质，有必要探索包含暗物质的双流体奇异夸克星构型能否调和这些矛盾。

Method: 采用双流体形式（two-fluid formalism），分别处理奇异夸克物质与标量玻色子暗物质，使用微扰QCD（perturbative QCD）描述夸克物质状态方程。通过改变暗物质质量、配对能隙Δ和中心暗物质压力分数f_r，扫描参数空间并计算最大引力质量M_TOV、半径比R_DM/R_SQM以及无量纲潮汐形变Λ，并与NICER和GW170817观测数据进行比较。

Result: M_TOV对暗物质质量呈现非单调依赖关系，存在一个临界值，超过后M_TOV下降。某些纯CFL奇异夸克星构型（尤其是极硬状态方程和大最大质量者）无法同时满足GW170817的Λ约束和低质量间隙区域。包含暗物质的双流体构型则能复现GW190814次组分等低质量间隙区致密天体的观测性质，并与GW170817的Λ范围定性兼容。

Conclusion: 结果表明，暗物质的引入允许双流体CFL奇异夸克星构型进入常规定义的低质量间隙区域，奇异致密星构型可能部分占据该区域。但需注意GW170817约束原基于单流体框架，对双流体晕构型仅提供定性指导。

Abstract: We investigate the structure of strange quark stars (SQSs) in the color--flavor--locked (CFL) phase in the presence of scalar bosonic dark matter within a two--fluid formalism employing perturbative QCD. By considering different dark matter masses and varying the pairing gap $Δ$ and {the central dark matter pressure fraction} $f_r$, we analyze the impact of dark matter on the structural properties of SQSs, including the maximum gravitational mass $M_{\mathrm{TOV}}$, the ratio of dark matter to strange-quark-matter radii $R_{\mathrm{DM}}/R_{\mathrm{SQM}}$, and the dimensionless tidal deformability $Λ$. We further examine the compatibility of the resulting mass--radius relations with the recent NICER measurements of compact stars. Within the parameter space considered in this study, we find that $M_{\mathrm{TOV}}$ exhibits a non-monotonic dependence on the dark matter mass, with a critical value beyond which $M_{\mathrm{TOV}}$ decreases. We also show that some pure CFL strange quark star configurations, particularly those associated with very stiff EOSs and larger maximum masses, may not simultaneously remain compatible with the $Λ$ range inferred from GW170817 while occupying the lower mass--gap region. In contrast, the inclusion of dark matter allows two-fluid CFL strange quark star configurations to reproduce the observed properties of massive compact objects in the lower mass--gap region, such as the secondary component of GW190814, while remaining qualitatively compatible with the $Λ$ range inferred from GW170817. We note, however, that the GW170817 constraints were originally inferred within single-fluid compact-star frameworks and therefore provide only {qualitative guidance} for the present two-fluid halo configurations. Our results suggest that exotic compact-star configurations may populate part of the conventionally defined lower mass--gap region.

### [57] [Nonlinear Causality and Strong Hyperbolicity of Einstein-Israel-Stewart Theories of Transient Relativistic Fluid Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05639)
*Ian Cordeiro,Enrico Speranza,Fábio S. Bemfica,Marcelo M. Disconzi,Jorge Noronha*

Main category: nucl-th

TL;DR: 本文首次针对一大类相对论瞬态流体动力学（relativistic transient fluid dynamics）的体黏滞与剪切黏滞理论，建立了非线性因果性（causality）所需的同时充分必要条件，以及强双曲性（strong hyperbolicity）的充分条件，给出了纯代数形式的判据，适用于动态度规与固定背景、含或不含宇宙学常数及重子数守恒等多种场景，为数值模拟和唯象研究提供了可即用的分析工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 相对论性黏滞流体动力学是描述重离子碰撞和天体物理中极端物质行为的重要工具，但其非线性因果关系（causality）和适定性（well-posedness）的严格分析此前一直缺失。现有工作需要填补这一空白，为数值模拟和唯象研究提供可靠的数学基础。

Method: 研究涵盖一大类瞬态流体理论，包括Israel-Stewart理论、基于动理学理论（kinetic theory）的方法以及重求和梯度展开（resummed gradient-expansion）公式。通过严格的代数分析，推导出因果性（causality）的同时充要条件以及强双曲性（strong hyperbolicity）的充分条件，并证明这些条件在耦合爱因斯坦方程（Einstein's equations）的动态度规和固定背景上均成立。

Result: 首次获得了非线性区域中因果性的同时充分必要条件（simultaneously necessary and sufficient algebraic conditions）以及强双曲性的充分条件。这些条件为纯代数形式，不依赖时空对称性假设或特定状态方程（equation of state），允许输运系数（transport coefficients）依赖于耗散流（dissipative currents）。同时证明了动力学变量在解持续期间满足归一化、正交性、对称性和无迹性等物理约束。

Conclusion: 本文为相对论黏滞流体动力学提供了严格的数学基础，所建立的条件可直接用于检验因果性和适定性（well-posedness），为重离子碰撞（heavy-ion collisions）和天体物理学（astrophysics）中的数值与唯象研究提供了实用的分析工具。

Abstract: We present the first complete analysis of nonlinear causality and local well-posedness for a very general class of bulk and shear viscous theories of relativistic transient fluid dynamics, which encompasses (i) the original Israel-Stewart theory derived from entropy-current arguments, (ii) approaches derived from kinetic theory, and (iii) resummed gradient-expansion based formulations as particular subcases. Our work establishes, for the first time, simultaneously necessary and sufficient algebraic conditions for causality, alongside sufficient conditions guaranteeing strong hyperbolicity, in the full nonlinear regime. These results are rigorously proven for both systems coupled to Einstein's equations featuring a dynamic metric and on a fixed background, with or without a cosmological constant, and include baryon conservation (in the absence of heat/diffusion currents). The conditions are purely algebraic, require no simplifying spacetime symmetry assumptions or a specific equation of state, and allow all transport coefficients to depend on the dissipative currents. We also demonstrate that the normalization, orthogonality, symmetry, and tracelessness physical constraints on the dynamical variables are properly propagated during the lifetime of the solutions. Our results provide a readily usable toolset with which one can investigate the domain of applicability of relativistic viscous fluid dynamics in numerical and phenomenological studies in heavy-ion collisions and astrophysics.

</details>

### [58] [Characterization of p-stop isolation implants in silicon sensors using MOSFET structures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05528)
*Thomas Bergauer,Suman Chatterjee,Marko Dragicevic,Ioannis Kopsalis,Veronika Kraus*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为监测p型硅传感器中n型电极间的p-stop隔离注入一致性及隔离特性，需要一种非破坏性的诊断方法，而现有技术难以有效评估局部空间电荷效应和电场屏蔽对掺杂分布的影响。

Method: 通过测量MOSFET测试结构的转移特性随背板电压的变化，提取阈值电压（threshold voltage）和场依赖迁移率参数；基于阈值电压特性重建深度依赖的掺杂分布（depth-dependent doping profiles），并纳入p-stop注入引起的局域空间电荷效应（space-charge effects）和电场屏蔽（electric-field screening）。

Result: 该方法对不同p-stop几何结构（geometries）、掺杂浓度（doping concentrations）及不同晶圆类型（wafer types）均表现出敏感性分析能力；结果证实基于MOSFET的结构可用于非破坏性地监控p-stop一致性和电极间隔离特性。

Conclusion: MOSFET测试结构可作为一种有效的非破坏性诊断工具，用于监测硅探测器（silicon detectors）中p-stop隔离注入的工艺一致性和互电极隔离性能。

Abstract: Metal-oxide-semiconductor field-effect transistor (MOSFET) test structures are investigated to characterize p-stop isolation implants between n-type electrodes in p-type silicon sensors. The device transfer characteristics are measured as a function of the voltage applied to the backside to extract the threshold voltage, which quantifies inter-electrode isolation, and the field-dependent mobility parameters. We present a methodology to reconstruct depth-dependent doping profiles from the threshold voltage characteristics, accounting for the localized space-charge effects and electric-field screening induced by the p-stop implants. The study evaluates the sensitivity of this technique to various p-stop geometries and doping concentrations across different wafer types. The results demonstrate the potential of MOSFET-based structures as a non-destructive diagnostic for monitoring p-stop consistency and inter-electrode isolation properties in silicon detectors.

</details>

### [59] [Finite signal-to-noise ratio bias in parameter estimation for damped oscillations: cautionary remark about catalog-level black-hole spectroscopy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05486)
*Koutarou Kyutoku*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了阻尼振荡参数估计中的系统偏差，发现即使模型与分析方法正确，有限信噪比（signal-to-noise ratio, ρ）也会导致阻尼时间（damping time）被高估，原因包括先验梯度（prior gradient）和高阶似然几何修正（higher-order finite-ρ correction to the likelihood geometry）；多个事件联合推断可能放大偏差，黑洞光谱学（black-hole spectroscopy）若不当组合约100个ρ=10的事件，可能错误报告Kerr假设（Kerr hypothesis）被违反。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 受引力波物理中黑洞光谱学应用的启发，研究阻尼振荡参数估计中的偏差来源，以识别和避免在黑洞光谱学分析中得出误导性结论。

Method: 考虑白噪声中固定起始时间的单模阻尼正弦信号（single-mode damped sinusoid），在有限信噪比条件下分析参数估计偏差：通过先验梯度效应和高阶似然几何修正两类机制推导偏差的产生原因，并设计缓和策略。

Result: 有限信噪比下阻尼时间偏向更大值，且该偏差不被质量因子（quality factor）抑制；两种偏差来源分别是振幅先验的递减趋势导致的先验梯度效应，以及有限ρ对似然几何的高阶修正；不当联合ρ=10的多个事件时，约100个事件即可能导致黑洞光谱学错误报告Kerr假设被违反。

Conclusion: 即便模型与分析正确，阻尼振荡参数估计仍存在系统性偏差，需在单事件层面采用简单策略以缓解偏差，避免在目录级（catalog-level）分析中产生虚假的物理学结论。

Abstract: We investigate biases in parameter estimation for damped oscillations motivated by applications to black-hole spectroscopy in gravitational-wave physics. Focusing on the simplest model of a single-mode damped sinusoid with a fixed start time in white noise, we show that, at finite signal-to-noise ratio ρ, the damping time is biased toward larger values without being suppressed by the quality factor for two reasons. One is the gradient of the prior, through which the damping time is affected by the typically decreasing prior on the amplitude. The other is a higher-order finite-ρcorrection to the likelihood geometry. These biases arise even if the model and analysis are appropriate. Moreover, they could be exaggerated in naive joint inferences from catalog events. Quantitatively, if estimates from multiple events with ρ=10 are combined without due care, the catalog-level black-hole spectroscopy could report false violation of the Kerr hypothesis with >~100 events. We also propose simple strategies to mitigate these biases at the level of individual events.

</details>


### [60] [Black Hole Black Boxes: Numerical Black Hole Metrics via AInstein Neural Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05489)
*Tancredi Schettini Gherardini,Edward Hirst,Alexander George Stapleton*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文扩展了AInstein无监督神经架构，使其能够求解洛伦兹号差下的黎曼爱因斯坦方程，并通过恢复最大扩展施瓦西度规验证了该方法，进一步将其作为搜索任意黑洞解的新工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将原有基于黎曼号差的爱因斯坦方程无监督神经求解方法扩展至物理上更重要的洛伦兹号差（Lorentzian signature），并验证其能否恢复已知黑洞解及发现新型黑洞解。

Method: 采用物理信息神经网络（Physics Informed Neural Network, PINN）架构，将$S^{2}$通过标准嵌入全局处理，网络在流形$\mathbb{R}^{2} \times \mathbb{R}^{3}$上学习环境度规（ambient metric），其中$\mathbb{R}^2$使用彭罗斯坐标（Penrose coordinates），$S^{2}$上的度规通过拉回（pullback）获得。训练目标先以真空爱因斯坦方程、二次外尔标量约束（quadratic Weyl scalar constraint）和$SO(3)$对称为损失函数恢复施瓦西度规，再引入佩特罗夫特殊指标（Petrov speciality index）、视界曲率锚（horizon curvature anchor）和捕获面约束（trapped-surface constraint）以搜索代数一般的佩特罗夫I型（Petrov type I）解。

Result: 成功恢复了最大扩展施瓦西几何（maximally extended Schwarzschild geometry），并展示了该方法作为任意黑洞解搜索工具的能力，可找到具有真实捕获内部（genuinely trapped interior）的新型一般型洛伦兹爱因斯坦度规。

Conclusion: 基于PINN的AInstein架构可有效推广至洛伦兹号差，不仅能验证已知黑洞解，还能系统搜索具有潜在新物理意义的代数一般型黑洞解。

Abstract: The AInstein architecture introduced an unsupervised neural method for solving the Riemannian Einstein equations on arbitrary manifolds. This Physics Informed Neural Network approach (PINN) is extended here to Lorentzian signature, validated by recovering the maximally extended Schwarzschild geometry, and tested as novel search method for arbitrary black hole solutions. The topology is built into the architecture by treating $S^{2}$ globally through its standard embedding, such that the network learns an ambient metric on the manifold $\mathbb{R}^{2} \times \mathbb{R}^{3}$, where Penrose coordinates are chosen for $\mathbb{R}^2$ and the metric on $S^{2}$ is obtained by pullback. The architecture is first trained with the objective of recovering the Schwarzschild metric via losses encoding the vacuum Einstein equation, a quadratic Weyl scalar constraint, and the $SO(3)$ symmetry of the resultant metric; directly motivated by the Birkhoff--Jebsen theorem. Following this, the objective is generalised to use the Petrov speciality index, a horizon curvature anchor, and a trapped-surface constraint, to allow search for algebraically general Petrov type I solutions, finding potentially novel general-type Lorentzian Einstein metrics with a genuinely trapped interior.

</details>


### [61] [Three-dimensional wave optics for weak-field lensing of gravitational waves](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05491)
*Mariana Carrillo-González,Alan Heavens,Lorne Whiteway*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种微扰格林函数（perturbative Green's function）方法，用于处理弱引力势下的引力透镜（gravitational lensing），无需将引力势局限在薄透镜平面上，且同时适用于波光学（wave optics）和几何光学（geometric optics）区域。通过将位置空间积分重写为傅里叶（Fourier）或动量空间（momentum-space）积分，该方法直接给出三维玻恩近似（Born approximation），并可系统推广至后玻恩阶（post-Born orders）。针对史瓦西透镜（Schwarzschild lens）的计算展示了广义相对论修正由参数 $GM\omega\,b/\chi_{\rm eff}$ 控制，在标准弱透镜配置下可忽略，但在极端几何（如层级三合星系统中小源-透镜间距）中变得重要。该方法明确了引力波透镜中玻恩近似、大距离近似和近轴近似的有效范围，并为处理一般透镜势提供了框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有弱引力透镜方法通常假设引力势局限在薄透镜平面上，且多在几何光学或波光学某一区域分别处理。本文旨在发展一种统一的微扰格林函数方法，克服薄透镜近似（thin-lens approximation）的限制，同时适用于波光学与几何光学区域，并系统处理后玻恩阶及广义相对论（general relativity）修正。

Method: 将透镜问题中的位置空间积分重写为傅里叶/动量空间积分，借鉴散射振幅（scattering amplitude）计算技术。该方法直接给出三维玻恩近似，并可系统扩展到后玻恩阶。在史瓦西透镜中，计算了领头玻恩项以及由 $\mathcal{O}(G^2)$ 势修正产生的新后玻恩贡献，保留了超出常规近轴展开（paraxial expansion）的有限距离修正。还讨论了高阶牛顿修正、长程势的红外敏感性（infrared sensitivity）以及由汤川势（Yukawa potential）给出的牛顿势的规范化形式，并在FLRW背景下进行了推广。

Result: 在史瓦西透镜的小角度区域，广义相对论修正由参数 $GM\omega\,b/\chi_{\rm eff}$ 控制。在标准弱透镜配置下该修正可忽略，但在源-透镜间距极小的极端几何（如层级三合星系统）中变得重要。识别了FLRW背景下的领先平直空间极限，并估计了包括尾部效应（tails）在内的曲率诱导修正的大小。

Conclusion: 该方法阐明了引力波透镜中玻恩近似、大距离近似和近轴近似各自的适用范围，为处理一般透镜势提供了一个系统框架。不同修正（广义相对论效应、高阶牛顿修正、曲率效应）的相对重要性可通过所识别的控制参数进行评估。

Abstract: We develop a perturbative Green's function approach to gravitational lensing by weak gravitational potentials that need not be localized on a thin lens plane and that applies in both the wave optics and geometric optics regimes. We recast position-space integrals as Fourier, or momentum-space, integrals that appear in scattering amplitude calculations. The method gives the Born approximation directly in three dimensions and can be systematically extended to post-Born orders. For a Schwarzschild lens, we compute the leading Born term and new post-Born contributions arising from the order $\mathcal{O}(G^2)$ correction to the potential, keeping finite-distance corrections beyond the usual paraxial expansion. We show that these general-relativistic corrections are controlled by the parameter $GMω\,b/χ_{\rm eff}$ in the small-angle regime, and are therefore negligible for standard weak-lensing configurations but become relevant in more extreme geometries (such as hierarchical triples with very small source--lens separations). We also discuss higher-order Newtonian corrections, their infrared sensitivity for a long-range potential, and the regulated form of the Newtonian potential given by the Yukawa potential. Finally, we formulate the corresponding calculation in an FLRW background, identifying the leading flat-space limit and estimating the size of curvature-induced corrections including tails. This method clarifies the regime of validity of the Born, large-distance, and paraxial approximations in gravitational-wave lensing and provides a framework for treating generic lensing potentials.

</details>


### [62] [Degenerate and connection-dependent cosmological sectors in f(Q,C) gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05521)
*Ismael Ayuso*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文在对称遥平行几何（symmetric teleparallel geometry）框架下研究 $f(Q,C)$ 引力理论中的宇宙学解，指出该理论中存在三种不同仿射联络实现所对应的宇宙学扇区，其中一种简并扇区在动力学上等价于 $f(\mathring{R})$ 引力，而另一类非等价模型则通过联络场方程引入新自由度，产生 $f(\mathring{R})$ 理论所不具备的新宇宙学现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索 $f(Q,C)$ 引力理论在 FLRW 时空中的宇宙学解，明确三种仿射联络实现是否导致不同的宇宙学动力学行为，并区分该理论中与 $f(\mathring{R})$ 等价的部分及其真正的新物理扇区。

Method: 在对称遥平行几何中构建 $f(Q,C)$ 引力理论，其中非度规标量（nonmetricity scalar）$Q$ 与边界项（boundary term）$C$ 通过 $\mathring{R}=Q+C$ 与广义相对论的里奇标量（Ricci scalar）相关联。利用 FLRW 度量的对称性导出仿射联络的三种不同实现，并分别分析其场方程及宇宙学动力学行为。

Result: 在一种最简单的联络实现中，联络场方程施加约束，使理论在动力学上等价于 $f(\mathring{R})$ 引力，三种联络实现的宇宙学背景方程趋于一致，形成简并宇宙学扇区。另一类非等价模型中，联络选择具有物理意义，联络扇区引入额外动力学自由度，产生 $f(\mathring{R})$ 引力中没有的新宇宙学现象。

Conclusion: $f(Q,C)$ 引力包含一个与 $f(\mathring{R})$ 等价的简并扇区，但也存在真正非等价的模型类别，后者通过联络自由度展现更丰富的宇宙学现象，超越标准广义相对论框架。

Abstract: We investigate cosmological solutions in $f(Q,C)$ gravity formulated within symmetric teleparallel geometry, where gravitation is described by the nonmetricity scalar $Q$ and the boundary term $C$, related to the Ricci scalar of General Relativity through $\mathring{R}=Q+C$ in the absence of curvature and torsion. The symmetry requirements of FLRW spacetime admit three distinct realizations of the affine connection, leading in principle to three different cosmological sectors within the same theory. We show that the connection field equations play a crucial role in determining the cosmological dynamics. In their simplest realization, these equations impose a constraint that renders the theory dynamically equivalent to $f(\mathring{R})$ gravity, causing the cosmological background equations associated with the three connection realizations to coincide. This defines a degenerate cosmological sector of $f(Q,C)$ gravity, in which three a priori distinct geometric constructions converge to the same cosmological dynamics. We then consider the complementary class of genuinely nonequivalent $f(Q,C)$ models, for which the choice of connection becomes physically relevant. In this regime, the connection sector introduces additional dynamical degrees of freedom and gives rise to novel cosmological phenomenology absent in $f(\mathring{R})$ gravity.

</details>


### [63] [Charged black holes embedded in matter with anisotropic pressure: Horizon Structure and Quasinormal Mode Spectra](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05550)
*D. N. Garzon,Jiayi Zhang,Elena Kopteva,Helvi Witek*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究嵌入各向异性压力物质环境中的带电黑洞，利用Kiselev度规描述时空，通过扩展Leaver连分数方法并结合自动微分技术计算无质量带电标量场的类正则模（quasinormal modes），发现环境物质会改变振荡频率和阻尼率，产生长寿命模式（long-lived modes）以及避免交叉区（avoided crossings）和谱系重组（reorganization of modes），凸显了在现实黑洞建模中纳入环境物质的重要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现实黑洞往往处于天体物理环境（astrophysical environments）中，包括可能的暗物质分布（dark matter distributions），这些环境会改变黑洞的可观测性质并在其类正则模谱（quasinormal mode spectra）中留下印迹，因此需要研究环境物质对黑洞物理的影响。

Method: 将环境建模为各向异性压力（anisotropic pressure）物质，采用Kiselev度规（Kiselev metric）描述嵌入其中的带电黑洞时空；对Leaver连分数方法（Leaver's continued fraction method）进行非平凡扩展以纳入周围物质效应，并结合自动微分技术（automatic differentiation techniques）；同时与六阶Wentzel-Kramers-Brillouin近似（sixth-order WKB approximation）的结果进行对比。

Result: 周围物质改变了振荡频率（oscillation frequencies）和阻尼率（damping rates），并导致长寿命模式（long-lived modes）的出现；谱中出现了避免交叉区（avoided crossings）和模式重组（reorganization of modes）现象。

Conclusion: 研究表明，在真实黑洞建模中纳入周围物质具有重要性；所开发的数值框架为研究非真空时空（non-vacuum spacetimes）中的类正则模提供了工具，并可推广到嵌入物质场中的一大类黑洞几何（black-hole geometries）。

Abstract: In realistic settings, black holes are expected to be embedded in astrophysical environments. These environments, including possible dark matter distributions, can modify observable properties of black holes and leave imprints on their quasinormal mode spectra. In this work, we model the environment as matter with anisotropic pressure, and we consider a charged black hole embedded in it. The resulting spacetime is described by the Kiselev metric. We first analyze its horizon structure. We then investigate the quasinormal modes of a massless charged scalar field propagating on this background. For this purpose, we develop a nontrivial extension of Leaver's continued fraction method to incorporate the effects of the surrounding matter, and we combine this framework with automatic differentiation techniques. We also compare our results to those obtained with the sixth-order Wentzel-Kramers-Brillouin approximation.
  We find that the surrounding matter modifies the oscillation frequencies and damping rates and leads to the appearance of long-lived modes. We also identify avoided crossings regions and reorganization of the modes in the spectra. Our results demonstrate the importance of incorporating surrounding matter when modeling realistic black holes. The numerical framework we developed here provides a tool for studying quasinormal modes in non-vacuum spacetimes and can be extended to a broad class of black-hole geometries embedded in matter fields.

</details>


### [64] [Ruppeiner thermodynamic geometry, microstructure, quasinormal modes and greybody factors of the Einstein-Skyrme black hole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05673)
*Shakhboz Khasanov,Akmal Safarov,Bo Yang,Habtamu Menberu Tedila*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了爱因斯坦-斯凯米理论（Einstein-Skyrme theory）中精确静态球对称黑洞的热力学微观结构、准正则模谱和灰体因子，发现曲率在极端极限下发散、朱尔-汤姆逊系数恒为负，并给出了灰体因子的严格下界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基于最近建立的将斯凯米耦合常数K和λ提升为广延变量的第一定律，首次对这种稀有解析有毛黑洞（analytic hairy black hole）的热力学微观结构和微扰谱学进行全面研究，填补此前热力学分析中未涉及的理论空白。

Method: 采用鲁佩纳几何（Ruppeiner geometry）构造质量黑塞矩阵（Hessian of the mass）得到标量曲率；进行类似焦耳-汤姆逊（Joule-Thomson）的等焓膨胀分析；推导无质量标量场的有效势，并用维瑟方法（Visser's method）获得灰体因子（greybody factor）的严格下界闭式解。

Result: 曲率在二阶（热容）相变点有限，但在极端零温极限下发散；整个物理允许区域内曲率符号单一，表明微观相互作用以吸引型为主且强度向极端极限增强；朱尔-汤姆逊系数严格为负，黑洞随λ增大而冷却，无反转温度；耦合K显著降低有效势垒，λ影响较小；增大K提高灰体因子下界，增大λ略微抑制低频透射。

Conclusion: 本文提供了该类精确解析有毛黑洞在热力学微观结构和微扰谱学方面的首个全面研究，补充并拓展了现有热力学分析至此前未探索的理论区域。

Abstract: We investigate the thermodynamic microstructure, quasinormal mode spectrum, and greybody factors of the exact, static, spherically symmetric black hole in Einstein-Skyrme theory, building on the recently established first law that promotes the Skyrme couplings K and λ to extensive variables. Using Ruppeiner geometry, we construct the scalar curvature from the Hessian of the mass. The curvature remains finite at the second-order (heat-capacity) phase transition but diverges in the extremal, zero-temperature limit. Throughout the physically admissible region the curvature retains a single sign, indicating microscopic interactions of one dominant (attractive) type whose strength grows towards extremality. We perform a Joule-Thomson-like isenthalpic expansion and prove analytically that the corresponding coefficient is strictly negative across the entire physical parameter space, implying the black hole always cools as λ increases at a fixed mass, with no inversion temperature. Turning to perturbations, we derive the effective potential for massless scalar fields. The solid-angle-deficit coupling K controls its shape-substantially lowering the barrier-while at fixed K the quartic coupling λ produces only minor changes. Rigorous lower bounds on greybody factors are obtained in closed form using Visser's method: increasing K raises the bound, since a larger horizon lowers the centrifugal barrier, whereas increasing λ mildly suppresses low-frequency transmission. Our results provide the first comprehensive study of the thermodynamic microstructure and perturbative spectroscopy of this rare analytic hairy black hole, complementing and extending the existing thermodynamic analysis into previously unexplored territory.

</details>


### [65] [On the Uniqueness of Embeddings of Causal Sets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05840)
*Nathan Madsen*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出了因果集（causal set）在洛伦兹流形（Lorentzian manifold）中良态嵌入（well-conditioned embedding）的概念，证明了若一个因果集可良态嵌入到两个流形中，则这两个流形的内部是ε-近似等距的。同时证明了在高密度极限下，泊松撒点（Poisson sprinkling）几乎必然生成可良态嵌入的因果集，且误差ε在高密度极限下趋于零。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 因果集理论是量子引力（quantum gravity）的一种离散化方案，其核心问题在于确定一个因果集能否唯一地对应一个光滑洛伦兹流形。本文旨在给出一个精确的数学框架，定义何种嵌入是“良态的”，并证明该嵌入在流形层面上能保证唯一的近似等距结构。

Method: 作者首先定义了因果集到洛伦兹流形的良态嵌入概念；然后通过构造性论证，证明在满足高密度条件的泊松撒点过程中，几乎必然可以产生具有良态嵌入的因果集；最后利用流形上的因果结构与离散因果集的对应关系，推导出两个良态嵌入之间的ε-近似等距关系。

Result: 如果同一个因果集允许两个良态嵌入到不同的洛伦兹流形中，那么这两个流形的内部必然在ε-近似等距（ε-approximate isometry）的意义下相互关联。误差ε有明确的解析表达式，并在高密度极限下趋于零。

Conclusion: 本文为因果集到洛伦兹流形的嵌入提供了严格的理论基础，证明了在高密度条件下该嵌入具有近似唯一的几何对应关系，从而支持了因果集理论作为量子引力离散模型的可行性。

Abstract: We introduce the notion of a well-conditioned embedding of a causal set into a Lorentzian manifold and prove that if a causal set admits well-conditioned embeddings into two manifolds, then their interiors are related by an $\varepsilon$-approximate isometry. To justify the definition, we show that in the high-density limit a Poisson sprinkling almost surely yields a causal set possessing a well-conditioned embedding. The error $\varepsilon$ is given explicitly and tends to zero in the high-density limit.

</details>


### [66] [Probing near-zone magnetic fields with extreme mass-ratio inspirals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05909)
*Jin-Lu Hu,Xin-Dong Du,Peng-Cheng Li,Tieguang Zi*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本研究探讨了弱近区磁场能否在极端质量比旋进（EMRI）波形上留下可观测印记。通过磁化施瓦西（Ernst）解建模中心大质量黑洞，采用混合源修正Regge–Wheeler–Zerilli近似计算旋进演化。结果表明，在特定参数下极强磁场可产生可探测的去相移，但普通磁场环境效应过弱，难以被LISA观测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究弱近区磁场是否能在极端质量比旋进（extreme-mass-ratio inspiral, EMRI）波形中留下可观测的印记，从而评估EMRI作为探测黑洞周围磁场环境的潜在工具。

Method: 采用磁化施瓦西解（magnetized Schwarzschild, Ernst solution）描述中心大质量黑洞，将次级致密天体视为位于赤道圆测地线上的中性点粒子。计算磁场对圆轨道参数和内稳定圆轨道（innermost stable circular orbit, ISCO）的修正，并利用混合源修正Regge–Wheeler–Zerilli近似（hybrid, source-corrected Regge–Wheeler–Zerilli approximation）演化旋进过程，其中施瓦西波传播势保持固定，而源项在磁化轨道上求值。

Result: 对标称系统（\(M=10^6M_\odot\), \(\mu=10M_\odot\)），场强\(B\simeq4\times10^{-5}M^{-1}\)（对应\(B_{\rm phys}\sim10^9\,{\rm G}\)）在一年内产生约1.3弧度的去相移（dephasing），并达到所采用的LISA噪声加权失配（noise-weighted mismatch）阈值。

Conclusion: EMRI原则上能够探测近区极强磁场，但大质量黑洞周围的普通磁场环境在现有近似下可能过弱，难以产生可探测效应。

Abstract: We investigate whether weak near-zone magnetic fields can leave observable imprints on extreme-mass-ratio inspiral (EMRI) waveforms. The central massive black hole is modeled by the magnetized Schwarzschild, or Ernst, solution, and the secondary compact object is treated as a neutral point particle on equatorial circular geodesics. We compute the magnetic corrections to the circular-orbit quantities and the innermost stable circular orbit, and then evolve the inspiral using a hybrid, source-corrected Regge--Wheeler--Zerilli approximation, in which the Schwarzschild wave-propagation potentials are kept fixed while the source is evaluated on the magnetized orbit. For a fiducial system with \(M=10^6M_\odot\) and \(μ=10M_\odot\), a field strength \(B\simeq 4\times10^{-5}M^{-1}\), corresponding to \(B_{\rm phys}\sim10^9\,{\rm G}\), produces a one-year dephasing of about \(1.3\) rad and reaches the adopted LISA-noise-weighted mismatch threshold. Our results suggest that EMRIs can in principle probe extremely strong near-zone magnetic fields, whereas ordinary magnetic environments around massive black holes are likely too weak to produce detectable effects within the present approximation.

Result: 所提出的PINN方法结合新技术能够成功求解通用双黑洞（BBH）系统的哈密顿约束方程。与传统数值结果的对比验证表明，该方法具有高精度和鲁棒性。

Abstract: Numerical relativity (NR), solving Einstein equation numerically, plays an important role in source modelling for gravitational wave astronomy. Traditional methods for NR including finite difference method, spectral method and finite element method have been well developed. But newly developed neural network methods for partial differential equations (PDE) have not been well studied yet for NR. We present a Physics-Informed Neural Network (PINN) method to solve the Hamiltonian constraint equation for binary black hole (BBH) initial data in NR. This equation is a highly non-linear elliptic PDE, posing significant challenges for conventional PINN approaches. To overcome these difficulties, we introduce a set of new techniques. We show that our PINN together with these techniques can successfully solve the Hamiltonian constraint equation for generic BBH systems. Validation against the traditional results demonstrates the high accuracy and robustness of our method, revealing the immense potential of constructing a PINN-based initial data solution to all BBH systems for NR.

### [68] [Quasinormal modes of scalar perturbations in Rastall thick brane](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06081)
*Shan Huang,Chun-Chun Zhu,Tao-Tao Sui*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在Rastall引力框架下研究五维厚膜模型中标量-引力（graviscalar）扇区的准正则模（quasinormal modes），通过伯恩斯坦谱方法（Bernstein spectral method）和频域直接积分结合时域演化，发现准正则模频谱强烈依赖于Rastall参数λ，其中虚部随λ增大单调减小（更长寿的模），实部呈现非单调行为，且晚期扰动尾巴遵循幂律衰减，其指数由Rastall参数决定。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究对Rastall引力中厚膜模型的动力学特性（特别是准正则模行为）缺乏系统分析，需要揭示其标量扰动在时域和频域中的完整演化特征，以探索修正引力在额外维度场景中可能的观测信号。

Method: 首先在五维厚膜模型中导出标量扰动的主方程（master equation），将其约化为关于卡鲁扎-克莱因模（Kaluza-Klein modes）的类薛定谔本征值问题（Schrödinger-like eigenvalue problem）；然后采用伯恩斯坦谱方法（Bernstein spectral method）和频域直接积分计算复准正则频率，并辅以数值时域演化进行验证。

Result: 准正则模频谱强烈依赖于Rastall参数λ：频率虚部（控制衰减率）随λ增大单调减小，表明模式寿命延长；实部表现出更复杂的非单调行为。晚期扰动尾巴呈现幂律衰减（power law），其指数由Rastall参数决定，与势函数渐近形式的理论预测一致。

Conclusion: 研究成果为Rastall厚膜模型标量扇区提供了全面的动力学刻画，为在多维场景中探测修正引力（modified gravity）提供了潜在的观测特征。

Abstract: We investigate quasinormal modes of the graviscalar sector in a five-dimensional thick brane model in Rastall gravity. By considering a specific flat brane solution supported by a canonical scalar field, we derive a master equation and reduce it to a Schrödinger-like eigenvalue problem for the Kaluza-Klein modes. Using the Bernstein spectral method and direct integration in the frequency domain, complemented by numerical time-domain evolutions, we compute the complex quasinormal frequencies for the scalar perturbations. Our results reveal a strong dependence of the QNM spectrum on $λ$: the imaginary parts of the frequencies, governing the decay rate, decrease monotonically with increasing $λ$, indicating longer-lived modes. The real parts exhibit a more complex, non-monotonic behavior. Furthermore, we analyze the late-time behavior of the perturbations, showing that the asymptotic tail follows a power law whose exponent is determined by the Rastall parameter, in agreement with theoretical predictions for the asymptotic form of the potential. These findings provide a comprehensive dynamical characterization of the scalar sector of Rastall thick branes, offering potential observational signatures for probing modified gravity in extra-dimensional scenarios.

### [69] [Noise-induced stabilization of Schwarzschild--AdS black holes under stochastic Ricci flow](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06100)
*Jihui Wang,Matteo Lulli,Antonino Marciano*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本论文研究球对称扰动的Schwarzschild–Anti de Sitter黑洞度规的随机Ricci流（stochastic Ricci flow），发现随机噪声可以抑制热力学不稳定（负热容）区域中的扰动增长，从而改变几何稳定性与热力学稳定性之间的关联。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在Headrick和Wiseman的Ricci流分析基础上，引入负宇宙学常数（negative cosmological constant）并通过Ricci目标项（Ricci-target term）加以描述，旨在探究Ricci流与黑洞热力学热容（thermodynamic heat capacity）之间的相关性。

Method: 采用数值模拟研究确定性Ricci流下角向扇区扰动的演化；随后引入乘性随机噪声（multiplicative stochastic noise），并基于熵变量在热力学自由能景观（thermodynamic free-energy landscape）上重新表述动力学，辅以蒙特卡洛模拟（Monte Carlo simulation）和福克-普朗克方程（Fokker–Planck equation）进行验证。

Result: 在正热容（positive heat-capacity）区域，扰动向Schwarzschild–Anti de Sitter不动点弛豫；在负热容（negative heat-capacity）区域，扰动在确定性Ricci流下增长；但足够强的随机性可以抑制这种增长，从而稳定原本热力学不稳定的构型。

Conclusion: 随机涨落（stochastic fluctuations）能够改变渐近Anti de Sitter黑洞时空中Ricci流下的几何稳定性与热力学稳定性之间的关系。

Abstract: We investigate the stochastic Ricci flow of spherically symmetric perturbations of the Schwarzschild--Anti de Sitter black-hole metric. Elaborating on the Ricci-flow analysis of Headrick and Wiseman, we include a negative cosmological constant through a Ricci-target term and study how the flow is correlated with the thermodynamic heat capacity of the black hole. Numerical simulations show that, in the positive heat-capacity regime, perturbations of the angular sector of the metric relax toward the Schwarzschild--Anti de Sitter fixed point, while in the negative heat-capacity regime they grow under the deterministic Ricci flow. We then introduce a multiplicative stochastic noise and find that sufficiently strong stochasticity can suppress the growth of these perturbations, effectively stabilizing configurations that would otherwise be thermodynamically unstable. Finally, we reformulate the dynamics in terms of an entropy variable evolving on a thermodynamic free-energy landscape, and support the metric-flow results through Monte Carlo simulations and the associated Fokker--Planck equation. These results suggest that stochastic fluctuations can modify the relation between geometric stability under Ricci flow and thermodynamic stability in asymptotically Anti de Sitter black-hole spacetimes.

### [70] [Starobinsky Inflation in k-Essence Framework: Attractor Dynamics, Reheating, and Consistency with ACT DR6](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06112)
*Abolhassan Mohammadi,Yogesh,Hongwei Tan,M. Sami*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出在k-本质（k-essence）框架下，通过引入幂律型动能耦合项$F(φ)=1+Aφ^n$，可以在不修改引力理论的前提下，使Starobinsky势的标量谱指数$n_s$、谱指数跑动$α_s$和张量标量比$r$的预测值重新落于ACT DR6的$1σ$置信区间内。数值求解背景方程、Hamilton-Jacobi形式论分析以及相空间检验均确认了暴涨解的吸引子行为。再加热（reheating）阶段的有效状态方程参数固定为$w_{\rm re}=0$，再加热温度$T_{\rm re} \sim 10^{14}~{\rm GeV}$远高于大爆炸核合成（BBN）下限，且残余引力波谱可被BBO探测到。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: ACT DR6的最新观测将标量谱指数（scalar spectral index）$n_s$的偏好值上移，导致包括Starobinsky势在内的许多成熟暴涨模型（inflationary model）被排除在观测支持范围之外。然而Starobinsky势本身具有深厚的理论动机，源于$R^2$引力、无标度超引力（no-scale supergravity）以及$α$-吸引子（$α$-attractor）框架，因此有必要探索在不修改引力理论的前提下恢复其观测相容性的途径。

Method: 在k-本质（k-essence）框架下采用拉格朗日量$\mathcal{L} = F(φ)X - V(φ)$，其中动能耦合项设为幂律形式$F(φ) = 1+Aφ^n$。通过对背景方程（background equations）进行数值求解，计算得到$n_s$、谱指数跑动（running of the spectral index）$α_s$以及张量标量比（tensor-to-scalar ratio）$r$；同时利用Hamilton-Jacobi形式论（Hamilton-Jacobi formalism）和相空间分析（phase-space analysis）从解析和数值两方面验证解是否具有吸引子行为（attractor behavior）。对于再加热（reheating）阶段，利用Starobinsky势的特性计算有效状态方程参数$w_{\rm re}$和再加热温度$T_{\rm re}$，并计算残余引力波（relic gravitational wave）谱。

Result: 在耦合参数$A$和$n$的适当取值范围内，模型的$n_s$、$α_s$和$r$预测值落入ACT DR6的$1σ$置信区间内。暴涨解的吸引子行为得到Hamilton-Jacobi形式论和相空间分析的双重确认。再加热阶段的有效状态方程参数固定为$w_{\rm re}=0$，再加热温度$T_{\rm re} \sim 10^{14}~{\rm GeV}$远高于大爆炸核合成（big bang nucleosynthesis, BBN）的下限。残余引力波谱处于大爆炸观测台（big bang observer, BBO）的灵敏度界限内。

Conclusion: Starobinsky势在规范框架（canonical setting）下与ACT DR6不相容的问题，可以通过引入简单的非规范动能耦合（non-canonical kinetic coupling）在k-本质框架中得到解决，且无需对底层引力理论做任何修改。这表明Starobinsky势作为暴涨候选者的理论可行性依然成立。

Abstract: The recent ACT DR6 has shifted the preferred value of the scalar spectral index upward so that many well-established inflationary models have been disfavoured, including the Starobinsky potential. Despite this, the Starobinsky potential remains exceptionally well-motivated, with origins in $R^2$ gravity, no-scale supergravity, and the $α$-attractor framework. In this work, we show that the Starobinsky potential can be fully revived within a k-essence framework, described by the Lagrangian $\mathcal{L} = F(φ)X - V(φ)$, with a power-law kinetic coupling $F(φ) = 1+Aφ^n$ and no modification to the gravitational sector. Solving the background equations numerically, we find that the predictions for $n_s$, $α_s$, and $r$ fall within the $1σ$ region of ACT DR6 for a well-defined range of the coupling parameters. The attractor behavior of the inflationary solution is confirmed both analytically through the Hamilton-Jacobi formalism and numerically via a phase-space analysis. For the reheating phase, it is discussed that due to the nature of the Starobinsky potential, the effective equation of state parameter is fixed as $w_{\rm re} = 0$, resulting in a reheating temperature $T_{\rm re} \sim 10^{14}~{\rm GeV}$, well above the BBN bound. The relic gravitational wave spectrum is also computed and it is found that they can lie within the sensitivity bound of the BBO. These results demonstrate that the Starobinsky potential remains a theoretically viable candidate for inflation and that its incompatibility with ACT DR6 in the canonical setting can be resolved by introducing a simple non-canonical kinetic coupling without any modification to the underlying gravitational theory.

Additionally, variations in the scalar field amplitude and magnetic charge significantly affect both the intensity and spatial distribution of the polarization. ### [72] [Observationally Constrained Cosmological model in $f(Q,\mathcal{L}_{m})$ Gravity with $H(z)$ parameterization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06436)

Motivation: 在广义相对论（General Relativity）的替代理论框架中，$f(Q,\mathcal{L}_{m})$ 引力通过非度量性标量（non-metricity scalar）$Q$ 与物质拉格朗日密度（matter Lagrangian density）$\mathcal{L}_{m}$ 构建修正引力理论，旨在更一致地描述宇宙从减速膨胀到当前加速膨胀的演化过程。

Method: 采用平坦 FLRW 时空推导修正的弗里德曼场方程（modified Friedmann field equations），对哈勃参数 $H(z)$ 进行特定参数化描述宇宙演化；利用 Cosmic Chronometers (CC)、Pantheon+SH0ES、Union 3.0、DESI-BAO 和 CMB 距离先验（CMB distance priors）共五类观测数据集，通过马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（MCMC）方法基于 $\chi^2$ 最小化过程约束自由模型参数。

Result: 减速参数（deceleration parameter）在转变红移 $z_t \approx 0.643$ 处发生符号翻转，证实从物质主导减速到暗能量驱动加速的转变；状态方程（EOS）参数处于精质（quintessence）区域并在晚期渐近趋向 $\Lambda$CDM 极限；宇宙年龄估计为 $13.724^{+0.087}_{-0.048}$ Gyr；statefinder 和 Om 诊断支持模型的精质特性；零能量条件（NEC）和主导能量条件（DEC）满足，强能量条件（SEC）被违背。

Conclusion: 该 $f(Q,\mathcal{L}_{m})$ 引力模型与近期宇宙学观测一致，成功描述了宇宙从减速到加速的过渡，并且在能量条件检验中符合当前加速膨胀的要求，表明该框架是描述宇宙晚时演化的可行候选理论。

Abstract: In the present work, we explore an observationally constrained cosmological model in the framework of $f(Q,\mathcal{L}_{m})$ gravity, where $Q$ denotes the non-metricity scalar and $\mathcal{L}_{m}$ represents the matter Lagrangian density. To derive the modified Friedmann field equations, we consider a flat FLRW space-time. We have considered a specific parameterization of the Hubble parameter $H(z)$ to explore the cosmic evolution, which successfully describes the shift of the cosmos from its initial decelerated expansion period to the current accelerated scenario. The free model parameters are constrained using recent observational datasets including Cosmic Chronometers (CC), Pantheon+SH0ES, Union 3.0, DESI-BAO, and CMB distance priors using MCMC approach through the $χ^2$-minimization process. The derived results indicate that the present model remains consistent with recent cosmological observations. We note that the deceleration parameter exhibits a signature flipping behavior at transition redshift $z_t \approx 0.643$, confirming the transition from matter-dominated deceleration to dark-energy-driven acceleration. The equation of state (EOS) parameter remains in the quintessence region and exhibits an asymptotical approach to the $Λ$CDM limit at late times. Moreover, the estimated cosmic age can be found as $13.724^{+0.087}_{-0.048}$ Gyr, which agrees well with recent observational estimations. The statefinder and Om diagnostics support the quintessence nature of the model. At the same time, the examination of energy conditions reveals that two specific energy conditions, viz. Null Energy Condition (NEC) and Dominant Energy Condition (DEC) are fulfilled, while the Strong Energy Condition (SEC) is violated, validating the accelerated expansion of the universe.

</details>


### [73] [Starting inflation in asymptotically flat spacetimes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06441)
*Sam E. Brady,Thomas W. Baumgarte,Katy Clough*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文通过渐近平直时空（asymptotically flat spacetimes）下的模拟，验证并推广了Goldwirth & Piran的结论：成功触发暴胀需要尺度为暴胀尺度（inflationary scale）数倍的局域涨落（localised fluctuation），并指出周期性边界条件可能带来的偏差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 早期宇宙宇宙学的一个关键问题是，暴胀（inflation）能否由暴胀子场（inflaton field）中一个探测势能暴胀部分的、常见的局域涨落成功触发。此前模拟主要采用周期性时空（periodic spacetimes），这对外曲率（extrinsic curvature）和内曲率（intrinsic curvature）施加了限制性条件，可能不具备普遍性。

Method: 本研究在渐近平直时空中考虑初始涨落，从而允许更一般的内曲率与外曲率廓线（profile），以此放宽周期性边界条件带来的限制。

Result: 研究结果证实并推广了Goldwirth & Piran的结论：成功触发暴胀需要固有尺度（proper size）为暴胀尺度 $(Gρ_{\rm infl})^{-1/2}$ 数倍的涨落。

Conclusion: 讨论了初始数据（initial data）的内在限制，并指出将周期性长度（periodic length）设定为接近暴胀尺度可能会使结果产生偏差。

Abstract: A key question in early universe cosmology is whether inflation can be successfully seeded by a generic, localised fluctuation in the inflaton field that probes the inflationary part of the potential. Past simulations have mainly considered periodic spacetimes representing either a closed universe of a specific size or a typical patch of a larger one, and as a result have needed to impose restrictive conditions on the extrinsic and intrinsic curvatures, which are arguably not generic. In this work we consider initial fluctuations in asymptotically flat spacetimes, allowing more general profiles of the intrinsic and extrinsic curvature. Our findings confirm and generalise the result of Goldwirth and Piran that a fluctuation with proper size several times the inflationary scale $(Gρ_{\rm infl})^{-1/2}$ is required for successful inflation. We also discuss inherent restrictions on the initial data, and how imposing a periodic length close to the inflationary scale may bias results.
