### [113] [An Intermediate Scale R-axion \& the QCD Axion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06375)
*James Unwin*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该研究指出，中等尺度R-轴子（R-axion）原本面临Dine-Festuccia-Komargodski（DFK）约束导致的普朗克尺度下限，但通过混合F项与D项抬升（mixed F- and D-term uplift）构建有效理论，可在局域亚稳真空中规避该约束，将下限放松至$f_R \gtrsim \sqrt{m_{3/2}M_{\rm Pl}}$。若R对称性（R-symmetry）存在QCD反常（QCD anomaly），R-轴子可扮演QCD轴子（QCD axion）角色；在TeV尺度超对称（supersymmetry）下，$f_R\sim10^{11}$ GeV既能避免天体与宇宙学轴子约束，又能通过错位机制（misalignment mechanism）解释观测到的暗物质（dark matter）丰度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 中等尺度R-轴子受到Dine-Festuccia-Komargodski（DFK）约束的严重阻碍：在近闵可夫斯基（Minkowski）真空中，超势（superpotential）必须满足$2|\langle W\rangle|\leq f_R F$，这通常导致R-轴子衰变常数$f_R$被限制在普朗克尺度$M_{\rm Pl}$以上，使得该轴子难以在低能有效理论中实现。

Method: 通过在有效理论中引入混合F项与D项抬升（mixed F- and D-term uplift）来精细调节标量势（scalar potential）近似为零，从而在局域构建一个亚稳真空（metastable vacuum），在该真空中DFK论证给出的普朗克尺度$f_R$下限被局部规避。

Result: 有效场论（effective field theory）的有效性以及小$f_R$真空的亚稳性（metastability）共同导出一个放松的约束：$f_R \gtrsim \sqrt{m_{3/2}M_{\rm Pl}}$。在TeV尺度超对称（supersymmetry）下，$f_R\sim10^{11}$ GeV不仅避开了某些天体物理与宇宙学轴子约束，而且恰好处于可通过错位机制（misalignment mechanism）再现观测暗物质（dark matter）丰度的窗口内。

Conclusion: 中等尺度R-轴子可以在规避DFK约束的有效理论中实现，且若R对称性（R-symmetry）具有QCD反常（QCD anomaly），该R-轴子可同时充当QCD轴子（QCD axion）；在TeV超对称框架下，$f_R\sim10^{11}$ GeV能够同时满足理论自洽性与暗物质（dark matter）观测约束。

Abstract: An intermediate scale R-axion faces an immediate obstruction from the Dine-Festuccia-Komargodski (DFK) bound on the superpotential, $2|\langle W\rangle|\leq f_R F$, since for a nearly Minkowski vacuum it typically follows that $f_R\gtrsim M_{\rm Pl}$. We show that this lower bound on $f_R$ can be relaxed in an effective construction with the scalar potential tuned near zero via a mixed $F$- and $D$-term uplift, leading to a metastable vacuum in which the usual Planckian-$f_R$ inference from the DFK argument is avoided locally. Validity of the effective field theory and metastability of the small $f_R$ vacuum generically both imply a relaxed bound: $ f_R \gtrsim \sqrt{m_{3/2}M_{\rm Pl}} $. We also highlight that if the R-symmetry has a QCD anomaly, this potentially permits the R-axion to play the role of the QCD axion. TeV-scale supersymmetry permits $f_R\sim10^{11}$ GeV, this not only evades certain astrophysical and cosmological axion constraints, but notably lies in the window for which the observed dark matter abundance can be reproduced by the R-axion via the misalignment mechanism.

</details>


### [114] [Axioms for physical reasoning: codifying the Seiberg--Witten solution in Lean](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06379)
*Michael R. Douglas*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文提出使用交互式定理证明器（interactive theorem prover）来验证非严格的物理学论证，通过明确定义一组可检查的物理公设（physical postulates），并利用机器可验证的证明从中推导出物理结论。作者以 Lean 4 形式化了 N=2 SU(2) 超杨-米尔斯理论的 Seiberg–Witten 解（亏格一情形）作为案例，论证了该方法可作为验证理论物理中 AI 生成结果的有效标准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理论物理中的多数结果并非严格定理，而是依赖学界信任的非严格论证；对于四维杨-米尔斯理论等前沿问题，从第一原理出发进行严格证明目前遥不可及。因此，需要一种在缺乏严格证明的情况下仍能确保论证可靠性的形式化验证方法。

Method: 方法核心为：(1) 提出一组明确的、命名的物理公设作为出发点；(2) 使用交互式定理证明器（Lean 4）从中进行机器可检查的证明；(3) 下游结果可回溯其所依赖的具体假设；(4) 假设的外部检查方式包括同行评审和独立的数值"神谕"。作者以 Seiberg–Witten 解（亏格一情形）为例进行了形式化实现，高阶亏格 SU(N) 推广则以公理化骨架形式给出。

Result: 在 Lean 4 中成功形式化了 N=2 SU(2) 超杨-米尔斯理论的 Seiberg–Witten 解（亏格一情形），并开发了高阶亏格 SU(N) 推广的公理化骨架。论文厘清了该形式化过程中"哪些已证明、哪些已假设、假设如何被检查"的完整流程。

Conclusion: 该形式化方法提供了一种可被独立审查的学科规范：读者可以选择信任 Seiberg–Witten 数学本身，但仍可评估形式化方法的合理性。这一规范被认为可作为验证理论物理中 AI 生成结果的有效标准。

Abstract: Mathematicians have embraced interactive theorem provers with growing enthusiasm -- building large shared libraries and machine-checking a string of landmark results. Theoretical physics is different: most of its results are not theorems but justified by arguments the community trusts without a rigorous proof. For many -- the one we treat here among them -- no rigorous proof is within reach. For 4d Yang--Mills theory, deriving exact rigorous results from first principles would first require constructing the interacting theory nonperturbatively, which is a sizable piece of one of the Clay Millennium prize problems.
  We argue here that an interactive theorem prover can be used to verify some non-rigorous physics arguments. The method is to postulate a short list of explicit, named physical postulates, which imply the physical results by virtue of a machine-checkable proof. The trust that remains then rests on that short, inspectable list, and the prover can report, for any downstream result, exactly which assumptions it used. We carry this out for the Seiberg--Witten solution of ${N}=2$ $SU(2)$ super-Yang--Mills -- the genus-one case -- formalized in Lean 4; the higher-genus $SU(N)$ generalization is developed in the same repository as an axiomatized skeleton and left to future work. We describe what is proved, what is assumed, how the assumptions are checked -- external review and an independent numerical oracle -- and why this discipline is a sound standard for validating AI-generated results in theoretical physics. What we offer is a discipline, reviewable on its own terms: a reader may take the Seiberg--Witten mathematics on trust and still assess the formalization method.

</details>


### [115] [Unitary matrix models, quantized symmetric functions and spin chain](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06384)
*Gao-fu Ren*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文建立了酉矩阵模型（unitary matrix models）与量子自旋链希尔伯特空间（quantum spin-chain Hilbert spaces）中真空关联函数之间的对应关系。核心步骤是将对称函数（symmetric functions）提升为作用于N-磁子扇区（N-magnon sector）的算符，从而保持环结构。利用酉群积分的舒尔正交性（Schur orthogonality）将积分转化为量子化舒尔态（quantized Schur states）的内积，并以Gross–Witten–Wadia模型、N=4超杨-米尔斯理论（super Yang–Mills theory）的超共形指标（superconformal indices）以及Toda tau函数为例进行验证。该算符表述为酉矩阵积分、量子可积系统（quantum integrable systems）与对称函数理论之间提供了统一的代数桥梁。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在构建酉矩阵模型与量子自旋链系统之间的统一对应关系，弥合矩阵积分、量子可积系统与对称函数理论三个领域之间的方法论鸿沟，寻找代数上一致的联系机制。

Method: 将对称函数提升为作用于N-磁子扇区的算符，保持其环结构；利用舒尔正交性将酉群积分中的因子化展开转化为量子化舒尔态的内积，从而建立对应。

Result: 成功将Gross–Witten–Wadia模型、N=4超杨-米尔斯理论的超共形指标（含经典规范群情形）以及Toda tau函数统一纳入该算符框架，验证了构造的普适性。

Conclusion: 该算符表述为酉矩阵积分、量子可积系统与对称函数理论之间提供了统一的代数桥梁。

Abstract: We construct a correspondence between a broad class of unitary matrix models and vacuum correlation functions in quantum spin-chain Hilbert spaces. The key step is to lift symmetric functions to operators acting on the $N$-magnon sector in a way that preserves the relevant ring structure. For any unitary matrix model whose integrand admits a factorized expansion in symmetric functions, the Schur orthogonality of the unitary group integral is then translated into the inner product of quantized Schur states. We illustrate the construction for the Gross--Witten--Wadia model, superconformal indices of $\mathcal{N}=4$ super Yang--Mills theory with classical gauge groups, and Toda tau functions. The resulting operator formulation provides a unified algebraic bridge between unitary matrix integrals, quantum integrable systems and symmetric function theory.

### [116] [Abelian 2-Form Gauge Theory: Basic Canonical Brackets and Nilpotency Property of Noether (Anti-)BRST Charges](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06486)
*R. P. Malik*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在Becchi-Rouet-Stora-Tyutin（BRST）形式主义框架下，研究了D维自由阿贝尔2-形式规范理论中Noether（反）BRST荷的幂零性（nilpotency）与不变性。通过使用高斯散度定理和基本正则（反）对易子，证明标准Noether荷在离壳幂零（off-shell nilpotent）变换下并非不变且不离壳幂零，但通过引入运动方程和高斯散度定理可构造出修正的（反）BRST不变且幂零的守恒荷，后者在狄拉克量子化条件意义上具有优越性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在BRST形式主义中，Noether（反）BRST荷的幂零性和不变性是规范理论量子化的核心问题。本文旨在严格证明自由阿贝尔2-形式规范理论中这些荷的性质，并揭示标准Noether荷与修正荷之间的不一致性，进而统一离壳幂零变换下生成元的行为与狄拉克量子化条件的要求。

Method: 方法基于BRST形式主义框架，利用基本正则（反）对易子（basic canonical (anti)commutators）和高斯散度定理（Gauss divergence theorem），分析Noether（反）BRST荷在离壳幂零（off-shell nilpotent）对称变换下的行为，并引入Curci-Ferrari（CF）型约束（non-trivial Curci-Ferrari type restriction）。通过将运动方程（equations of motion）恰当地代入Noether荷表达式，构造了修正版本的（反）BRST不变荷。

Result: 标准Noether（反）BRST荷在离壳幂零变换下既不是不变的，也不是离壳幂零的；只有在引入运动方程和高斯散度定理后，这些荷才表现出（反）BRST不变性和幂零性。修正后的（反）BRST荷不仅在离壳幂零变换下不变，且利用基本正则（反）对易子也能证明其不变性。

Conclusion: 修正后的（反）BRST不变版本的Noether荷在物理性判据（physicality criteria）上优于标准Noether荷，能更好地满足狄拉克量子化条件（Dirac quantization conditions）对规范理论的一致性要求。该工作为带有CF型约束的BRST量子化理论提供了更自洽的生成元构造方案。

Abstract: Within the framework of Becchi-Rouet-Stora-Tyutin (BRST) formalism, we invoke the beauty of the basic canonical (anti)commutators to prove the nilpotency property of the Noether (anti-)BRST charges for the D-dimensional BRST-quantized version of the free Abelian 2-form gauge theory which is endowed with a non-trivial Curci-Ferrari (CF) type restriction. In this proof, we use only the theoretical strength of the Gauss divergence theorem. We demonstrate that, under the off-shell nilpotent (anti-)BRST symmetry transformations, the Noether conserved (anti-)BRST charges are not invariant and they are also found to be not off-shell nilpotent (if we exploit the standard relationship between the continuous symmetry transformations and their generators as the Noether conserved charges). However, these charges become (anti-)BRST invariant and nilpotent if we use (i) the appropriate equations of motion at suitable places, and (ii) the Gauss divergence theorem. We derive the consistently modified versions of the Noether (anti-)BRST charges which are invariant under the off-shell nilpotent (anti-)BRST transformations. We prove the (anti-)BRST invariance of these modified versions of charges by using the basic canonical (anti)commutators, too. We discuss the physicality criteria w.r.t. (i) the conserved Noether (anti-)BRST charges, and (ii) the modified (anti-)BRST invariant versions of the Noether (anti-)BRST charges. We prove the superiority of the latter over the former (in view of the consistency with the Dirac quantization conditions for the gauge theories).

### [117] [Holographic Tests of the $μ$ Ensemble](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06493)
*Nikolay Bobev,Fridrik Freyr Gautason,Jesse van Muiden*

TL;DR: 本文详细研究了M-理论中M2-膜量子化产生的可观测量在固定$A_3$系综（ensemble）中自然计算的理论，并在全息对偶框架下，通过对渐近AdS$_4$背景的11维引力理论进行导数展开和单圈对数修正的精确检验，验证了固定化学势$\mu$系综下的全息对偶关系，进而利用对数修正确定了拉普拉斯变换的测度，计算了对偶SCFT中的超共形指标（superconformal index）和挤压$S^3$配分函数（squashed $S^3$ partition function），结果与Airy函数（Airy function）形式的微扰$1/N$展开一致。

Method: 采用导数展开（derivative expansion）方法，聚焦11维理论前两项主导贡献；同时计算单圈对数修正（one-loop logarithmic corrections），并将其与对偶ABJM超共形场论（SCFT）中的超对称局域化（supersymmetric localisation）结果进行对比。

Conclusion: 本文为固定化学势系综下的全息对偶提供了精确检验，并展示了对数修正可用于确定积分变换测度，从而在微扰$1/N$展开中全阶计算对偶SCFT的超对称配分函数，拓宽了全息对偶的定量验证方法。

Abstract: We study in detail a recent proposal stating that M-theory observables arising from the quantisation of M2-branes are naturally computed in a fixed $A_3$ ensemble. In a holographic setting this implies that in a semiclassical approximation 11d bulk observables in an asymptotically AdS$_4$ background are computed in a grand canonical ensemble of fixed chemical potential $μ$ conjugate to the integer $N$ determining the rank of the gauge group in the dual CFT. We provide detailed precision tests of holography in the fixed $μ$ ensemble by focusing on the two leading terms in the derivative expansion of the 11d theory. In addition, we study one-loop logarithmic corrections which we compute in detail. For asymptotically AdS$_4\times S^7/\mathbf{Z}_k$ 11d backgrounds our results are in agreement with supersymmetric localisation calculations in the dual ABJM SCFT. Moreover, we employ the logarithmic corrections in the $μ$ ensemble to determine the measure of the integral Laplace transform and use this to compute dual SCFT supersymmetric partition functions, like the superconformal index and the squashed $S^3$ partition function, to all orders in the perturbative $1/N$ expansion in terms of Airy functions in harmony with results and conjectures in the dual SCFT.

### [119] [The Chiral Random-Matrix Ensemble of the Type-IIB Axion--Dilaton Wormhole Partition Function](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06566)
*Soo-Jong Rey*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文构建了IIB型弦理论中轴子-膨胀子虫洞配分函数中约化电荷区系数$W_ν[b]$的微观ADHM/手征Wishart代表，证明了该系数在BPS瞬子端点处的物理二次涨落算符等价于一个正伴随平方，其非零谱为平方奇异值谱，微观端点为Laguerre/手征硬边，且超ADHM集体坐标积分在大$N$极限下退化为$AdS_5\times S^5$上的$k$-D-瞬子测度与零维超对称矩阵模型因子的乘积。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论文试图从微观（microscopic）层面构造并分析IIB型弦理论中轴子-膨胀子（axion-dilaton）虫洞（wormhole）配分函数中的约化电荷区系数$W_ν[b]$，以理解其与超ADHM构造、手征Wishart系综以及超对称矩阵模型之间的结构对应关系。

Method: 作者将轴子-电荷区固定为与QCD中固定拓扑区（fixed-topology sector）结构相同的域，在该域内先计算微观系数再进行最终的$\theta$求和；在BPS瞬子端点$E=0$处施加哈密顿约束（Hamiltonian constraint）、规范商化（gauge quotient）、电荷区边界条件和集体零模商化（collective zero-mode quotient）后，得到物理二次涨落算符为正伴随平方（positive adjoint square），其非零谱为平方奇异值谱（squared singular-value spectrum），微观端点为Laguerre/手征硬边（chiral hard edge）；进而利用D(-1)/D3超ADHM集体坐标积分作为该系数的微观代表。

Result: 在Dorey等人的大$N$极限下，超ADHM测度退化为$AdS_5\times S^5$上的$k$-D-瞬子测度乘以中心化零维超对称矩阵模型因子（centered zero-dimensional supersymmetric matrix-model factor）；手征/Wishart系综（chiral/Wishart ensemble）构成了该超ADHM积分中矩形块（rectangular block）的硬边极限（hard-edge limit）。费米型ADHM变量和超引力费米子以配对的非零模抵消（paired non-zero mode cancellation）和零模饱和（zero-mode saturation）形式参与系数，并决定了哪些约化数据$b$给出非零的$W_ν[b]$。

Conclusion: 本文成功建立了虫洞配分函数中约化电荷区系数与超ADHM构造、手征Wishart系综及超对称矩阵模型之间的精确微观对应关系，揭示了该系数在BPS端点处的谱结构具有手征硬边特征，并明确了费米变量在决定系数非零条件中的关键作用。

Abstract: I construct a microscopic ADHM/chiral-Wishart representative of the reduced charge-sector coefficient $W_ν[b]$ that enters the Type-IIB axion--dilaton wormhole partition function $Z_{\rm wh}(θ;b)$. I fix the axion-charge sector, equivalently the form-field-flux sector, which plays the exact same structural role as a fixed-topology sector in QCD: it supplies the domain where I compute the microscopic coefficient before forming the final theta sum. At $E=0$, the axion--dilaton radial family reaches its BPS instanton endpoint. After I impose the Hamiltonian constraint, gauge quotient, charge-sector boundary condition, and collective zero-mode quotient, the physical quadratic fluctuation operator at that endpoint becomes a positive adjoint square. Its non-zero spectrum is therefore a squared singular-value spectrum, and its microscopic endpoint is a Laguerre/chiral hard edge. The D(-1)/D3 super-ADHM collective-coordinate integral supplies the Type-IIB microscopic representative of this same coefficient. In the large$N$ result of Dorey et al., this super-ADHM measure becomes the $k$-D-instanton measure on $AdS_5\times S^5$, multiplied by a centered zero-dimensional supersymmetric matrix-model factor. The chiral/Wishart ensemble forms the hard-edge limit of the rectangular block inside this super-ADHM integral. Fermionic ADHM variables and supergravity fermions remain part of the coefficient: in protected sectors they cancel paired non-zero modes, impose zero-mode saturation, and determine which reduction data \(b\) give a non-vanishing $W_ν[b]$.

</details>

### [120] [On low-rank tensor train approximability for linear nearest neighbor systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06453)
*Patrick Gelß,Sebastian Matera,Reinhold Schneider,André Uschmajew*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 本文研究了低秩张量方法在高维最近邻相互作用系统（如Ising模型、马尔可夫跳跃过程和一维有限态量子系统）中的理论合理性。通过将Arad等人关于一维自旋系统基态面积律（area laws）中局部算子的部分交换性技术，推广到具有最近邻结构的定常线性方程和耗散线性常微分方程的多项式求解方法中，推导出与系统大小无关的低秩可逼近性结论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 低秩张量列车/矩阵乘积态（low-rank tensor train/matrix product state）模型在模拟高维最近邻相互作用系统时表现出极高的效率，但为其提供理论证明仍然是一个挑战。一种获得所需秩估计的方法是通过研究Krylov子空间方法（Krylov subspace methods）中的秩增长特性；本文旨在沿着这一方向给出严格的低秩可逼近性保证。

Method: 本文将Arad等人[arXiv:1301.1162]在研究一维自旋系统基态面积律时，利用最近邻算子多项式（nearest neighbor operator polynomials）的局部算子部分交换性（partial commutativity）来证明秩增长性质的技术，推广至定常线性方程和耗散线性常微分方程（dissipative linear ODEs）的多项式求解方法中，这些方程均具有最近邻结构。

Result: 推导出与系统大小无关的低秩可逼近性（low-rank approximability）结论，并通过高维最近邻系统的数值模拟验证了理论结果。

Conclusion: 本文所发展的技术为最近邻结构下线性方程和耗散线性常微分方程的解提供了系统大小无关的低秩可逼近性保证，从而为低秩张量方法在相关高维问题中的有效性提供了理论支撑。

Abstract: Low-rank tensor methods are an important tool in the numerical treatment of equations with a high-dimensional state space. Nearest neighbor interaction systems like the Ising model or more general Markov jump processes, as well as 1D finite-state quantum systems are examples of such problems. While low-rank tensor train/matrix product state models have been shown to be highly efficient for the simulation of such systems, providing theoretical justification for this remains a challenging task. One approach for obtaining estimates on required ranks for certain accuracies is to investigate the rank increase in Krylov subspace methods for solving the problem at hand. In the context of area laws for ground states of 1D spin systems, nontrivial results on rank-increasing properties of nearest neighbor operator polynomials have been obtained in work of Arad et al. [arXiv:1301.1162] by studying the partial commutativity of local operators. In the present work, this technique is applied to polynomial methods for definite linear equations and dissipative linear ODEs with nearest neighbor structure. This allows to derive corresponding low-rank approximability statements for solutions of such problems which are independent of the system size. Numerical simulations of high-dimensional nearest neighbor systems illustrate the theoretical findings.

</details>

### [121] [Spontaneous emission of light by non-equilibrium phonons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06399)
*J. Plo,P. Valvin,M. Moret,T. Taliercio,J. Batista,T. Sohier,A. Vasanelli,C. Sirtori,B. Gil,W. Desrat,G. Cassabois*

Main category: cond-mat.other

TL;DR: 本论文通过实验发现，在非平衡态下，声子（phonon）可以通过自发辐射（spontaneous emission）光子直接退激，这是一种与固有的非谐衰减（anharmonic decay）相竞争的有效辐射弛豫通道（radiative relaxation pathway），从而挑战了此前认为弛豫早期阶段完全是非辐射的假设。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统观点认为，系统受外部激发脱离平衡态后，弛豫至热平衡的早期阶段——即声子通过级联非谐衰减过程最终形成玻色-爱因斯坦分布（Bose-Einstein distribution）的初始热化阶段——完全是非辐射的，在热对流、热传导和热辐射（incandescence）之前发生。本文旨在检验这一假设是否成立。

Method: 采用飞秒双光子激发（femtosecond two-photon excitation）光谱技术，对氮化硼（boron nitride）材料进行光学激发，并在中红外（mid-infrared）光谱范围内测量其光致发光（photoluminescence, PL）信号。

Result: 实验观测到一个源于非平衡声子自发辐射的中红外光致发光信号，表明声子可以直接辐射光子，且该辐射弛豫过程的效率足以与非谐衰减相竞争。

Conclusion: 声子的非热辐射（non-thermal radiation）现象的发现，为非平衡态物理学（out-of-equilibrium physics）、中红外光学（mid-infrared optics）和热管理（thermal management）领域引入了新的范式。

Abstract: When a system is brought out of equilibrium by an external excitation, its relaxation to thermodynamic equilibrium generates phonons. These non-equilibrium phonons degrade via cascaded anharmonic decay processes, progressively leading to a thermal population of phonons following a Bose-Einstein distribution at the system temperature. Preceding heat dissipation by convection, conduction and incandescence, this early phase of the relaxation dynamics is commonly assumed to be exclusively non-radiative. Here, we demonstrate that the radiative emission by phonons can be an efficient relaxation pathway competing with the intrinsic anharmonic decay. Optical spectroscopy under femtosecond two-photon excitation in boron nitride unveils a photoluminescence signal in the mid-infrared spectral range, stemming from the spontaneous emission of light by non-equilibrium phonons. This observation of non-thermal radiation from phonons introduces a new paradigm for out-of-equilibrium physics, mid-infrared optics, and thermal management.

</details>

TL;DR: 本文报道了NA61/SHINE合作组在CERN超级质子同步加速器上对中心碰撞40Ar+45Sc系统中K*(892)0共振态产生的首次测量，利用K*(892)0与带电K介子产额比来估算化学冻结（chemical freeze-out）与动力学冻结（kinetic freeze-out）之间的时间间隔。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 分析奇异K*(892)0共振态的产生有助于理解高能核-核碰撞的时间演化，尤其是通过测量K*(892)0与带电K介子产额比来确定化学冻结与动力学冻结之间的时间间隔。

Method: 实验由NA61/SHINE合作组在CERN超级质子同步加速器（Super Proton Synchrotron）上开展，测量了中心40Ar+45Sc碰撞中K*(892)0共振态的产生，质心系对撞能量为sqrt(s_NN) = 8.8, 11.9, 16.8 GeV；通过对比p+p碰撞结果估计化学冻结与热冻结（thermal freeze-out）的时间间隔。

Result: 获得了K*(892)0与K+及K−的平均多重数比值〈K*(892)0〉/〈K+〉和〈K*(892)0〉/〈K−〉，并与p+p碰撞的相应结果进行了比较，这是40Ar+45Sc碰撞体系中关于该时间间隔的首个测量结果。

Conclusion: K*(892)0共振态测量可用于约束化学冻结与动力学冻结之间的时间间隔，为理解高能核-核碰撞系统的演化动力学提供了新信息。

Abstract: The analysis of the production of strange $K^{*}(892)^0$ resonances allows us to better understand the temporal evolution of high-energy nucleus--nucleus collisions. In particular, the ratio of $K^{*}(892)^0$ to charged kaon yields is used to determine the time interval between chemical and kinetic freeze-outs. In this paper, the first measurements of $K^{*}(892)^0$ production in central $^{40}$Ar+$^{45}$Sc collisions at the CERN Super Proton Synchrotron are reported. They were performed by NA61/SHINE at collision center-of-mass energies per nucleon pair $\sqrt{s_\mathrm{NN}}$ = 8.8, 11.9, 16.8 GeV.
  The obtained $\langle K^{*}(892)^0 \rangle/\langle K^{+} \rangle $ and $\langle K^{*}(892)^0 \rangle/\langle K^{-} \rangle$ mean multiplicity ratios are compared with corresponding results in $p$+$p$ collisions, allowing for an estimate of the time interval between chemical and thermal freeze-outs in the $^{40}$Ar+$^{45}$Sc system. These are the first such results reported for $^{40}$Ar+$^{45}$Sc collisions.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 质子的自旋结构远比最初预期的复杂，早期$g_1$测量表明质子自旋并非仅来源于夸克的自旋，引发了“质子自旋危机”（proton spin crisis）。目前尚缺乏在同一运动学条件下同时使用纵向极化靶和横向极化靶测量质子结构函数的已发表低动量转移（low momentum transfer）实验数据。

Method: 利用杰斐逊实验室E08-027实验的纵向极化靶数据，并结合同一实验中先前发表的横向极化靶数据，生成联合矩（linked moments）进行分析。

Result: 获得了共振区（resonance region）内极高精度的质子$g_1$结构函数提取结果，并提供了依赖于$g_1$的和规则（sum rules）及矩（moments）的新信息。

Conclusion: 这些高精度测量结果为检验手征微扰理论和量子色动力学提供了重要的实验依据，增进了对质子自旋结构的理解。

Abstract: The proton's spin structure has proven to be far more complicated than was originally believed, and has been the subject of a number of experimental investigations. %Early measurements of the proton's spin structure function $g_1$ showed that the proton does not solely derive its spin from the spins of its quarks, starting the `proton spin crisis'. Of particular interest are the spin structure functions $g_1$ and $g_2$, which can be used to generate moments to directly compare experimental results to Chiral Perturbation Theory and other theories of Quantum Chromodynamics (QCD). The proton's $g_1$ structure function has been the subject of two other recent low momentum transfer experiments, but there are currently no published low momentum transfer measurements which collected data on the proton structure functions using both a longitudinally-polarized and a transversely-polarized target at the same kinematics. In this paper, we present the longitudinally polarized results of the Jefferson Lab E08-027 experiment, along with linked moments which combine this new result with the previously published transversely-polarized data from the same experiment. These results provide a proton $g_1$ extraction measured with very high precision across the resonance region, and provide new information on the value of $g_1$ dependent sum rules and moments.

### [124] [Autoencoder-Based Unsupervised Identification of Nonequilibrium Phases in Sheared Binary Colloids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05860)
*Yoshitaka Miyahara,Taiki Haga*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于无监督机器学习（unsupervised machine learning）的框架，通过整合傅里叶预处理（Fourier-based preprocessing）、自编码器（autoencoder）和高斯混合模型（Gaussian mixture model, GMM），对粒子系统中的非平衡相（nonequilibrium phases）进行分类，并在剪切流下二元带电胶体系统中验证了其有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 识别粒子系统中的非平衡相面临重大挑战，因为这些相通常呈现复杂且空间异质的结构，缺乏长程有序（long-range order）。

Method: 该框架首先将全局空间构型变换到傅里叶空间（Fourier space），以傅里叶系数振幅作为自编码器的输入，从而抑制空间噪声并保留相特异性结构特征；随后使用高斯混合模型对自编码器生成的潜空间（latent space）中的聚类进行鲁棒识别。

Result: 在稳态剪切流下的二元带电胶体系统中，潜空间呈现出分离良好的聚类，基于聚类隶属概率构建的非平衡相图与通过径向分布函数分析和无监督异常检测独立获得的相边界一致。

Conclusion: 基于自编码器的无监督学习为识别复杂粒子系统中的非平衡相提供了一种有效框架。

Abstract: Identifying nonequilibrium phases in particle systems remains a major challenge because they often exhibit complex and spatially heterogeneous structures without long-range order. Here, we develop an unsupervised machine-learning framework for classifying such nonequilibrium phases by integrating Fourier-based preprocessing, an autoencoder, and a Gaussian mixture model (GMM). Specifically, we transform global spatial configurations into Fourier space and use the amplitudes of Fourier coefficients as inputs to the autoencoder. This preprocessing suppresses spatial noise while preserving phase-specific structural features and physical interpretability. We demonstrate the effectiveness of this framework using a binary charged colloidal system under steady shear flow, where the competition between Coulomb interactions and shear gives rise to three nonequilibrium phases characterized by distinct local structures. The encoded latent space reveals well-separated clusters that are robustly identified by the GMM, enabling the construction of a nonequilibrium phase diagram based on cluster membership probabilities. The resulting phase boundaries are consistent with those independently obtained from radial distribution function analysis and unsupervised anomaly detection. These results demonstrate that autoencoder-based unsupervised learning provides an effective framework for identifying nonequilibrium phases in complex particle systems.

</details>


### [125] [Electron-Phonon Dephasing in Ultrathin Disordered Films: From Power Laws to Diagnostic Maps](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05951)
*Eugeniy Yu. Beliayev*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文论证了超薄无序金属膜中电子-声子退相位（electron-phonon dephasing）的幂律指数并非普适材料常数，而是一个交叉（crossover）可观测量，其值取决于清洁-无序参数、声子约束、薄膜-衬底声学耦合以及无序的微观特性，并基于Ar离子辐照Au膜的受控无序实验提供了诊断图谱。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超薄无序金属膜中电子-声子退相位常被总结为幂律$τ_{e-ph}^{-1}=AT^p$，但实际薄膜表现出接近2、3、4以及中间非普适（nonuniversal）的有效指数，现有理论无法统一解释。

Method: 提出将指数视为交叉可观测量，需要清洁-无序参数$q_T l$、声子约束、薄膜-衬底声学耦合以及无序微观特性等多个坐标来解释；并以Ar离子辐照Au膜作为受控无序系列进行实验验证。

Result: 在Ar离子辐照Au膜中，拟合的电子-声子指数在低纯脏交叉温度$T_{tr}\simeq \hbar s/(k_B l)$时保持$p\simeq 2$，随无序增加增大至$p\simeq 2.8$；前因子（prefactor）趋势表明平均自由程减小抑制了电子-声子散射，符合脏极限（dirty-limit）减弱而非静态无序增强。

Conclusion: $p<4$的持续性指向薄膜或薄膜-衬底声子效应；所建立的诊断图谱为比较超薄无序膜中的电子-声子退相位数据提供了紧凑的框架。

Abstract: Electron-phonon dephasing in ultrathin disordered metallic films is often summarized by a power law, $τ_{e-ph}^{-1}=AT^p$. However, thin metals, alloys, and superconducting films exhibit effective exponents close to 2, 3, and 4, as well as intermediate nonuniversal values. We argue that in ultrathin supported films, the exponent should be treated not as a universal material constant, but as a crossover observable. Its interpretation requires several coordinates: the clean-to-dirty parameter $q_T l$, phonon confinement and film-substrate acoustic coupling, and the microscopic character of disorder.
  The diagnostic picture is illustrated using Ar-ion-irradiated Au films as a controlled-disorder series. In these films, the fitted electron-phonon exponent remains near $p\simeq 2$ for low values of the pure-dirty crossover temperature $T_{tr}\simeq \hbar s/(k_B l)$ and increases toward $p\simeq 2.8$ as disorder increases. At the same time, the prefactor trend indicates suppression of electron-phonon scattering with decreasing mean free path, consistent with dirty-limit weakening rather than static-disorder enhancement. The persistence of $p<4$ points to the role of thin-film or film-substrate phonon effects. The resulting diagnostic map provides a compact framework for comparing electron-phonon dephasing data in ultrathin disordered films.

</details>

### [126] [Three-point density correlations in a weakly interacting 2D Fermi liquid](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05747)
*C. L. Kane*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本论文研究了弱相互作用自旋1/2费米气体中密度的三点等时关联函数，给出了总密度三点函数到相互作用参数一阶的精确动量依赖结果，以及长波共线极限下同自旋三点函数的三阶领头阶相互作用修正，这些结果与当前原子费米气体的量子气体显微镜实验直接相关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在弱相互作用自旋1/2费米气体（weakly interacting spin-1/2 Fermi gas）中，密度三点等时关联函数（three-point equal-time correlation）是理解多体关联的重要物理量。此前仅已知长波共线极限下三点函数与朗道费米液体参数（Landau Fermi liquid parameters）的关系，缺乏更一般的动量依赖结果及更高阶相互作用修正，这限制了与量子气体显微镜实验的定量比较。

Method: 论文采用微扰论方法，以无量纲相互作用参数 $\mathcal{I}$ 为展开小量，分别计算了总密度 $\rho = \rho_\uparrow + \rho_\downarrow$ 的三点关联函数到 $\mathcal{O}(\mathcal{I})$ 阶的精确动量依赖表达式，以及同自旋三点关联函数在长波共线极限（long-wavelength collinear limit）下的 $\mathcal{O}(\mathcal{I}^3)$ 领头阶相互作用修正。

Result: 得到了两个主要结果：一是总密度三点函数到 $\mathcal{O}(\mathcal{I})$ 阶的完整动量依赖形式，推广了此前仅限于长波共线极限且与朗道参数 $F_0^s$ 和 $F_0^a$ 关联的结果；二是同自旋三点函数在长波共线极限下 $\mathcal{O}(\mathcal{I}^3)$ 阶的领头阶修正项。

Conclusion: 这些理论结果直接适用于当前利用量子气体显微镜（quantum gas microscopy）对原子费米气体进行的实验观测，有望为高精度测量多体关联提供理论支撑。

Abstract: We study the three-point equal-time correlations of the density in a weakly interacting spin 1/2 Fermi gas and present two new results. First, we compute the three-point correlation for the total density $ρ= ρ_\uparrow + ρ_\downarrow$ exactly as a function of momentum to first order in a dimensionless interaction parameter ${\cal I}$. This generalizes a previous result that related the three-point function to the Landau Fermi liquid parameters $F_0^s$ and $F_0^a$ and applied in a certain long-wavelength collinear limit. Second, we compute the leading order ${\cal O}({\cal I}^3)$ interaction correction to the same-spin three-point correlation function in the long-wavelength collinear limit. These results are directly relevant to current experiments on atomic Fermi gases using quantum gas microscopy.

</details>

Conclusion: 磁振子激发导致的动态散射是隧穿谱发生重要修正的关键机制，磁振子边带是该修正的明显特征。

Abstract: The surface tunnelling spectrum of a dual system consisting of localised moments with antiferromagnetic order coupled to conduction electrons by on-site exchange interaction is investigated. In this work we consider dynamic effects by including the scattering of conduction electrons from the local moment magnon excitations. Abstract: We have investigated the electronic structure of LaSr$_2$Mn$_2$O$_7$ in the CE-type antiferromagnetic (CE-AFM) state below the Néel temperature using micro-focused angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy ($μ$-ARPES) and tight-binding models. Many observed features can be explained by the CE-AFM tight-binding bands, although some of them and the overall near-Fermi level intensity mapping can be explained by the A-AFM band structure. This indicates that the CE-AFM domain size would be no larger than the beam footprint size of a $\sim\!20$~{\textmu}m scale.

### [129] [Bose Einstein Condensation of Magnons in BaCuSi$_{2}$O$_{6}$: An experimental perspective](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06028)

Result: 在零场或小磁场下，BaCuSi₂O₆ 表现为量子顺磁体（quantum paramagnet）。在 23–49 T（约地球磁场的一百万倍）的高磁场与亚液氦低温条件下，该材料发生磁有序（magnetic ordering），进入近乎理想的易平面（XY）反铁磁态（easy-plane antiferromagnetic state），被解释为磁振子玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（Bose-Einstein condensate of magnons）。

Conclusion: BaCuSi₂O₆ 在实验可及的磁场范围（23–49 T）内为研究量子多体物理学（quantum many-body physics）的理论预言提供了一个极佳的实验平台。

Abstract: Han Purple, a pigment first obtained in ancient China, is one of the earliest known synthetic pigments. Also naturally occurring, as a mineral, it is known as colinowensite (Cwn). Its chemical formula is BaCuSi$_{2}$O$_{6}$, and its structure is a layered cyclosilicate in which magnetic Cu$^{2+}$ ions (S = 1/2) form dimers arranged on a square lattice, making it also the first known synthetic metal dimer compound. Most interesting magnetic properties arise from a strong intradimer spin coupling, accompanied by weaker interdimer interactions within and between Cu-dimer layers. In zero or small magnetic fields, BaCuSi$_{2}$O$_{6}$ remains a quantum paramagnet. However, under high magnetic fields between 23 and 49 Tesla -- about a million times stronger than Earth's magnetic field -- it undergoes magnetic ordering at subliquid Helium temperatures into an almost ideal easy-plane (XY) antiferromagnetic state regarded as a realization of a Bose-Einstein condensate of magnons. Within this experimentally accessible field range, BaCuSi$_{2}$O$_{6}$ serves as an extraordinary playground for testing predictions of quantum many-body physics.

### [130] [Weak-coupling altermagnetism and chiral magnetic excitations in a checkerboard lattice](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06106)
*Abhigya Rangari,Manna Paul,Sayandip Ghosh*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过最小单带哈伯德模型在棋盘格晶格上展示了交变磁性（altermagnetism）的实现，并利用平均场和随机相位近似分析了其相变与磁激发特性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 交变磁体（altermagnets）作为一类具有自旋分裂电子能带但净磁矩为零的新型磁性材料，近年来受到广泛关注，但其微观机制与激发特性尚需深入研究。

Method: 采用最小单带哈伯德模型（one-band Hubbard model）描述棋盘格晶格上的电子；通过弱耦合下的交变磁化率发散判定失稳条件；使用平均场（mean-field）处理哈伯德排斥项，分析相变；利用随机相位近似（random-phase approximation, RPA）处理动力学自旋磁化率，研究磁激发。

Result: 棋盘格晶格在弱耦合下出现交变磁化率发散，表明交变磁序失稳。平均场计算显示从非磁性到交变磁半金属（altermagnetic semimetal）再到交变磁绝缘体（altermagnetic insulating phase）的相变，清晰识别出自旋分裂态。RPA分析表明交变磁序对自旋涨落稳定，激发谱呈现良好定义的磁振子（magnon）激发，随相互作用减弱磁振子衰变为单粒子激发。磁激发表现出强烈的手性（chirality）和方向依赖，呈现交替手性分裂（alternating chirality splitting），与电子能带的交替自旋分裂类似。

Conclusion: 棋盘格晶格是交变磁性的天然平台，交变磁序在弱耦合下稳定，其磁激发中的交替手性分裂是交变磁性的显著特征。

Abstract: Altermagnets, characterized by spin-split electronic bands with compensated magnetic moments, have emerged as a new class of magnetic materials garnering attention in recent years. Here, using a minimal one-band Hubbard model, we show that the checkerboard lattice serves as a natural platform for altermagnetism for electrons. The instability towards altermagnetic order is denoted by diverging altermagnetic susceptibility at weak-coupling. Carrying out mean-field treatment of the Hubbard repulsion, we show phase transitions from the nonmagnetic to altermagnetic semimetal and then to altermagnetic insulating phase, allowing clear identification of spin-split states. We then examine magnetic excitations in the altermagnetic phases using a random-phase approximation treatment of the dynamical spin susceptibility. The altermagnetic order is found to be stable against spin-fluctuations with the excitation spectra showing well-defined magnon excitations, which decay into single-particle excitations with decreasing interaction strength. Remarkably, the magnetic excitations exhibit strong dependence on both chirality and direction, showing an alternating chirality splitting, similar to the alternating spin splitting of the electronic bands, which serves as a salient feature of altermagnetism.

### [131] [Bockstein Braiding Statistics Versus Three-Loop Braiding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06279)
*Hanyu Xue*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该论文发现了一种新型统计过程 $W_N(X,Y)=(Y^{-1}X^{-1})^N(YX)^N$，用于描述 $p+q+1$ 维空间中两个 $N$ 阶拓扑激发之间的统计，该统计能够检测 Bockstein 响应 $A\smile β(B)$。研究进一步指出，三维空间中的环路统计（loop statistics）由阿贝尔群（Abelian group）$G$ 的融合规则（fusion rules）分类，对应 $H^5(B^2G,U(1))$，而传统的三环编织（three-loop braiding）超出该分类，因此必须具有非阿贝尔融合规则（non-Abelian fusion rules）。论文建议将三环编织视为粒子-环路编织（particle-loop braiding）与环路和点缺陷之间奇异融合规则的组合，并尝试阐明统计与对称性反常（symmetry anomaly）之间的关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统上，$p$ 维和 $q$ 维拓扑激发（topological excitations）的编织统计（braiding statistics）定义在 $p+q+2$ 维空间中。该研究旨在探索 $p+q+1$ 维空间中高阶拓扑激发之间的新型统计过程，并澄清当前分类框架（如三维环路统计分类）与已知现象（如三环编织）之间的不一致性。

Method: 通过数学构造，提出了一个新的统计过程 $W_N(X,Y)=(Y^{-1}X^{-1})^N(YX)^N$，用于描述 $p+q+1$ 维空间中两个 $N$ 阶激发之间的统计，该过程可检测 Bockstein 响应 $A\smile β(B)$。同时结合上同调分类（cohomology classification）$H^5(B^2G,U(1))$ 对三维环路统计进行系统分类，并对比传统三环编织行为。

Result: 三维空间中所有融合规则构成阿贝尔群 $G$ 的环路统计由 $H^5(B^2G,U(1))$ 完全分类。然而，传统的三环编织行为超出了该分类框架，表明三环编织必然具有非阿贝尔融合规则。此外，新发现的统计过程 $W_N$ 与费米子环路统计（fermionic loop statistics）共同穷尽了三维空间中所有可能的环路统计。

Conclusion: 论文建议将三环编织重新解释为粒子-环路编织与环路和点缺陷之间奇异融合规则的结合。同时，研究还尝试阐明拓扑激发统计与对称性反常之间的内在联系。

Abstract: Braiding statistics of $p$- and $q$-dimensional topological excitations is conventionally defined in $p+q+2$ spatial dimensions. We find a novel statistical process $W_N(X,Y)=(Y^{-1}X^{-1})^N(YX)^N$ for two order-$N$ excitations in $p+q+1$ dimensions, detecting the Bockstein response $A\smile β(B)$. This new statistics and fermionic loop statistics exhaust all loop statistics in three dimensions whose fusion rules form an Abelian group $G$, classified by $H^5(B^2G,U(1))$. Surprisingly, conventional three-loop braiding goes beyond this classification, so it must have non-Abelian fusion rules. We suggest viewing three-loop braiding as particle-loop braiding together with exotic fusion rules between loops and point-like defects. We also try to clarify the relationship between statistics and symmetry anomaly.

</details>


### [132] [Skyrmion Phase Control by Magnetic Dipole-Dipole Interaction and Electric Field in Centrosymmetric Materials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06419)
*Raz Rivlis,Alexander Petrović,Yuri Dahnovsky*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了三角晶格中心对称斯格明子（skyrmion）材料中磁偶极-偶极相互作用（dipole-dipole interaction）、外电场及磁场对斯格明子螺旋性（helicity）与空间构型的调控机制，发现偶极相互作用偏好布洛赫型（Bloch）螺旋性，零磁场下的斯格明子相以及无Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya相互作用（DMI）下的meron/antimeron晶格相，同时外电场可连续调控螺旋性，为斯格明子量子比特（qubit）应用提供潜在控制手段。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实现对磁性斯格明子（magnetic skyrmion）螺旋性（helicity）和空间构型的精确控制，是利用其在经典、模拟及量子计算应用中潜力的关键前提。

Method: 在三角晶格中心对称斯格明子宿主（triangular lattice centrosymmetric skyrmion host）中，系统考察了磁偶极-偶极相互作用（dipole-dipole interaction）、外电场和外磁场对该材料中斯格明子螺旋性及空间构型的控制作用。

Result: 偶极-偶极相互作用强烈偏好布洛赫螺旋性（Bloch helicity）；提高偶极耦合强度时可出现零磁场斯格明子相；在无Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya相互作用（DMI）条件下观察到了meron/antimeron晶格相；外电场可稳定高密度奈尔型斯格明子晶体（Néel skyrmion crystals）；偶极相互作用与外电场的共同作用可导致两种斯格明子类型之间的连续转变，而非突变。

Conclusion: 外电场可作为斯格明子螺旋性的连续调谐机制（continuous tuning mechanism），进而为斯格明子量子比特（skyrmion qubit）中的两能级系统（two-level system）提供有效控制手段。

Abstract: Establishing precise control over the helicity and spatial configuration of magnetic skyrmions will be essential to realize their promise in classical, analog and quantum computation applications. In this work, we explore the role of magnetic dipole-dipole interactions, external electric fields, and magnetic fields in controlling these parameters within a triangular lattice centrosymmetric skyrmion host. We demonstrate that dipole-dipole interactions strongly favor Bloch helicity. Notably, a zero magnetic field skyrmion phase appears upon raising the dipole-dipole coupling strength, with substantial potential for cost-effective quantum device applications. We also report the emergence of a meron/antimeron lattice phase, in the absence of any Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya interaction. In contrast, applied electric fields stabilize high density Néel skyrmion crystals. The interplay between dipole-dipole interactions and external electric fields creates a continuous transition between the two skyrmion types, rather than an abrupt switch. Applied electric fields can therefore be used as a continuous tuning mechanism for skyrmion helicity, and hence a control handle for tuning two-level systems in skyrmion qubits.

### [133] [Instabilities of Fermi Liquids with Arbitrary Forward Scattering: Exact Approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06430)
*Dmitry Miserev,Joel Hutchinson,Herbert Schoeller,Jelena Klinovaja,Daniel Loss*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文基于维度约化（dimensional reduction）方法，将具有球对称费米面（spherical Fermi surface）和前向散射密度-密度相互作用（forward-scattering density-density interaction）的D维简并电子气映射到一维可玻色化（bosonizable）理论，精确计算了有限程相互作用下的费米子格林函数（fermion Green function）、配对/电荷/味磁化率（pair and charge/flavor susceptibilities）以及复合关联函数（composite correlation functions）。结果显示单粒子谱保持费米液体行为，而多体通道的修正等价于单圈重整化群（one-loop renormalization group）。在前向散射模型下，系统不存在稳定长程序，相关磁化率在零温极限下呈现奇异幂律标度行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高维电子气中的前向散射相互作用在有限程条件下无法通过常规微扰理论精确求解，需要发展非微扰方法。此外，维度约化方法与多维玻色化技术之间的数学等价性尚未得到充分验证和系统应用。

Method: 采用与Haldane patch构造及多维玻色化（multidimensional bosonization）技术数学等价的维度约化方法，将D维两点关联函数映射到具有相同图结构的一维可玻色化高斯理论中精确求解。

Result: 单粒子谱函数保持费米液体（Fermi liquid）行为；多体通道被有限程相互作用有效重整化，等效于单圈重整化群修正；由于前向散射模型限制，系统不存在稳定长程序，相关磁化率在温度趋于零时呈现奇异幂律标度（singular power-law scaling）。

Conclusion: 维度约化方法为处理有限程前向散射相互作用的简并电子气提供了精确的非微扰框架，单粒子与多体通道表现出截然不同的行为模式，前者保持费米液体特征，后者则展现非费米液体式的奇异标度行为。

Abstract: In this work, we consider $N$-fold degenerate $D$-dimensional electron gas with spherical Fermi surface and arbitrary forward-scattering density-density interaction transferring small momentum compared to the Fermi momentum $k_{\mathrm{F}}$. The dimensional reduction that is mathematically equivalent to the Haldane patch construction and similar multidimensional bosonization techniques, provides a natural map of two-point $D$-dimensional correlation functions (fermion Green function, susceptibilities etc.) onto effective one-dimensional (1D) correlators with the same diagrammatic structure, which can be evaluated exactly within a 1D bosonizable (Gaussian) theory. We then apply this formalism to evaluate the fermion Green function, pair and charge/flavor susceptibilities, as well as the composite correlation functions for the case of a finite-range interaction, where the interaction range $R_{\mathrm{s}} \gg 1/k_{\mathrm{F}}$ is large compared to the Fermi wavelength. First, we find that the single-particle spectral function remains Fermi-liquid-like which is fully consistent with the previous research. In contrast to the single-particle sector, the many-body channels are efficiently dressed by finite-range interactions, and this dressing is fully equivalent to the one-loop renormalization group (RG), which is also in line with previous multidimensional bosonization results. Within the forward-scattering model, stable long-range order is not possible, and relevant susceptibilities demonstrate singular power-law scaling with temperature $T$ at $T \to 0$. The rest of the abstract is in the PDF.

### [134] [Correlation of maximum superconducting critical temperature with copper-oxygen energy distance and oxygen hole content in the Emery model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06460)
*Eleanor M. O'Callaghan,Nicolas Kowalski,A. -M. S. Tremblay,Giovanni Sordi*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文利用有限温度的细胞动力学平均场理论（cellular dynamical mean-field theory）研究Emery模型，发现最大超导临界温度（$T_c^{\rm max}$）在三个条件下达到最优：掺杂电荷转移绝缘体、靠近电荷转移绝缘体-金属边界、并深入电荷转移区间，且$T_c^{\rm max}$随铜氧能量距离增加而意外增大。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 识别优化铜氧化物超导关键模型——Emery模型中最大超导临界温度（$T_c^{\rm max}$）的微观参数仍然是一个挑战。

Method: 采用有限温度的细胞动力学平均场理论（cellular dynamical mean-field theory）对铜氧平面的Emery模型进行数值计算。

Result: 在固定母体电荷转移绝缘态（charge-transfer insulating state）的电荷隙（charge gap）大小时，$T_c^{\rm max}$随铜氧能量距离（copper-oxygen energy distance）增加而意外上升，这有利于电子从氧轨道转移到铜轨道。该结果自然地出现在Zaanen-Sawatzky-Allen框架中，并捕捉了空穴掺杂铜氧化物的实验趋势。

Conclusion: $T_c^{\rm max}$在Emery模型中的优化需要同时满足三个条件：掺杂电荷转移绝缘体（charge-transfer insulator）、靠近电荷转移绝缘体-金属边界（charge-transfer insulator to metal boundary）、以及深入电荷转移区间（charge-transfer regime），这为未来优化$T_c^{\rm max}$指明了新方向。

Abstract: Identifying microscopic parameters that optimize the maximum superconducting critical temperature $T_c^{\rm max}$ in the canonical model of the copper-oxygen plane of cuprates, the Emery model, remains challenging. Using cellular dynamical mean-field theory at finite temperature, we find that for a fixed charge gap size in the parent charge-transfer insulating state, $T_c^{\rm max}$ unexpectedly increases with increasing the copper-oxygen energy distance, as this favors the transfer of electrons from oxygen to copper orbitals. We show that these findings emerge naturally in the Zaanen-Sawatzky-Allen scheme and capture observed trends in hole-doped cuprates. Overall, our study uncovers that $T_c^{\rm max}$ is optimized in the Emery model under three conditions: upon doping a charge-transfer insulator, close to the charge-transfer insulator to metal boundary, and deep into the charge-transfer regime. This finding indicates new paths for optimizing $T_c^{\rm max}$.

</details>


### [135] [Charge-transfer gap size and oxygen hole content as two mechanisms controlling $T_c$ in the Emery model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06462)
*Eleanor M. O'Callaghan,Nicolas Kowalski,A. -M. S. Tremblay,Giovanni Sordi*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文利用胞动力学平均场理论（cellular dynamical mean-field theory, CDMFT）研究了Emery模型中铜氧化物超导临界温度（$T_c^{\rm max}$）的驱动因素，发现$T_c^{\rm max}$不仅在电荷转移绝缘体-金属边界附近存在优化，在电荷转移区深处也存在优化；氧空穴含量和电荷转移能隙大小是两个主要控制机制，其中氧空穴含量是主导变量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 揭示铜氧化物高温超导机理的关键在于理解超导临界温度（$T_c$）变化趋势的驱动因素，本研究旨在系统量化Emery模型中铜-氧能量距离与铜轨道局域排斥作用如何影响最大超导临界温度（$T_c^{\rm max}$）。

Method: 采用胞动力学平均场理论（cellular dynamical mean-field theory, CDMFT）研究铜氧面（copper-oxygen plane）的规范模型——Emery模型，并以Zaanen-Sawatzky-Allen（ZSA）相图作为指导框架进行系统性量化分析。

Result: $T_c^{\rm max}$不仅在电荷转移绝缘体-金属边界（charge-transfer insulator to metal boundary）附近存在优化，在电荷转移区（charge-transfer regime）深处也存在优化；$T_c^{\rm max}$随氧空穴含量（oxygen hole content）增加和电荷转移能隙（charge-transfer gap）减小而单调上升，氧空穴含量是主导变量。

Conclusion: 本文为冷原子体系实现Emery模型的实验方案提供了理论预测，并为理解空穴掺杂铜氧化物（hole-doped cuprates）的关键实验趋势建立了理论框架，揭示了一个此前未被探索的$T_c^{\rm max}$优化机制。

Abstract: Investigating the drivers of superconducting critical temperature trends in cuprates is crucial for uncovering the mechanism of high-temperature superconductivity. Here we study this problem in the canonical model of the copper-oxygen plane, the Emery model, with cellular dynamical mean-field theory. Using the Zaanen-Sawatzky-Allen diagram as a guiding framework, we systematically quantify how the maximum superconducting critical temperature $T_c^{\rm max}$ depends on the copper-oxygen energy distance and on the local repulsion on the copper orbital. Unexpectedly, $T_c^{\rm max}$ is optimized not only near the charge-transfer insulator to metal boundary, consistent with previous findings, but also deep in the charge-transfer regime, revealing an unexplored mechanism. Then we link model parameters to physical observables, identifying the charge-transfer gap size and the oxygen hole content as two mechanisms controlling $T_c^{\rm max}$. $T_c^{\rm max}$ increases monotonically as the oxygen hole content increases and the charge gap size decreases. The oxygen hole content is the dominant variable in varying $T_c^{\rm max}$. Our work provides predictions for proposed realizations of the Emery model with ultracold atoms and a theoretical framework for understanding key experimental trends in hole-doped cuprates.

### [136] [Eclipsing Kitaev: off-diagonal exchange governs the correlated high-field phases of $β$-Li$_2$IrO$_3$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06463)
*Vikram Nagarajan,Ioannis Rousochatzakis,Yuanqi Lyu,Darian Hall,Augusto Ghiotto,Josue Rodriguez,Koh Yamakawa,James Analytis,John Singleton,Mun K. Chan,Natalia B. Perkins,K. A. Modic*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过高达60 T的磁致磁化率（magnetotropic susceptibility）实验，解析了超蜂窝状Kitaev材料β-Li₂IrO₃的低温磁场-角度相图，发现系统并非直接从低场非公度态进入极化态，而是表现出强烈的方向依赖关联相。特别在ac平面内存在一个其他平面缺失的高场相。通过基于J-K-Γ模型的对称性分析，证明非对角Γ交换（off-diagonal Γ exchange）耦合了铁磁序与交错磁序，稳定了高场关联相，解释了为何场致自旋液体（field-induced spin liquid）的预言在候选材料中未能实现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解Kitaev材料在强磁场下的相行为，澄清为何理论上预期的场致自旋液体态在候选材料如β-Li₂IrO₃中未能出现，揭示限制极化态（polarized state）出现的关键相互作用机制。

Method: 采用高场（最高60 T）磁致磁化率测量，系统扫描主要晶面（principal crystallographic planes）的低温磁场-角度相图；结合基于J-K-Γ模型的微观计算进行对称性分析（symmetry-based description）。

Result: 系统从低场非公度态（incommensurate state）进入一系列强烈依赖于磁场方向的关联相（correlated phases），而非直接进入极化态。在ac平面内发现一个额外的高场相，该相在其余主晶面中不存在且仅存在于有限的磁场-角度空间区域。临界场（critical fields）的角度依赖性与理论定量吻合。

Conclusion: 非对角Γ交换是控制高场响应的关键相互作用，它通过耦合铁磁序与交错磁序稳定了对称性约束的关联相，从而阻止了极化态的出现。这解释了为何即使Kitaev相互作用很强，场致自旋液体在候选材料中仍未实现。

Abstract: We report a high-field thermodynamic study of the hyperhoneycomb Kitaev material $β$-Li$_2$IrO$_3$, using magnetotropic susceptibility to resolve its low-temperature field-angle phase diagram across the principal crystallographic planes in magnetic fields up to $60$ T. Rather than evolving directly from the low-field incommensurate state into a polarized regime, the system exhibits a strongly direction-dependent sequence of correlated phases. Most notably, for fields in the $ac$-plane, we identify an additional high-field phase that is absent in the other principal planes and exists only within a restricted region of field-angle space. This phase structure is naturally explained by the competition between magnetic field and bond-directional exchange interactions. Using a symmetry-based description supported by microscopic calculations within the $J$-$K$-$Γ$ model, we show that off-diagonal $Γ$ exchange couples the ferromagnetic and staggered magnetic orders and thereby stabilizes the observed correlated high-field phases. The measured angular dependence of the critical fields is quantitatively captured by this theory, identifying $Γ$ exchange as the key interaction controlling the high-field response. These results clarify why the promise of a field-induced spin liquid -- the notion that suppressing magnetic order might reveal the underlying Kitaev physics -- remains unfulfilled in candidate materials: even when the Kitaev interaction is large, off-diagonal exchange stabilizes symmetry-constrained correlated phases that instead preempt the polarized state.

### [137] [Economised path integrals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06414)
*Zezhu Zeng,David E. Manolopoulos*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种“Eco路径积分”（Eco path integral）方法，通过优化环聚合物弹簧势的简正模频率来改进标准Trotter路径积分近似，在仅需二阶Trotter计算量的情况下达到与四阶Suzuki-Chin方法相当的收敛速度，并成功应用于六方冰和MOF-5的热力学性质计算。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准Trotter路径积分（Trotter path integral）在环聚合物弹簧势的Hessian矩阵中具有零本征值（centroid eigenvalue）和简并对（degenerate pairs），但剩余的自由度仍可用于改进Trotter近似。本文旨在利用这些自由度优化简正模频率，以更高效地逼近精确量子力学结果。

Method: 利用环聚合物弹簧势的Hessian矩阵（一个$P\times P$的对称循环矩阵（symmetric circulant matrix））的可交换性和本征结构，保留其本征变换；通过求解简单最小二乘问题（least squares problem），优化剩余的$\lfloor P/2\rfloor$个独立非零简正模频率（normal mode frequencies），使其匹配频率范围$0\le\omega\le\omega_{\rm max}$内谐振环聚合物的精确量子力学回转半径（radii of gyration）

Result: 在六方冰（hexagonal ice）的算例中，Eco路径积分的收敛速度与四阶Suzuki-Chin路径积分相当，但仅需二阶Trotter的计算量。在MOF-5材料中，Eco方法被集成到GPUMD软件中，结合机器学习神经进化势（neuroevolution potential），成功收敛了负热膨胀系数（negative thermal expansion coefficient）和恒压热容（constant pressure heat capacity）。

Conclusion: Eco路径积分方法无需计算Suzuki-Chin方法中所需的投影Hessian（projected Hessians），无需开发新的可观测量估计器（estimators），且实现简便——仅需修改Trotter路径积分代码中的几行。该方法在保持二阶计算复杂度的同时获得了高阶收敛性能。

Abstract: The Hessian of the ring polymer spring potential in the standard Trotter path integral is a $P\times P$ symmetric circulant matrix with a centroid eigenvalue of zero. All such matrices commute and are diagonalised by the same bead to normal mode transformation matrix, and their eigenvalues contain $\lceil P/2\rceil-1$ degenerate pairs by symmetry. However, this still leaves some freedom to improve on the Trotter approximation: one can optimise the remaining $\lfloor P/2\rfloor$ independent non-zero normal mode frequencies to fit the exact quantum mechanical radii of gyration of harmonic ring polymers with frequencies in the range $0\leω\leω_{\rm max}$, where $ω_{\rm max}$ is the maximum physical frequency in the problem of interest. The optimisation involves solving a simple least squares problem for the optimum (economised or "Eco") internal mode frequencies. The remainder of the calculation then proceeds in the same way as a Trotter path integral calculation. An example application to hexagonal ice shows that the convergence of the Eco path integral is comparable to that of the 4th order Suzuki-Chin path integral, but with purely 2nd order Trotter effort. There is no need to calculate the projected Hessians that arise in the Suzuki-Chin method by finite differences, there is no need to develop any new estimators for observables, and once the Eco frequencies have been calculated the implementation of the Eco path integral involves changing just a few lines of a Trotter path integral code. To provide a more impressive example we have implemented the Eco method in GPUMD and used it to converge the (negative) thermal expansion coefficient and the constant pressure heat capacity of MOF-5 with a machine-learned neuroevolution potential.

</details>

Method: 在石墨烯π电子最近邻紧束缚（tight binding）框架内，Tan Bo模型利用Möbius变换结合指数衰减（exponential decay）对基于键长和键角的跃迁能量t(dr)进行参数化；通过对比各向同性（isotropic）、几何各向异性（geometrically anisotropic）及Slater-Koster（SK）尺度进行评估，并构造非厄米（non-Hermitian）TB组装方案。

Abstract: Within the tight binding framework of graphenes π electron nearest neighbors, the Tan Bo model parametrizes transition energies t(dr) based on bond lengths and angles via the Mobius transformation combined with exponential decay. Comparisons between isotropic , geometrically anisotropic , and Slater Koster scales reveal that B = 0 is equivalent to the SK scheme, with L(B) reaching its optimum at Bopt = 0. The Hermitian assembly maintains the Dirac cone at the K point.The Tan Bo geometry dependent transition model and non Hermitian TB assembly scheme developed in this study provide a reproducible single particle benchmark and parameterization reference for future non Hermitian chemical calculations incorporating electron correlation effects in graphene systems.

### [139] [Raman spectroscopy of the van der Waals altermagnet Co$_{1/4}$NbSe$_2$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05616)

TL;DR: 本文结合偏振分辨拉曼光谱和密度泛函理论（DFT），系统研究了Co插层和交错磁（altermagnetic）有序对层状化合物Co₁/₄NbSe₂晶格动力学的影响。研究发现Co插层通过能带折叠（zone folding）显著重构振动谱，并观测到A₁g对称性模式中的自旋-声子耦合（spin-phonon coupling），但在交错磁相变温度附近未发现拉曼光谱的不连续性。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用偏振分辨拉曼光谱（polarization-resolved Raman spectroscopy），并结合密度泛函理论（density-functional theory, DFT）进行理论支持。

Result: 识别出六个拉曼活性声子模；Co插层通过NbSe₂声子的能带折叠（zone folding）显著重构振动谱，产生兼具区中心和区边界特征的杂化模；Co原子因对称性不参与任何拉曼活性模，这与相关1/3化合物不同；交错磁相变温度附近的变温拉曼测量未显示不连续性；在A₁g对称性模式中发现了自旋-声子耦合（spin-phonon coupling）的证据，归因于其面外Se位移。

Conclusion: 插层对过渡金属二硫属化物（TMD）的振动性质有显著影响，并证实了在新发现的交错磁（altermagnetic）材料中存在自旋-声子相互作用（spin-phonon interactions）。

Abstract: We investigate the influence of Co intercalation and altermagnetic order on the lattice dynamics of the layered compound Co$_{1/4}$NbSe$_2$. Polarization-resolved Raman spectroscopy, supported by density-functional theory, enables identification of six Raman-active phonons. Co intercalation drives a substantial reconstruction of the vibrational spectrum through zone folding of NbSe$_2$ phonons, producing hybridized modes with mixed zone-center and zone-boundary character. Despite this, Co atoms do not participate in any Raman-active modes by symmetry, which is in marked contrast to related 1/3 compounds where intercalant modes do contribute to the Raman spectrum. Temperature-dependent Raman measurements across the altermagnetic transition show no discontinuities, which is consistent with short-range spin correlations in the quasi-one-dimensional Co chains. However, we find evidence for spin-phonon coupling in A$_{1g}$ symmetry modes owing to their out-of-plane Se displacements. Our work demonstrates the substantial impact of intercalation on the vibrational properties of transition metal dichalcogenides and the presence of spin-phonon interactions in a newly discovered altermagnetic material.

### [140] [Domain-Growth Kinetics and Scaling Laws Governing Pulse-Driven Accumulative Polarization Switching in HZO](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05617)
*Manish Anand*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过基于含时Landau-Ginzburg（time-dependent Landau-Ginzburg）形式论的相场模型，系统研究了HZO铁电体中由亚矫顽电场脉冲序列驱动的累积极化翻转（accumulative polarization switching）动力学，建立了畴壁动力学与宏观极化积累之间的定量联系，揭示了三种不同的标度（scaling）区间，并提出了一个统一的标度框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 累积极化翻转为实现低功耗铁电存储器和神经形态器件提供了有前景的途径，但控制这一非平衡过程的动力学机制（kinetic regimes）尚不明确。

Method: 采用基于含时Landau-Ginzburg形式论（time-dependent Landau-Ginzburg formalism）的相场模型，系统变化初始畴结构（domain configuration）、脉冲幅度、脉冲开启时间和脉冲关闭时间，研究铁电HZO中的脉冲驱动累积翻转。

Result: 有效翻转畴半径遵循由局域动力学指数（local kinetic exponent）表征的三种不同标度区间：局域指数大于1时呈超线性畴增长；接近1时呈稳态自相似增长；小于1时因几何约束、可翻转极化耗尽和弛豫导致的反向翻转而呈减速动力学。增加脉冲幅度或脉冲开启时间延长超线性区，而更长的脉冲关闭时间促进弛豫并抑制累积。

Conclusion: 这些发现建立了脉冲驱动累积翻转的统一标度框架（unified scaling framework），为非平衡铁电畴演化提供了定量认识，并为基于HZO的存储器和神经形态器件提供了设计指南。

Abstract: Accumulative polarization switching driven by sequential sub-coercive electric-field pulses offers a promising route toward low-power ferroelectric memories and neuromorphic devices. However, the kinetic regimes governing this nonequilibrium process remain poorly understood. Here, we employ a phase-field model based on the time-dependent Landau-Ginzburg formalism to investigate pulse-driven accumulative switching in ferroelectric HZO. By systematically varying the initial domain configuration, pulse amplitude, pulse-on time, and pulse-off time, we establish a quantitative link between microscopic domain-wall dynamics and macroscopic polarization accumulation. We show that the effective switched-domain radius follows distinct scaling regimes characterized by the local kinetic exponent. Initially, a local exponent greater than 1 indicates superlinear domain growth driven by enhanced irreversible domain-wall propagation under successive pulses. As switching progresses, a local exponent close to unity marks steady self-similar growth, whereas a local exponent less than 1 signifies decelerating dynamics caused by geometric confinement, depletion of switchable polarization, and relaxation-induced back switching. The transition between these regimes is governed by the competition between field-driven excitation during the pulse-on interval and spontaneous relaxation during the pulse-off interval. The initial domain geometry further influences this transition. Increasing the pulse amplitude or pulse-on duration extends the superlinear regime, whereas longer pulse-off times promote relaxation and suppress accumulation. These findings establish a unified scaling framework for pulse-driven accumulative switching, providing quantitative insight into nonequilibrium ferroelectric domain evolution and design guidelines for HZO-based memory and neuromorphic devices.

### [141] [Electric Field Induced Multi-Space Topological Phase Transitions in Janus Monolayer MnBi2Se2Te2](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05631)
*Kefan Zhang,Jian Wu,Weiyi Pan*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 通过第一性原理计算和原子自旋模拟，本研究证明了Janus单层MnBi2Se2Te2在外电场作用下可同时实现动量空间拓扑相变（从拓扑平庸态到低陈数和高陈数量子反常霍尔态）和实空间拓扑相变（从铁磁态到孤立斯格明子态再到斯格明子-螺旋畴共存相），为多功能自旋电子学器件提供了材料平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在单一材料中操控共存的多种空间拓扑态是低功耗自旋电子学（spintronics）应用的关键前沿，而垂直电场门控提供了一种高精度的调控机制。该研究旨在探索一种能够同时实现动量空间和实空间拓扑相变协同控制的材料体系。

Method: 采用第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）和原子自旋模拟（atomistic spin simulations），研究了Janus单层MnBi2Se2Te2在外电场作用下的拓扑性质变化。

Result: 电场驱动了动量空间拓扑相变，包括拓扑平庸态（C=0）、低陈数量子反常霍尔态（C=-1）和高陈数态（C=2）。同时，通过调控Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya相互作用（Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya interaction）与磁各向异性（magnetic anisotropy）的竞争，实空间磁态从均匀铁磁态转变为孤立斯格明子（skyrmion）态，最终进入斯格明子-螺旋畴共存相。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了一个强大的材料平台和有效路径，用于协同控制共存的拓扑序，涉及纯k空间拓扑、RK联合斯格明子和纯实空间斯格明子等多种拓扑相区，为下一代多功能自旋电子学器件提供了有前景的方案。

Abstract: Manipulating coexisting multi-space topological states within a single material is a critical frontier for low-power spintronic applications, for which perpendicular electric-field gating offers a highly precise tuning mechanism. Using first-principles calculations and atomistic spin simulations, it is demonstrated that Janus monolayer MnBi2Se2Te2 can exhibit simultaneous momentum-space and real-space topological phase transitions under an external electric field. Specifically, the electric field drives momentum-space transitions across a topologically trivial state (C = 0), a low-Chern-number quantum anomalous Hall state (C = -1), and a high-Chern-number state (C = 2). Concurrently, by actively tuning the competition between the Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya interaction and magnetic anisotropy, the electric field induces real-space magnetic transitions from a uniform ferromagnetic state to an isolated skyrmion state, and ultimately to a skyrmion-spiral domain coexistence phase. Electric-field-induced variations in both the QAHE and magnetic textures may give rise to multiple topological phase transitions, involving distinct topological regimes: a purely k-space topology, RK-joint skyrmions, and pure real-space skyrmions. These findings establish a powerful material platform and efficient route for the synergistic control of coexisting topological orders, making it highly promising for next generation multi-functional spintronic devices.

</details>


### [142] [Ultrahigh-Entropy Compositionally Complex Ceramics: Fluorite-Pyrochlore Phase Stability and Order-Disorder Transitions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05675)
*Keqi Song,Jian Luo*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究合成了三组共96种超高等熵组分复杂陶瓷（CCCs），包含16-19种组分。其中首次观察到氟石-氟石双相结构；与三元A2B2O7烧绿石和五元高熵陶瓷相比，超高等熵CCCs更易形成有序烧绿石相，且在高晶格畸变下烧绿石形成反而增强。新19组分系列中，保持2:2阳离子比的系列在y~0.84处发生烧绿石-氟石有序-无序转变（ODT），而非2:2比的系列在z~0.41-0.44处发生突变性ODT，显著偏离序参量投影的预期转变点z~0.64。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究超高等熵（ultrahigh-entropy）组分复杂陶瓷在包含16-19种组分时的相形成行为与有序-无序转变（order-disorder transition, ODT）规律，并与低组分体系进行对比。

Method: 合成了三组共96种超高等熵组分复杂陶瓷，包含16-19种组分；通过X射线衍射等表征手段分析相结构，并利用序参量（order parameter）线性投影分析烧绿石超结构峰强度。

Conclusion: 超高等熵组分复杂陶瓷展现出与低熵体系不同的相形成行为和有序-无序转变规律，阳离子配比（2:2 vs 非2:2）显著影响ODT的临界点和转变方式。

Abstract: Three groups of 32 ultrahigh-entropy compositionally complex ceramics (CCCs) containing 16-19 components were synthesized and characterized. The first group of 15 CCCs forms single ultrahigh-entropy fluorite or pyrochlore phases in 12 compositions, while two compositions exhibit fluorite-fluorite dual phases, observed for the first time. Compared with ternary A2B2O7 pyrochlore, these ultrahigh-entropy CCCs are more prone to ordering (pyrochlore formation), surprisingly even more at higher size disorder (more lattice distortion), with suppressed dual-phase formation relative to five-component high-entropy ceramics. Two new 19-component series, denoted as "19CCC-P|Fy" and "19CCC-P|Fz", form single ultrahigh-entropy fluorite or pyrochlore phases. The 19CCC-P|Fy series, maintaining a 2:2 ratio of 3+ and 4+ cations, exhibits a pyrochlore-to-fluorite order-disorder transition (ODT) at y ~ 0.84, consistent with the linear projection of the pyrochlore superstructure peak intensity as an order parameter. In contrast, the 19CCC-P|Fz series with non-2:2 ratios of 3+ and 4+ cations show an abrupt ODT at z ~ 0.41-0.44, despite a projected transition at z ~ 0.64 from the order parameter.

*Yu Liu,Boris Slautin,Ian Mercer,Jon-Paul Maria,Sergei V. Kalinin*

Method: 引入耦合数字孪生框架，分别构建样本孪生（编码材料状态）和仪器孪生（捕获信号形成、反馈动力学及操作约束），再通过耦合估计预期输出、不确定性和风险。在调幅扫描探针显微镜中，采用物理信息编码器处理力-距离曲线、确定性扫描仪模型描述悬臂与反馈动力学，并结合稀疏学习残差校正。

Result: 编码器以亚纳米级精度恢复扫描仪驱动描述符；校准后的扫描仪在几纳米内复现典型迹线，并识别出操作点噪声放大是失配的主要来源。补充的相位分析将残差误差定位到相位通道，明确了需要补充物理模型的区域。

Abstract: Automated experimentation is moving from closed-loop optimization toward open decision-making, where human or AI planners must forecast the consequences of candidate actions before executing them. Such forecasts require a model of both sides of the experiment: how the sample is likely to respond and what the instrument is likely to detect. We therefore introduce a coupled digital-twin framework that separates these roles and then links them. In this framework, the sample twin encodes material state inferred from prior knowledge and measurements till the moment. The instrument twin captures signal formation, feedback dynamics, and operating constraints based on prior knowledge. When coupled, the two twins estimate expected outcomes, uncertainty, and risk for candidate microscope operations. For amplitude-modulation scanning probe microscopy, we realize this framework with a physics-informed encoder of force-distance curves, a deterministic scanner model of cantilever and feedback dynamics, and sparse learned residual corrections. The encoder first recovers scanner-driving descriptors with sub-nanometer accuracy. The calibrated scanner then reproduces typical traces within a few nanometers and identifies operating-point noise amplification as the main source of mismatch. Supplementary phase analysis localizes residual error to the phase channel, which clarifies where added physics is needed. Together, these results establish coupled sample and instrument twins as a practical foundation for predictive microscope operation and autonomous experimental planning.

### [144] [Efficient Bethe-Salpeter Equation Calculations Based on Numerical Atomic Orbitals and Norm-Conserving Pseudopotentials: Dual-${\boldsymbol k}$-Mesh Strategy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05853)
*Ziqing Guan,Yu Cao,Min-Ye Zhang,Peize Lin,Ruiyi Zhou,Xinguo Ren*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的GW+BSE计算方法在计算吸收谱时，BSE核的构建和哈密顿量对角化通常需要精细的k网格采样，计算成本高昂。因此需要发展一种能够从粗k网格高效插值到密k网格的实现方案，降低计算开销同时保持精度。

Method: 采用数值原子轨道（NAO）和模守恒赝势。利用局域化分辨率恒等式（LRI）技术，将屏蔽库仑相互作用表示为实空间、按单胞索引的短程形式$W_{μν}(\boldsymbol R)$，实现BSE核从粗k网格到密k网格的傅里叶插值，构建双k网格工作流。

Result: 对分子体系和周期性体系的基准计算验证了该实现的准确性；系统考察了吸收谱在NAO基组、辅助基组和k点采样下的收敛行为。

Conclusion: 双k网格策略被确立为GW+BSE计算中一种实用且可靠的方法；本工作在ABACUS+LibRPA框架下的实现为大规模激发态计算提供了高效工具。

Abstract: We present an efficient implementation of the Bethe--Salpeter equation (BSE) based on numerical atomic orbitals (NAOs) and norm-conserving pseudopotentials within the ABACUS+LibRPA framework. By exploiting the localized resolution-of-identity (LRI) technique, the screened Coulomb interaction is cast into a real-space, unit-cell-indexed form $W_{μν}(\boldsymbol R)$ that is inherently short-ranged and well localized. This spatial locality enables an efficient Fourier interpolation of the BSE kernel from the coarse $\boldsymbol k$-mesh used in the preceding $GW$ calculation to an arbitrarily dense $\boldsymbol k$-mesh on which the BSE Hamiltonian is assembled and diagonalized, thereby giving rise naturally to a dual-$\boldsymbol k$-mesh workflow. Building on this scheme, we systematically examine the convergence of the absorption spectra with respect to the NAO basis set, the auxiliary basis set, and the $\boldsymbol k$-point sampling. Benchmark calculations for both molecular and periodic systems collectively validate the accuracy of the present implementation and establish the dual-$\boldsymbol k$-mesh strategy as a practical and reliable approach for $GW$+BSE calculations.

### [145] [Anomalous Piezoelectricity from Polarization-Dependent Electrostriction in Wurtzites](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05854)

Method: 选取强极性纤锌矿材料（wurtzites），包括AlN、Al₁₋ₓScₓN、Al₁₋ₓBₓN、GaN和ZnO，研究其电致伸缩张量和压电张量随极化的变化关系，分析其物理起源。

Result: 发现纤锌矿中的电致伸缩系数和弹性模量均强烈依赖于极化；压电系数与极化呈高度非线性关系，并存在极化减小反而增大电致应变（electromechanical strain）响应的反常现象。

Conclusion: 电致伸缩和压电效应中表现出的反常极化依赖性源于极化增加过程中层状参考非极性结构向四面体配位纤锌矿网络结构的演化；该发现对理解纤锌矿铁电体（wurtzite ferroelectrics）的热力学行为及调控其压电与铁电性能具有重要意义。

Abstract: The piezoelectric coefficient is a third-rank tensor connecting the strain or stress with the electric field or polarization, whereas the electrostriction coefficient is a fourth-rank tensor relating the strain to the square of electric polarization. The electrostriction tensor components in the current literature are often treated as constants independent of polarization, resulting in piezoelectric tensor components that are linearly proportional to polarization and the dielectric susceptibility tensor. Here, we study the electrostriction and piezoelectricity in strongly polar wurtzites, including AlN, Al$_{1-x}$Sc$_x$N, Al$_{1-x}$B$_x$N, GaN, and ZnO. We discover that electrostriction and the elastic modulus in wurtzites are both strongly polarization-dependent, and the piezoelectric coefficient is highly nonlinear with respect to polarization, including the anomalous possibility that decreasing polarization increases the electromechanical strain response. These unusual dependencies of electrostriction and piezoelectric effects on polarization arise from the evolution of a layered reference nonpolar structure toward a tetrahedrally coordinated wurtzite network structure as the polarization increases. The findings have important implications in understanding the thermodynamics of the general class of wurtzite ferroelectrics and in manipulating their piezoelectric and ferroelectric behaviors.

While this equilibrium transition has been studied, it remains an open question whether such a reorientation can be triggered on ultrafast timescales using femtosecond laser excitation. In this work, we investigate the ultrafast spin-reorientation dynamics in DyCo$_5$. The time-dependent orientation of the magnetization vector following femtosecond laser excitation is quantified by combining polar with transverse magneto-optical Kerr effect (MOKE) measurements in the extreme ultraviolet spectral range, which are sensitive to the out-of-plane and in-plane magnetization component, respectively. ### [147] [Modelling the mean inner potential of alloyed and strained materials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05948)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: In this publication, we study the influence of strain and alloying on the mean inner potential (MIP) using density functional theory (DFT) within an augmented plane waves plus local orbitals basis set. Two major effects have been identified allowing to model the influence of strain and alloying on the mean inner potential with a reasonable accuracy. First, alloying for constant volume results in a linear relationship between the MIP and the concentration. Second, the MIP scales with changes in volume as we already pointed out in an earlier publication (M. Schowalter, D. Lamoen, A. Rosenauer, P. Kruse, and D. Gerthsen, Appl. Phys. Lett. 85, 4938-4940 (2004)). Specifically, a linear relationship between MIP and concentration x was found for AlGaAs (nearly no change in lattice parameter), whereas InGaP and GeSi (volume changes with concentration x) exhibits a clear bowing. The bowing can be modeled by taking the rescaling of the MIP with the varying volume additionally into account. The rescaling could be also used to model the dependence of the MIP on strained binary cells and the density dependence of e.g. amorphous materials.

Motivation: 磁性范德瓦尔斯材料（magnetic van der Waals materials）在块体或少量层状薄片中已被广泛研究，但由于原子级薄膜制备的困难，仅有少数材料能以单层形式被分离，且通常在150 K以下才表现出长程磁有序。因此，探索能在更高温度下保持单层铁磁性的材料及其合成方法是本研究的主要动机。

Method: 采用分子束外延（molecular beam epitaxy, MBE）技术合成Co掺杂的Fe5GeTe2，实现了对薄膜厚度和组分比例的精确控制。利用元素特异性X射线磁圆二色性（X-ray magnetic circular dichroism, XMCD）和密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）对Co掺杂位点及磁性变化机制进行了表征与分析。

Result: 多层Co掺杂Fe5GeTe2样品表现出远超室温的铁磁性，单层样品在约200 K以下仍存在铁磁有序。随着组分变化，居里温度（Curie temperature）和磁各向异性（magnetic anisotropy）在单层与更厚薄膜中呈现相同的变化趋势。Co掺杂虽自身磁矩较弱，但能够增强邻近Fe原子的磁矩，并强化层内铁磁交换相互作用（intralayer ferromagnetic exchange interactions），从而提升居里温度。

Conclusion: 本研究表明，磁性性质主要由层内磁相互作用（intralayer magnetic interactions）主导。Co掺杂的Fe5GeTe2在单层条件下实现了远高于传统磁性范德瓦尔斯材料的居里温度，为二维磁性材料在室温以上应用提供了可行路径。

Abstract: Magnetic van der Waals materials have mainly been investigated in their bulk form or as few-layers flakes. Due to the challenges in producing atomically thin films, only a few have been isolated as monolayers, which typically exhibit long-range magnetic order below 150 K. In this work, we use molecular beam epitaxy to synthesize Co-doped Fe5GeTe2, achieving precise control over both thickness and composition. We demonstrate ferromagnetism well above room temperature in multilayer samples and present clear evidence of ferromagnetic ordering in monolayers up to $\sim$200 K. The changes in Curie temperature and magnetic anisotropy with composition exhibit similar trends in both monolayers and thicker films, indicating that the magnetic properties are primarily governed by intralayer magnetic interactions. Through element-specific X-ray magnetic circular dichroism and density functional theory, we identify the substitution site of Co dopants and reveal the mechanism behind the Curie temperature enhancement induced by Co doping. Our findings suggest that, despite their weak magnetic moment, Co dopants strengthen the magnetic moments on neighboring Fe atoms and enhance the intralayer ferromagnetic exchange interactions.

</details>


### [149] [Deep-learning Hamiltonian reveals twist-tunable flat bands and nonlinear photocurrents in SrTiO3 moire bilayers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06053)
*Meiyang Yu,Chen Shen,Ruiwen Xie,Jingwei Tao,Lijun Zhang,Hongbin Zhang*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究将密度泛函理论（DFT）与E(3)等变深度学习哈密顿量框架DeepH-E3相结合，研究扭转双层SrTiO₃的电子结构和光学响应，揭示了扭转角减小会导致价带平坦化，并显著增强非线性光学响应如二次谐波产生（SHG），而线性响应则基本保持不变。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）结合E(3)等变深度学习哈密顿量框架DeepH-E3，在未扭转双层（untwisted bilayer）的不同层间滑动构型上训练模型，然后应用于具有不同扭转角（8.80°至53.13°）的共格扭转双层（commensurate twisted bilayer）系统。

Result: 扭转角减小导致价带（valence bands）系统性地展平，在最小扭转角下形成近乎无色散的能带。介电响应（dielectric response）和自旋霍尔电导率（spin Hall conductivity）与未扭转双层相近，而非线性光学响应受扭转影响更显著；二次谐波产生（second-harmonic generation, SHG）相对于未扭转时的弱响应大幅增强，移位电流（shift current）在响应计算范围（53.13°至22.62°）内呈现清晰的扭转角依赖性。

Conclusion: 扭转工程（twist engineering）可以有效调控氧化物莫尔体系（oxide moire systems）中的电子和光电响应，为设计新型功能氧化物器件提供可能。

Abstract: The extension of moire physics to complex oxides offers new ways to manipulate electronic states, but the large oxide moire supercells make systematic first-principles calculations demanding. Here, we combine density functional theory with the E(3)-equivariant deep-learning Hamiltonian framework DeepH-E3 to investigate the twist-angle-dependent electronic structure and optical responses of twisted bilayer SrTiO3. The model is trained on untwisted bilayers with different interlayer-sliding configurations and then applied to commensurate twisted bilayers with twist angles from 8.80 degrees to 53.13 degrees. Compared with the untwisted bilayer, decreasing twist angle systematically flattens the valence bands and leads to nearly dispersionless bands at the smallest angles studied. Based on the predicted Hamiltonians, we evaluate the dielectric response, second-harmonic generation (SHG), shift current, and spin Hall conductivity. The dielectric response and spin Hall conductivity remain close to those of the untwisted bilayer, whereas the nonlinear optical responses are more strongly affected by twisting. SHG is strongly enhanced relative to the weak untwisted response, and the shift current shows a clear twist-angle dependence within the response-calculation range (53.13 degrees-22.62 degrees). These results show that twist engineering can control electronic and optoelectronic responses in oxide moire systems.

### [150] [Stabilization of Stone-Wales Defects in Metal-supported Graphene](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06057)
*Rob H. Mason,Manuka M. S. Sinharage,Hansika I. Sirikumara,Sabrina Nilufar,Thushari Jayasekera*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用第一性原理密度泛函理论（first-principles density functional theory, DFT）计算，比较了自由石墨烯与金属支撑石墨烯（石墨烯/Cu(111)和石墨烯/Al(111)体系）中SW缺陷的激活能（activation energy）、形成能（formation energy）和恢复能（restoration energy）三个能量参数。

Result: 金属支撑石墨烯中SW缺陷的形成能在自由石墨烯基础上增加约12%，激活能降低约20%，恢复能降低约35%。能量参数对金属类型（Cu vs Al）的依赖较小。这些变化共同表明金属衬底使SW缺陷在能量上更易形成，但恢复能仍显著高于自愈合阈值。

Conclusion: 金属衬底的存在使SW缺陷的形成在能量上更为有利，且恢复能仍足够高，阻止了缺陷的自愈合。因此，一旦形成，SW缺陷趋于稳定，表明在金属支撑石墨烯中可能实现终端SW缺陷（terminal SW defect）的形成。

Abstract: The characteristics of graphene-metal interfaces play a decisive role in their electronic, optoelectronic, and mechanical applications. Properties such as charge transfer across the interface become particularly significant in the presence of topological defects. The stability of Stone Wales (SW) defects in graphene is governed by the balance between three energy descriptors, the activation energy, formation energy, and restoration energy. By comparing the energy parameters obtained from first-principles density functional theory calculations, we show that SW defect formation is energetically more favorable on metal-supported graphene. Our calculations for SW defects in graphene/Cu(111) and graphene/Al(111) systems indicate only a little dependence of energy profile on the type of metal. The presence of the metal substrate leads to a $\sim$ 12\% increase in the formation energy and a $\sim$ 20\% reduction in the activation energy, which together favor the formation of Stone Wales defects. Although the restoration energy decreases by about $\sim$ 35\% in metal-supported graphene, it remains significantly higher to prevent self-healing. As a result, once formed, the Stone Wales defects are likely to remain stable, suggesting the possibility of terminal SW defect formation in metal-supported graphene.

### [151] [Multiscale modelling of diffusion and retention of hydrogen in multi-occupancy traps in irradiated bcc metals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06122)

Result: 全原子模拟结果与多占据陷阱解析理论之间取得良好一致，验证了该解析模型适用于含有辐射损伤特征纳米级缺陷的材料。研究证明了氢陷阱占据快速达到稳态、空洞在钨中自发形成以及空洞内分子氢的生成，并给出了从第一性原理出发的氢在钨空洞中扩散与滞留的预测。

Conclusion: 多占据陷阱（multi-occupancy traps）的扩散率和滞留解析形式不仅是一种实用且可从第一性原理推导和参数化的预测方案，而且优于现有的单占据陷阱（single-occupancy trap）形式体系，为预测辐射损伤微观结构中氢同位素的扩散与滞留提供了有效的理论工具。

Abstract: We use molecular dynamics simulations to directly compute the effective diffusivity of hydrogen gas atoms in homogeneous distributions of monovacancies in tungsten and vanadium, and voids in tungsten. Rather than fitting the results to an Arrhenius law, we compare to an analytic approximation for the effective diffusivity recently derived for multi-occupancy traps [Kaur et al (2025), Phys. Rev. Mater. 9:125404]. We find good agreement between full atomistic simulation and our theory, validating the analytic model for diffusivity for materials containing nanoscale defects characteristic of radiation damage. There are no parameters fitted, only physically motivated quantities that can be computed with static density functional or atomistic potential calculations. In this study we prove rapid convergence of hydrogen trap occupation to the steady state using lattice kinetic Monte Carlo, the spontaneous emergence of voids in tungsten using atomistic simulation with empirical potentials, and molecular hydrogen formation in voids using molecular dynamics. We conclude with a prediction for diffusion and retention of hydrogen in voids in tungsten starting from first principles. This work shows that not only is the analytic form for diffusivity and retention in multi-occupancy traps a practical scheme for making predictive simulations of hydrogen isotope diffusion and retention in irradiated microstructures, derived and parameterized from first principles, it is superior to existing single-occupancy trap formalisms.
