### [152] [Inverse heterodyne effect in bimodal Kelvin probe force microscopy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06135)
*Hugo Valloire,Sylvain Clair,Christian Loppacher,Laurent Nony,Benjamin Grévin*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文发现了异质外差开尔文探针力显微镜（He-KPFM）中的逆异质外差效应：第二本征模的异质外差驱动运动通过频域转换对第一本征模产生反作用，引起可测量的模间能量交换。结合双模态维里与功率平衡框架以及非截断的针尖-表面电容梯度动力学，推导出闭合解析表达式，并在超高真空实验中得到验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在开环He-KPFM中，第二本征模被激励至有限振幅时，其异质外差驱动运动对基频本征模产生的动力学反作用（dynamical back-action）尚未被充分研究。作者旨在揭示这一被忽视的逆异质外差效应（inverse heterodyne effect）及其物理机制。

Method: 结合双模态维里与功率平衡框架（bimodal virial and power-balance framework），以及配套论文中发展的非截断针尖-表面电容梯度动力学（non-truncated tip-surface capacitance-gradient dynamics）描述，推导逆异质外差耦合与开环振幅调制He-KPFM可观测量的闭合解析表达式，并通过超高真空频率依赖和电压依赖实验进行验证。

Result: 理论预测逆异质外差耦合主要出现在耗散通道中，且在解调频率接近第二本征模共振时表现出尖锐的共振依赖性；其保守贡献对频率偏移的影响在典型条件下相对较弱。超高真空实验通过频率和电压依赖测量验证了上述预测。

Conclusion: 逆异质外差效应建立了模间能量交换和基于耗散的可观测量的物理图像。该工作将异质外差力显微镜与更广泛的驱动多模系统联系起来，其中非线性耦合和频率转换产生模间能量转移、反作用和耗散型可观测量。

Abstract: Heterodyne Kelvin probe force microscopy (He-KPFM) enables high-sensitivity electrostatic measurements by converting a bias-modulated interaction into a resonant response at a higher cantilever eigenmode. While the "direct" heterodyne actuation of the second eigenmode is well established, the dynamical back-action of this heterodyne-driven motion on the fundamental eigenmode has remained largely unexplored, particularly in open-loop operation where the second mode is excited to a finite amplitude. Here, we demonstrate an inverse heterodyne effect: a force component generated by heterodyne frequency conversion acts back on the first eigenmode and produces measurable inter-mode energy exchange. The analysis combines a bimodal virial and power-balance framework with a non-truncated description of the tip-surface capacitance-gradient dynamics developed and validated in a companion manuscript submitted concurrently to the same journal. On this basis, we derive closed-form expressions linking inverse heterodyne coupling to the experimentally accessible observables of non-contact AFM open-loop amplitude-modulated He-KPFM. The theory predicts that inverse heterodyne coupling appears predominantly in the dissipation channel, with a sharply resonant dependence on the demodulation frequency near the second-eigenmode resonance, while its conservative contribution to the frequency shift remains comparatively weaker under typical conditions. Ultrahigh-vacuum experiments validate these predictions and isolate the inverse heterodyne signature through frequency- and voltage-dependent measurements. Beyond KPFM, this work connects heterodyne force microscopy to a broader class of driven multimode systems in which nonlinear coupling and frequency conversion produce inter-mode energy transfer, back-action, and dissipation-based observables.

### [153] [On the capacitance gradient description in Heterodyne Kelvin Probe Force Microscopy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06161)
*Hugo Valloire,Sylvain Clair,Christian Loppacher,Laurent Nony,Benjamin Grévin*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文针对异频开尔文探针力显微镜（heterodyne KPFM）中传统一阶截断泰勒展开的局限性，建立了尖端-表面电容梯度（CG）动力学的严格谱描述，证明了非截断泰勒级数在单模态和双模态运动中的收敛性，并通过数值模拟验证了截断区域分层的有效性。该工作为多模态力显微镜中的静电力和可观测量的描述提供了形式化基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统异频KPFM中，一阶截断泰勒级数处理电容梯度（capacitance gradient, CG）的方法仅适用于小振幅区域且收敛性未解决，缺乏严谨的谱描述。

Method: 建立了非截断的泰勒级数描述CG动力学，基于Hudlet电容模型在单模态和双模态运动中证明其收敛性；在单模态情形下推导了傅里叶系数与泰勒系数的等价性及阶截断准则，并将形式化方法推广至双模态运动。

Result: 数值模拟验证了泰勒系数向傅里叶系数的收敛，以及单模态和双模态两种配置下的截断区域分层结构。

Conclusion: 该工作为开放环异频实验中的静电力分量和原子力显微镜（AFM）可观测量的描述提供了形式化基础，并建立了多模态力显微镜中涉及非线性机电耦合与频率转换的CG动力学通用框架。

Abstract: Kelvin probe force microscopy (KPFM) probes local surface-potential variations through the electrostatic force between a conductive tip and a surface, which depends on the potential difference and the tip-surface capacitance gradient (CG). In heterodyne KPFM, the oscillating tip is usually treated by combining a bias-modulated electric field with a first-order truncated Taylor-series expansion of the CG. Although convenient, this treatment is limited to a poorly defined small-amplitude regime and leaves the convergence of the series unresolved. Here, we establish a rigorous spectral description of the CG dynamics and of the resulting electrostatic force beyond this approximation.
  We formulate a non-truncated Taylor-series description of the CG and prove its convergence for a realistic Hudlet-based capacitance model in both monomodal and bimodal motion. In the monomodal case, we show the equivalence between Fourier-series and Taylor-series descriptions, derive explicit expressions for the dominant Fourier coefficients, and introduce order-truncation criteria that replace the usual qualitative notion of a small-amplitude regime. We then extend the formalism to bimodal motion and derive the effective CG coefficients governing the static, first-eigenmode, and second-eigenmode components of the electrostatic interaction.
  Numerical simulations confirm the convergence of the Taylor-based coefficients toward the Fourier coefficients and support the truncation-regime hierarchy in both configurations. This work establishes the formal basis for describing electrostatic force components and AFM observables in open-loop heterodyne experiments and provides a general framework for CG dynamics in multimode force microscopy involving nonlinear electromechanical coupling and frequency conversion.

</details>


### [154] [Piezoaxial coupling for strain-selected ferroaxial domain control](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06209)
*Rikuto Oiwa,Satoru Hayami*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文基于对称性构建了铁轴序（ferroaxial order）的应变衍生共轭场层级体系，并通过第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）证明了应变可以选择性地控制铁轴畴（ferroaxial domain）。在三角晶系铁轴化合物Na₂BaMg(PO₄)₂中，理论预测的立方应变标度关系与角度依赖关系得到了计算验证，确立了静态均匀应变作为铁轴序对称性允许的共轭场（conjugate field）的地位，并提出通过应变场冷却控制铁轴畴的路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 铁轴序在空间反演和时间反演下均为偶宇称（even parity），因此普通的电场和磁场不能作为其普适的线性共轭场（linear conjugate fields），需要寻找新的对称性允许的物理场来实现铁轴畴的控制。

Method: 首先基于对称性分析（symmetry analysis）构建了应变衍生共轭场的层级体系，考虑了不同母点群（parent point group）和铁轴分量对主导阶次（leading order）的影响；然后采用第一性原理计算，对三角晶系铁轴化合物Na₂BaMg(PO₄)₂进行固定应变下的原子弛豫（fixed-strain atomic relaxations）验证。

Result: 基面应变（basal-plane strain）的主导共轭场在正交晶系为线性、四方晶系为二次、三角和六方晶系为三次；立方晶系分为两类：立方-I群（23和m\bar{3}）允许选定轴的线性全场，立方-II群（432、\bar{4}3m和m\bar{3}m）禁止线性场。对三角晶系，基面偏差应变（deviatoric strain）给出单轴场h∝ε_u³sin6θ。第一性原理计算验证了该角度依赖关系和立方应变标度，并展示了从顺铁轴（para-axial）结构向铁轴畴的应变选择演化。

Conclusion: 静态均匀应变是一种对称性允许的铁轴序共轭场，可以通过应变场冷却（strain-field cooling）的途径实现铁轴畴的定向控制。

Abstract: We formulate a symmetry-based hierarchy of strain-derived conjugate fields for ferroaxial order, and demonstrate strain-selected ferroaxial domain control using first-principles calculations. Since ferroaxial order is even under both spatial inversion and time reversal, ordinary electric and magnetic fields cannot serve as universal linear conjugate fields. Homogeneous strain, however, can generate symmetry-allowed piezoaxial fields whose leading order is determined by the parent point group and by the chosen ferroaxial-axis component. For basal-plane strain, the leading field is linear in orthorhombic systems, quadratic in tetragonal systems, and cubic in trigonal and hexagonal systems. Cubic parent groups further split into two classes: cubic-I groups, $23$ and $m\bar{3}$, allow linear full-strain fields for selected axes, whereas cubic-II groups, $432$, $\bar{4}3m$, and $m\bar{3}m$, forbid linear fields and require quadratic or cubic strain combinations depending on the selected axis. In trigonal systems, the basal-plane deviatoric strain with signed amplitude $\varepsilon_{\rm u}$ and principal-axis angle $θ$ gives the single-axis field $h\propto\varepsilon_{\rm u}^3\sin6θ$. First-principles calculations for the trigonal ferroaxial compound Na$_2$BaMg(PO$_4$)$_2$ verify both the predicted angular dependence and cubic strain scaling of the ferroaxial domain splitting, and fixed-strain atomic relaxations show strain-selected evolution from the para-axial structure. These results establish static homogeneous strain as a symmetry-allowed conjugate field for ferroaxial order and suggest a route to ferroaxial domain control through strain-field cooling.

</details>


### [155] [Phonon-Mediated Thermal Transport in Nanocrystalline Silicon Using Machine-Learning Interatomic Potentials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06470)
*Houssem Rezgui,Catalina Coll Benejam,Miguel Pruneda,Clivia M. Sotomayor Torres*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文开发了一种基于机器学习力场（MLIP）的框架，结合GAP和MACE模型与晶格动力学计算及非平衡分子动力学（NEMD），用于研究体相和纳米晶硅中的声子热输运，相较于经典势能模型（Stillinger-Weber和Tersoff）提供了更准确且内部自洽的描述。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在结构复杂材料中，晶界和界面无序会严重限制热耗散，理解其中的声子介导热输运是下一代电子和纳米机械器件的核心挑战。经典原子间势能虽能支持大尺度模拟，但其可迁移性（transferability）有限，导致振动性质和界面声子散射的计算不准确。

Method: 结合高斯近似势（Gaussian approximation potential, GAP）和多原子团簇展开（multi-atomic cluster expansion, MACE）两种机器学习原子间势能模型，与晶格动力学计算及非平衡分子动力学（non-equilibrium molecular dynamics, NEMD）相融合。在统一的Phonopy/Phono3py工作流中，利用MLIP导出的谐波和非谐波力常数（force constants）计算声子色散、寿命和晶格热导率。

Result: 在纳米晶硅中，NEMD模拟直接量化了与晶界相关的热边界电阻（thermal boundary resistance），并揭示了其对界面粗糙度及底层原子间描述的敏感性。与Stillinger-Weber和Tersoff势相比，MLIP对体相和界面声子输运提供了更准确且内部自洽的描述。

Conclusion: 本文所发展的基于机器学习力场的框架能够更精确地预测低维材料中的纳米尺度热输运行为，为下一代器件中的热管理设计提供了更具预测能力的建模工具。

Abstract: Understanding phonon-mediated heat transport in structurally complex materials remains a central challenge for next-generation electronic and nanomechanical devices, where grain boundaries and interfacial disorder strongly limit thermal dissipation. Although classical interatomic potentials enable large-scale simulations, their limited transferability can lead to inaccuracies in vibrational properties and interfacial phonon scattering. In this work, we develop a machine-learning based framework for modeling thermal transport in bulk and nanocrystalline silicon by combining Gaussian approximation potential (GAP) and multi-atomic cluster expansion (MACE) models with lattice-dynamical calculations and non-equilibrium molecular dynamics (NEMD). Harmonic and anharmonic force constants derived from machine-learning interatomic potentials (MLIPs) are used within a unified Phonopy/Phono3py workflow to compute phonon dispersions, lifetimes, and lattice thermal conductivity, providing an internally consistent description of vibrational properties. In nanocrystalline silicon, NEMD simulations directly quantify the thermal boundary resistance associated with grain boundaries and reveal its sensitivity to interfacial roughness and the underlying interatomic description. Compared with the Stillinger-Weber and Tersoff potentials, the MLIPs provide a more accurate and internally consistent description of bulk and interfacial phonon transport, enabling more predictive modeling of nanoscale thermal transport in low-dimensional materials.

### [156] [Shifted Poisson unfoldings and quantum anomalies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05918)
*Mauricio Corrêa,Simone Noja*

Main category: math.AG

TL;DR: 本文研究经典场论族在几何参数变化下可观测量的平坦平行输运及其量子化延续问题，针对转移泊松结构（shifted Poisson structures）族构造了泊松横向控制器（Poisson transverse controller），并分析了$ħ$进提升（$ħ$-adic lifting）中的输运反常（transport anomalies），最终在泊松西格玛模型（Poisson sigma model）中实现了无反常平坦输运的量子化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典场论族通常依赖于几何参数，核心问题是相应的经典可观测量是否能在参数空间上通过平坦平行输运（flat parallel transport）进行比较，以及这种比较能否在量子化（quantization）后依然保持。

Method: 针对转移泊松结构族，构造泊松横向控制器（Poisson transverse controller）$\mathbb U_π$——一种同伦稳定化子（homotopy stabilizer），用于编码保持泊松Maurer–Cartan元素到上同伦一致的横向对称性（transverse symmetries）。其平坦分裂（flat splittings）恰是横向转移泊松展开（transversal shifted Poisson unfoldings），作用于垂直对称性（vertical symmetries）、泊松上同调（Poisson cohomology）和局部形变理论（local deformation theory）。随后形式化$ħ$进提升问题，其二阶障碍类即为输运反常。该构造在星积（star-products）、BV可观测量（BV observables）、因子化代数（factorization algebras）和AKSZ理论中实现。

Result: 在泊松西格玛模型中，平坦输运的无反常量子化使得Cattaneo–Felder/Kontsevich边界乘积（boundary product）在参数空间上成为水平的（horizontal）。

Conclusion: 为转移泊松结构族建立了平坦平行输运及其量子化异常的通用框架，并在多种量子化形式中得到了具体实现。

Abstract: Families of classical field theories often depend on geometric parameters. A basic question is whether the corresponding classical observables can be compared by flat parallel transport, and whether this comparison survives quantization. We study this problem for families of shifted Poisson structures. To such a family we attach a Poisson transverse controller $\mathbb U_π$, a homotopy stabilizer encoding transverse symmetries which preserve the Poisson Maurer--Cartan element up to coherent homotopy. Its flat splittings are precisely transversal shifted Poisson unfoldings, and they act on vertical symmetries, Poisson cohomology and local deformation theory. We then formulate the $\hslash$-adic lifting problem for quantized objects; its degree-two obstruction classes are the transport anomalies. The construction is realized for star-products, BV observables, factorization algebras and AKSZ theories. For the Poisson sigma model, anomaly-free quantization of the flat transport makes the Cattaneo--Felder/Kontsevich boundary product horizontal over the parameter space.

### [157] [Motivic quasimap wall-crossing for Grassmannians](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06189)
*Siddarth Kannan,Terry Dekun Song*

Main category: math.AG

TL;DR: 本文证明了格拉斯曼簇 $\mathbb{G}(r, N)$ 上 $\varepsilon$-稳定拟映射（quasimap）模空间欧拉示性数（作为虚拟混合霍奇结构）的壁穿越公式，并通过对幂和对称函数进行显式 $q$-形变，定义了将稳定映射模空间的生成函数映到稳定拟映射模空间生成函数的 $\mathbb{Q}$-代数自同构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 建立稳定映射模空间与 $\varepsilon$-稳定拟映射模空间之间欧拉示性数的壁穿越关系，并统一不同 $\varepsilon$ 参数下的模空间理论，特别是将稳定映射空间与 Marian–Oprea–Pandharipande 稳定商（stable quotients）模空间通过 $\varepsilon \to 0$ 极限联系起来。

Method: 利用相对 Quot 概形（relative Quot scheme）的几何结构建立拟映射空间与加权稳定映射模空间之间的联系，并借助对称函数论（symmetric function theory）推导壁穿越公式。关键工具是定义 $\mathbb{Q}$-代数自同构，它通过幂和对称函数的显式 $q$-形变（$q$-deformation）实现生成函数的变换。

Result: 得到了格拉斯曼簇上 $\varepsilon$-稳定拟映射模空间欧拉示性数（作为虚拟混合霍奇结构）的壁穿越公式；该公式在 $\varepsilon \to 0$ 极限下将稳定映射空间与稳定商模空间联系起来；构建了对称函数环上的 $\mathbb{Q}$-代数自同构，它将稳定映射模空间的 $\mathbb{S}_n$-等变欧拉示性数生成函数变换为稳定拟映射模空间的相应生成函数。

Conclusion: 通过对称函数论和相对 Quot 概形的几何方法，成功建立了格拉斯曼簇上拟映射模空间欧拉示性数的壁穿越公式，统一了不同 $\varepsilon$ 参数下的模空间理论，并揭示了稳定映射、稳定拟映射与稳定商空间之间的结构关系。

Abstract: We prove a wall-crossing formula for the Euler characteristics, considered as virtual mixed Hodge structures, of moduli spaces of $\varepsilon$-stable quasimaps to the Grassmannian $\mathbb{G}(r, N)$. For each $\varepsilon > 0$, we define a $\mathbb{Q}$-algebra automorphism of the ring of symmetric functions which takes the generating function for the $\mathbb{S}_n$-equivariant Euler characteristics of the moduli spaces of stable maps $\overline{\mathcal{M}}_{g, n}(\mathbb{G}(r, N), d)$ to the corresponding generating function for Toda's moduli spaces of $\varepsilon$-stable quasimaps $\overline{\mathcal{Q}}_{g, n}^{\varepsilon}(\mathbb{G}(r, N), d)$. The automorphism is given by explicit $q$-deformations of the power sum symmetric functions. The $\varepsilon \to 0$ limit of our formula exchanges the spaces of stable maps and the Marian--Oprea--Pandharipande moduli spaces of stable quotients. Our proof uses the geometry of relative Quot schemes to relate the quasimap spaces to moduli spaces of weighted stable maps, for which we obtain wall-crossing formulas via symmetric function theory.

### [158] [Topological Dynamics of Pullback Maps on Full Shifts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06423)
*Alonso Castillo-Ramirez,Luguis De Los Santos Baños*

Main category: math.DS

TL;DR: 本文研究由群自同态 $φ: G \to G$ 诱导的拉回映射 $φ^*: A^G \to A^G$ 的拓扑动力学性质。在一维情形 $G=\mathbb Z$ 下，证明了 $φ_k^*$ 等度连续与共限敏感的精确二分性；在可数群情形下，将等度连续性、共限敏感性等性质等价于群元素的最终周期性（eventual periodicity）；并进一步刻画了伯努利测度保持性与强混合性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 广义元胞自动机（generalized cellular automaton）是经典元胞自动机的重要推广，而由群自同态诱导的拉回映射是一类典型例子。本文旨在系统研究该类映射的拓扑动力学性质，尤其是等度连续性（equicontinuity）、敏感性与混合性等核心概念在不同群结构下的刻画。

Method: 采用拓扑动力系统分析方法，分别针对一维整数群 $G=\mathbb Z$（乘性自同态 $φ_k(n)=kn$）和一般可数群两种情形，利用群元素的最终周期性条件，建立拉回映射的等度连续性、共限敏感性（cofinite sensitivity）与混合性等性质的充要条件。同时结合伯努利测度（Bernoulli measure）分析概率测度下的保持性与强混合性。

Result: 在一维情形下，$φ_k^*$ 等度连续当且仅当 $k\in\{-1,0,1\}$，否则为共限敏感。在完整移位空间（full shift）上虽因固定恒等坐标不满足传递性（transitivity），但在自然不变分量上的限制恰好在 $k\notin\{-1,0,1\}$ 时拓扑混合（topologically mixing）。在可数群上，$φ^*$ 等度连续等价于 $G$ 中每个元素在 $φ$ 下最终周期；非最终周期元素的存在等价于共限敏感性与无等度连续点。最后，在穿孔构型空间（punctured configuration space）上，伯努利测度保持性与强混合性可由 $φ$ 的单射性和最终周期性刻画。

Conclusion: 本文完整刻画了拉回映射 $φ^*$ 在不同群结构和自同态下的拓扑动力学行为，建立了等度连续性、敏感性、混合性与群元素最终周期性之间的等价关系，并拓展至概率测度性质，为广义元胞自动机的动力学分类提供了基础性结论。

Abstract: Let $G$ be a group, let $A$ be a finite alphabet, and let $φ: G \to G$ be an endomorphism. We study the topological dynamics of the pullback map $φ^* : A^G \to A^G$, given by $φ^*(x)=x\circφ$, a canonical example of a generalized cellular automaton. In the one-dimensional case, where $G=\mathbb Z$ and $φ_k(n)=kn$, we prove a sharp dichotomy: $φ_k^*$ is equicontinuous precisely for $k\in\{-1,0,1\}$, and cofinitely sensitive otherwise. Although the fixed identity coordinate prevents transitivity on the full shift, the restriction to the natural invariant components is topologically mixing exactly when $k\notin\{-1,0,1\}$. We then extend the analysis to countable groups, showing that $φ^*$ is equicontinuous if and only if every element of $G$ is eventually periodic under $φ$, while the existence of a non-eventually-periodic element is equivalent to cofinite sensitivity and to the absence of equicontinuous points. Finally, we characterize Bernoulli measure preservation and strong mixing on the punctured configuration space in terms of injectivity and eventual periodicity.

</details>

### [159] [Dynamical crossover from motor-dominated to drag-dominated transport in a minimal active transport network](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05827)
*Kazuhiko Mitsuhashi*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个最小活性输运网络模型，研究马达驱动输运与滑移相关耗散阻力之间的竞争关系。通过扫描滑移系数（γ_Slip）和马达活性参数（α_m），发现增大γ_Slip会显著抑制平均输运速度，而马达结合比例几乎不变；马达机械活性在高γ_Slip区仍然保持，但输运主导权从马达主导（R≈1.69）向拖曳主导（R≈1.01）发生动力学交叉。该模型为理解主动力产生持续存在但净输运被耗散阻力抑制的现象提供了简洁的物理图像。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 马达驱动的细胞内输运通常用马达活性来描述，但宏观输运还取决于马达产生的力如何有效地转化为相干运动。受细胞质环流（cytoplasmic streaming）现象的启发，本文旨在构建一个最小模型，以分离马达活性、阻力和输运输出三者之间的关系，探究活性力产生与有效耗散阻力之间的竞争机制。

Method: 构建了一个最小活性输运网络模型，其中马达驱动输运与有效滑移相关耗散阻力（slip-related dissipative resistance）相互竞争。对滑移系数（γ_Slip）和马达活性参数（α_m）进行系统扫描，每个条件取三个独立随机种子，分析其对平均输运速度、马达结合比例、平均负载和马达力的影响，并通过马达主导比（motor dominance ratio, R）量化主导权转变。

Result: 增大γ_Slip显著抑制平均输运速度，而马达结合分数几乎不变；高γ_Slip区平均负载和马达力仍保持有限值，表明马达仍保持机械活性。随γ_Slip增大，输运速度对α_m的依赖逐渐消失：马达主导比从R≈1.69降至R≈1.01，对应速度差从约1.9 μm/s降至约0.003 μm/s。

Conclusion: 结果表明存在从马达主导（motor-dominated）输运到拖曳主导（drag-dominated）输运的动力学交叉。该最小模型提供了一个紧凑的物理场景：活性力产生持续存在，但其对净输运的贡献被增大的有效耗散阻力所抑制。

Abstract: Motor-driven intracellular transport is often described in terms of motor activity, but macroscopic transport also depends on how effectively motor-generated force is converted into coherent motion. Motivated by cytoplasmic streaming, a minimal active transport network is examined in which motor-driven transport competes with an effective slip-related dissipative resistance. The model is not intended as a quantitative reconstruction of Nitella cytoplasmic streaming, but as a minimal system for isolating the relation between motor activity, resistance, and transport output.
  A controlled scan over $γ_{\mathrm{Slip}}$ and $α_m$, with three independent seeds per condition, shows that increasing $γ_{\mathrm{Slip}}$ strongly suppresses mean transport speed while leaving the motor-bound fraction nearly unchanged. The mean load and motor force remain finite in the high-$γ_{\mathrm{Slip}}$ regime, indicating that motors remain mechanically active even when transport is suppressed. The dependence of transport speed on $α_m$ progressively disappears with increasing $γ_{\mathrm{Slip}}$: the motor dominance ratio decreases from $R\approx1.69$ to $R\approx1.01$, and the corresponding velocity difference decreases from $\sim1.9~μ\mathrm{m/s}$ to $\sim0.003~μ\mathrm{m/s}$.
  These results indicate a dynamical crossover from motor-dominated to drag-dominated transport. The minimal model provides a compact physical scenario in which active force generation persists while its contribution to net transport is suppressed by increased effective dissipative resistance.

</details>


### [160] [Spatially heterogeneous noise restructures flocking into geometry-locked and vortex states](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05870)
*Ankush Semwal,Mahak Poonia,Pintu Patra*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过扩展Vicsek模型（Vicsek model），在活性物质（active matter）中引入一个圆形无噪声区域与周围有噪声环境构成的对比结构，发现了三种不同的动力学状态：全局群聚（global flocking）、几何锁定运动（geometry-locked motion）和涡旋运动（vortical motion），并展示了空间有序-无序调制可作为调控活性物质集体行为的通用策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解活性物质在空间异质（spatially heterogeneous）环境中如何维持稳健的集体运动（collective motion），这对于生物系统功能与智能活性物质设计都至关重要。

Method: 扩展Vicsek模型，设置一个圆形无噪声区域（non-noisy region）被有噪声环境（noisy environment）包围，通过调节周围噪声强度来研究系统的集体动力学行为，并进一步将环境扩展至多个无噪声区域。

Result: 发现了三个不同的动力学状态：低噪声时的全局群聚、中等噪声时与模拟边界对齐的几何锁定运动、高噪声时无噪声区域内的涡旋运动。在多区域扩展中，几何锁定状态可产生方向耦合（directional coupling），涡旋模式则导致区域间的反铁磁序（antiferromagnetic order）。

Conclusion: 空间有序与无序的调制可作为引导活性物质的强大且通用的策略，这一发现与近期在图案化景观（patterned landscapes）中活性粒子的实验观察一致。

Abstract: Spatially heterogeneous environments continually challenge the ability of active matter to sustain coherent collective motion. Understanding how collective motion remains robust under changing environments is central to both the functioning of biological systems and the design of smart active matter. Here, we extend the Vicsek model to include a circular non-noisy region surrounded by a noisy environment - a configuration in which the noise difference sets up a contrast in local directional order between the two regions. We find that, as the surrounding noise is increased, the system passes through three distinct dynamical regimes: (i) conventional global flocking at low noise; (ii) geometry-locked motion, aligned with simulation boundaries, at intermediate noise; and (iii) vortical motion within the non-noisy region at high noise. Extending the environment to multiple non-noisy regions, we find that the geometry-locked regime can develop a directional coupling, while the vortex mode leads to antiferromagnetic order between the regions. Taken together, our results demonstrate that the spatial modulation of order and disorder offers a powerful and generic strategy for steering active matter, aligning with recent experimental observations of active particles in patterned landscapes.

### [161] [From Active to Odd to Smart Matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06051)
*Olivier Dauchot*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文提出了一条从活性物质（active matter）到奇弹性物质（odd matter）再到智能物质（smart matter）的统一发展轨迹，沿着凝聚态物理的气-液-固传统进程和从自发集体动力学到任务驱动功能性的范式转变这两条交织主轴，论证学习可能作为一种特殊的涌现形式，在物理领域替代传统的控制观念。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 活性物质的研究已深刻重塑了对远离平衡态（far from equilibrium）的集体态的理解，而奇弹性（odd elasticity）和非互易机械耦合（nonreciprocal mechanical couplings）的发现进一步将这一思想拓展到类固体活性系统。同时，群体机器人（swarm robotics）、可编程超材料（programmable metamaterials）和学习算法（learning algorithms）的进展催生了集体行为和力学响应不再由设计固定，而是通过适应、优化和学习实现功能目标的新前沿。本文旨在整合这些分散的发展，提出一个统一的视角。

Method: 本文采用展望（Perspective）综述的方法，沿两条交织主轴组织分析：一是凝聚态物理（condensed matter）传统的气-液-固（gas-liquid-solid）演变进程；二是从自发集体动力学（spontaneous collective dynamics）到任务驱动功能性（task-driven functionality）的范式转变。通过这条从活性到奇弹性再到智能物质的轨迹，梳理涌现原理、概念转变和开放挑战。

Result: 研究指出，将微观尺度的能量注入可以在宏观尺度上产生有序、集体运动（collective motion）和异常力学响应。奇弹性和非互易机械耦合揭示了具有非保守弹性响应（nonconservative elastic response）的材料。群体机器人、可编程超材料和学习的进展使得集体行为和力学响应能够适应、优化和学习以实现功能目标。

Conclusion: 本文认为，学习可能扮演一种特殊的涌现（emergence）形式，至少在物理学领域，这种涌现视角可以有效替代传统的控制（control）观念。沿活性-奇弹性-智能物质的轨迹，仍存在重要的开放挑战和概念转变有待深入探索。

Abstract: The study of active matter has reshaped our understanding of collective states of matter far from equilibrium by proving that energy pumped into the microscopic scale leads to order on the macroscopic scale, collective motion, and anomalous mechanical responses. More recently, the discovery of odd elasticity and nonreciprocal mechanical couplings has extended these ideas to solid-like active systems, revealing materials with nonconservative elastic response. Simultaneously, innovative developments in swarm robotics , programmable metamaterials , and learning algorithms have led to the emergence of a new frontier in which collective behavior and mechanical response are no longer fixed by design, but adapted, optimized, and learned toward functional goals. This Perspective proposes a unifying trajectory, from active to odd to smart matter, organized along two intertwined axes: the traditional gas--liquid--solid progression of condensed matter, and the more recentparadigm shift from spontaneous collective dynamics to task-driven functionality. We try to highlight emerging principles, conceptual shifts, and open challenges that come along this trajectory, and argue that learning may play the role of a specific form of emergence, which could advantageously replace the more traditional view of control, at least in the realm of physics.

</details>


### [162] [Robust Topologically Protected Edge Transport in Doubly Chiral Active Particles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06193)
*Tristan Edwards,Maxim Nikolaev,Jaime Agudo-Canalejo*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过理论、模拟与实验，提出了一类新的活性粒子——双旋手性活性布朗粒子（dcABPs），其双旋性源于内在角速度与平动-转动耦合的共存；当两种手性源符号相反且内在旋转弱于平动-转动耦合时，出现拓扑保护的边界输运模式，且在拐角处无反散射。实验上通过构建双旋振动机器人（vibrobot）实现了原理验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有手性活性粒子（如简单手性ABPs、手性活性杆或自对齐手性ABPs）虽能产生边界流或边界诱导输运，但存在拐角背散射或缺乏边界诱导输运等局限。因此，本文旨在设计一种新型活性粒子，使其能够实现拓扑保护的（topologically protected）边界输运，即在边界上沿特定方向无损耗传播，且在拐角处不发生背散射（backscattering）。

Method: 采用理论分析、数值模拟与实验相结合的方法。理论上定义双旋手性活性布朗粒子（dcABPs）模型，包含内在角速度（intrinsic angular velocity）与平动-转动耦合（translation-rotation coupling）两个手性来源；通过机械详模型（mechanically detailed model）揭示后者源于垂直于自推进方向的不对称摩擦分布。实验上构建双旋振动机器人（vibrobot）实现原理验证。

Result: 当两个手性源符号相反且内在旋转弱于平动-转动耦合时，拓扑保护模式在直边界、曲边界以及粒子间相互作用过程中均出现。与简单手性ABPs的边缘流（edge currents）对比显示其不具备边界诱导输运；与手性活性杆或自对齐手性ABPs对比显示其虽具有边界诱导输运但在拐角处发生背散射，缺乏拓扑保护。

Conclusion: 双旋手性活性布朗粒子（dcABPs）能够实现拓扑保护的边界输运，在拐角处无反散射，这区别于已有的各类手性活性粒子体系。该工作为活性物质中拓扑输运行为的设计提供了新途径。

Abstract: Using theory, simulation, and experiment, we introduce a new class of active particle which we term doubly chiral active Brownian particles (dcABPs), which show robust topologically protected transport along boundaries without backscattering at corners. Their double chirality stems from the coexistence of an intrinsic angular velocity, which can cause rotation independently of translation, and a translation-rotation coupling inducing cross-alignment to the instantaneous velocity, which causes rotation only concomitantly with translation. A mechanically detailed model shows that the latter effect can arise from an asymmetric friction distribution in the direction perpendicular to the self-propulsion direction. We show that topologically protected modes emerge when the two sources of chirality have opposite sign and the intrinsic rotation is weaker than the translation-rotation coupling. In the deterministic limit, we characterize the emergence of these modes not only along straight boundaries, but also along curved boundaries and during interparticle interactions. We provide a proof-of-principle experimental realization by building a doubly chiral vibrobot. While setting the work into context, we moreover show that the topologically protected boundary-induced transport of dcABPs stands in contrast to the edge currents observed for simple chiral ABPs, which we demonstrate are not associated with boundary-induced transport, as well as to those observed for chiral active rods or self-aligning chiral ABPs, which we show to be associated with boundary-induced transport but to backscatter at corners, implying lack of topological protection.

</details>


### [163] [Uncovering Collective Modes Underlying the Giant Dielectric Response of Ferroelectric Nematic Liquid Crystals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06257)
*Kazuma Nakajima,Hirokazu Kamifuji,Masanori Ozaki,Hirotsugu Kikuchi,Kenjiro Fukuda*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本研究通过介电谱（dielectric spectroscopy）揭示了铁电向列型液晶（FNLC）的巨介电响应并非单一过程，而是由两种不同弛豫模式叠加产生：低频软模（soft mode）与高频Goldstone-like模，并系统分析了温度、电场、样品厚度和取向层的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 铁电向列型液晶表现出异常的介电和机电响应，但其巨介电响应背后的集体模式（collective modes）尚不清楚，亟待阐明。

Method: 采用介电谱技术，结合温度、电场、样品厚度和取向层的系统依赖性分析，对FNLC的介电响应进行表征。

Result: 发现巨介电响应源于两个不同弛豫过程的叠加：低频模式呈现软模行为，与短轴分子旋转相关；高频模式对应有效横向极化分量绕指向矢旋转的Goldstone-like相位位移。

Conclusion: FNLC的巨介电响应反映了具有不同对称性和恢复力的多种集体极化动力学，为极性向列流体介电谱的解析提供了理论框架。

Abstract: Ferroelectric nematic liquid crystals (FNLCs) are polar fluids in which spontaneous polarization coexists with nematic orientational order, giving rise to unusual dielectric and electromechanical responses. However, the collective modes underlying their giant dielectric response remain unclear. Here, we show that this response originates from the superposition of two distinct relaxation modes rather than a single process. Dielectric spectroscopy reveals that the low-frequency mode exhibits soft-mode-like behavior associated with short-axis molecular rotation, whereas the high-frequency mode corresponds to a Goldstone-like phase displacement of an effective transverse polarization component rotating around the director. These assignments are supported by systematic analyses of temperature, electric-field, cell-thickness, and alignment-layer dependences. Our results demonstrate that the giant dielectric response of ferroelectric nematics reflects multiple collective polarization dynamics with different symmetries and restoring forces, providing a framework for interpreting dielectric spectra in polar nematic fluids.

### [164] [Dynamical Simulation of Membrane Bending by Flexible Protein Assemblies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06378)
*Samuel L. Foley,Margaret E. Johnson*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种将柔性蛋白质晶格（flexible protein lattice）与Helfrich膜（Helfrich membrane）耦合的傅里叶空间过阻尼模拟方法，重点研究网格蛋白（clathrin）晶格的力学特性，揭示了弯曲刚度（flexural rigidity）随晶格结构变化的有效硬化（effective stiffening）效应，并验证了模型与理论预期的吻合性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 膜变形蛋白质晶格在胞吞作用（endocytosis）和病毒出芽（viral budding）等关键生物过程中发挥重要作用，但大规模膜重塑事件在模拟中难以达到所需的时间和空间尺度。

Method: 建立了一个柔性蛋白质晶格与Helfrich膜耦合的模型，在过阻尼（over-damped） regime下于傅里叶空间（Fourier space）进行传播；采用屈曲方法（buckling methods）测量材料属性，定量分析网格蛋白模型晶格的抗弯刚度随粗粒化势能函数（coarse-grained potential energy function）力常数的变化。

Result: 比较了屈曲法测得的抗弯刚度与使用Helfrich-like弯曲能项模拟球形网格蛋白外壳（spherical clathrin coat）时观察到的有效刚度，发现弯曲刚度的解释随蛋白质外壳结构而变化，导致外壳生长时出现有效硬化；模拟膜的张力引起网格蛋白外壳几何形状的变化与理论预期一致。

Conclusion: 常用的Helfrich-like近似需谨慎应用，因为它可能根据所假设的解释高估组装晶格的刚度；展示了将刚性体反应-扩散（rigid-body reaction-diffusion）组装的结构（使用NERDSS模拟包）转移至该柔性膜耦合动力学框架中的新代码，并应用于膜结合的HIV-1未成熟Gag晶格（membrane-bound HIV-1 immature Gag lattice）。

Abstract: Membrane-deforming protein lattices play a key role in essential and pathogenic biological processes, including endocytosis and viral budding. Attaining the necessary length- and time-scales in simulation can be difficult for such large-scale membrane remodeling events. We present a model of a flexible protein lattice coupled to a Helfrich membrane propagated in Fourier space in the over-damped regime. We focus primarily on membrane-bound clathrin lattices, an essential part of the endocytic machinery. We quantify the material properties of our clathrin model lattices using buckling methods to measure the flexural rigidity as it varies with force constants of the coarse-grained potential energy function. By comparing this flexural rigidity to the effective rigidity observed when modeling the bending energy of a spherical clathrin coat using a Helfrich-like bending energy term, we show how the interpretation of the bending rigidity changes with the structure of the protein coat, resulting in an effective stiffening as the coat grows. This relatively common approximation thus must be applied with care, as it can over-estimate the stiffness of assembled lattices depending on the interpretation assumed. We validate our model by verifying that the tension of our simulated membrane results in changes to the geometry of the clathrin coat consistent with theoretical expectations. We conclude by demonstrating our newly available code for transferring structures assembled via rigid-body reaction-diffusion (using the NERDSS simulation package) into our flexible membrane-coupled dynamical framework, applying it to the membrane-bound HIV-1 immature Gag lattice.

### [165] [Dimensional Crossover of Thermal Transport in Nanoconfined Liquids Driven by the Interplay of Quasi-One-Dimensional Structure and Wall Dissipation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06448)
*Kenta Hisamoto,Yusei Kobayashi,Takahiro Ikeda,Eiji Yamamoto,Masashi Yamakawa*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究通过分子动力学模拟，发现纳米受限液体（nanoconfined liquids）的轴向热导率存在由管径控制的交叉行为：在单列（single-file）和单壳层（single-shell）状态下，长度依赖性热输运可维持较长管长；而一旦形成混合壳层（mixed-shell）或多层堆积（multilayer packing），该依赖性被强烈截断或接近饱和。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管已知纳米受限会改变液体结构并引发界面耗散（interfacial dissipation），可能导致准一维输运或过阻尼声弛豫（overdamped sound relaxation），但长度依赖的热输运在何种条件下持续存在仍不清楚。

Method: 采用分子动力学模拟（molecular dynamics simulations），对封装在碳纳米管（carbon nanotubes）中的单原子液态氩（monatomic liquid argon）进行研究，系统地改变纳米管的半径和长度。

Result: 发现管径控制的交叉行为：单列和单壳层状态下，长度依赖的轴向热导率可在长管中持续；混合壳层或多层堆积状态下则被强烈截断或饱和。该交叉伴随清晰的类声学轴向模式（acoustic-like axial modes）消失以及壁-液体摩擦（wall-liquid friction）增强。

Conclusion: 纳米管半径通过耦合受限液体结构与壁诱导耗散，决定了长度依赖的热输运是否持续或被截断。

Abstract: Heat transport in nanoconfined liquids can deviate from ordinary Fourier behavior because confinement alters liquid structure and interfacial dissipation. Although such changes may lead to quasi-one-dimensional transport or overdamped sound relaxation, the conditions under which length-dependent transport persists remain unclear. Here we use molecular dynamics simulations of monatomic liquid argon confined in carbon nanotubes with systematically varied radii and lengths. We find a radius-controlled crossover: length-dependent axial thermal conductivity persists over long tube lengths in single-file and single-shell states, but is strongly truncated or nearly saturated once mixed-shell or multilayer packing develops. This crossover is accompanied by the loss of clear acoustic-like axial modes and enhanced wall--liquid friction. Thus, tube radius controls whether length-dependent heat transport persists or is truncated by coupling confined-liquid structure to wall-induced dissipation.

### [166] [Sedimentation equilibrium and gravity dependent stiffness coefficients of colloidal hard-spheres](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06510)
*Luis G. MacDowell,Eva G. Noya*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在可调浮力质量条件下，对胶体硬球体系进行计算机模拟（computer simulation），系统考察重力对晶体-熔体界面刚度系数的影响。

Result: 发现长期存在的晶体-熔体刚度系数差异可归因于一个此前未被认识的重力依赖性贡献。

Conclusion: 该重力效应是外场（external field）影响任意界面刚度系数这一更一般性结果的一个具体实例。

Abstract: Spherical colloids with harsh repulsive forces have long been used as experimental analogs of the hard sphere model, with demonstrated good agreement with computer simulations for bulk and structural properties of the fluid, glass and crystal phases. However, an enigmatic discrepancy remains for the crystal-melt stiffness coefficient. Here we perform computer simulations of colloidal hard spheres under tunable buoyant mass and show that the long-standing discrepancy can be traced to a hitherto unrecognized gravity dependent contribution of the stiffness coefficient. This effect is one practical realization of a more general result for the external field dependence of stiffness coefficients of arbitrary interfaces.

### [167] [Magnon-Mediated Superconductivity in a 2D Itinerant Ferromagnet with Weak Easy-plane Magnetic Anisotropy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05754)
*Vladimir Calvera,Heqiu Li,Yijie Wang,B. Andrei Bernevig,Andrey V. Chubukov*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文研究二维铁磁相中由磁振子（magnon）介导的等自旋费米子配对机制，发现易平面磁各向异性（easy-plane magnetic anisotropy）可破坏SU(2)对称性，从而产生p波配对吸引相互作用，并推导出耦合常数λ_p作为各向异性强度和铁磁相变接近程度的标度函数，预言在铁磁相变附近可达到显著的超导转变温度T_c。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 受自旋和谷极化石墨烯多层膜中的四分之一金属（quarter-metal）态超导电性实验观测的启发，作者试图理解铁磁相中是否存在配对机制及其物理本源。

Method: 基于Hubbard相互作用的单谷二维巡游电子铁磁模型，在自旋SU(2)对称情形下分析磁振子介导的等自旋配对；随后引入易平面磁各向异性Ω₀以破坏SU(2)对称性，推导并标度化p波配对的耦合常数λ_p。

Result: 在自旋SU(2)对称模型中，磁振子介导的等自旋费米子配对相互作用在T=0时为零；引入易平面磁各向异性Ω₀后，产生了等自旋p波配对吸引作用。耦合常数λ_p在铁磁相内部由Ω₀/E_F参量化地小，但在靠近铁磁相变时被增强至O(1)量级，与Ω₀/E_F大小无关。

Conclusion: 该机制可在铁磁序参量接近零时产生显著的超导转变温度T_c，其峰值位于铁磁性起始点附近。

Abstract: Motivated by recent observations of superconductivity in a quarter-metal state of spin- and valley- polarized graphene multilayers, we investigate pairing within a ferromagnetic phase of a single-valley model of itinerant two-dimensional (2D) electrons with Hubbard-type interaction and no artificial high-energy cutoff. In 2D, the Stoner transition is first-order into a fully-polarized state wherein the only gapless collective excitations are transverse magnons. We find that in a spin-SU(2) symmetric model, this magnon-mediated pairing interaction between equal-spin fermions vanishes at $T=0$. We show that a small easy-plane magnetic anisotropy $Ω_0 \ll E_F$, where $E_F$ is the Fermi energy, breaks the SU(2) symmetry and generates an attractive interaction for equal-spin $p-$wave pairing. We explicitly derive the corresponding coupling constant $λ_p$ as the scaling function of both the relative strength of the easy-plane anisotropy, $Ω_0/E_F$, and the proximity to the ferromagnetic transition. While $λ_p$ is parametrically small in $Ω_0/E_F$ deep inside the ferromagnetic phase, it becomes enhanced near the ferromagnetic transition, reaching order unity regardless of how small $Ω_0/E_F$ is. This mechanism yields a sizable $T_c$, peaked near the onset of ferromagnetism.

</details>


### [168] [Chiral-Structured Superconductors TrX4 (Tr = Rh, Ir; X = Ge, Si): A Platform for Mixed-Parity Pairing and Topological States](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05881)
*Zhenhai Yu,Yunguan Ye,Yuwei Zhou,Chaoyang Chu,Congcong Le,Lin Wu,Jian Yuan,Tong Shi,Qingxin Dong,Jinggeng Zhao,Wei Xia,Xiangqi Liu,Xia Wang,Bosen Wang,Jinguang Cheng,Yanhang Ma,Xianxin Wu,Xiangang Wan,Huiqiu Yuan,Yanfeng Guo*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文报道了三种在高压下合成的具有手性结构（空间群P3121）的超导体RhGe4、IrGe4和IrSi4，其超导转变温度Tc分别约为1.6 K、1.1 K和2.5 K。通过原子分辨率的Cs校正扫描透射电子显微镜（STEM）直接确认了其手性结构，克服了传统衍射方法的模糊性。这些材料呈现第二类超导性（type-II superconductivity），自旋-轨道耦合（SOC）的增强导致了混合宇称配对（mixed parity pairing）的出现。计算还揭示了费米面附近受对称性保护的Weyl点，该点对SOC具有鲁棒性。这项工作不仅扩展了手性结构超导体家族，也展示了STEM在直接确定手性晶体结构中的不可或缺作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 手性结构（chiral-structured）超导体通过宇称混合（parity-mixing）机制促进非常规超导，然而目前已知的块体手性结构超导体数量有限，部分原因在于难以直接确定其原子尺度手性。本研究旨在合成新的手性结构超导体，并探索直接确定手性结构的实验方法。

Method: 在高压条件下合成了三种化合物RhGe4、IrGe4和IrSi4。采用原子分辨率Cs校正扫描透射电子显微镜（STEM）结合X射线衍射表征，直接确认其手性结构（空间群P3121）。通过电输运和磁性测量表征超导性质，并结合第一性原理计算分析电子结构。

Result: 三种材料的超导转变温度Tc分别为约1.6 K、1.1 K和2.5 K，均表现为第二类超导性。STEM实空间成像直接确认了P3121手性空间群，克服了传统衍射方法的模糊性。自旋-轨道耦合（SOC）的增强导致混合宇称配对的出现。计算显示费米面附近存在受对称性保护的Weyl点，且该拓扑特征对SOC具有鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 本研究不仅扩展了手性结构超导体的家族，还证明了STEM在直接确定手性晶体结构中的不可或缺作用。这些材料为探索结构手性、自旋-轨道耦合、混合宇称超导与拓扑量子现象之间的相互作用提供了一个洁净的平台。

Abstract: Chiral-structured superconductors, with simultaneous broken mirror and inversion symmetries, promote unconventional superconductivity through parity-mixing mechanisms. Yet a few bulk chiral-structured superconductors are known, partly due to the difficulty in directly determining their atomic-scale chirality. Here we report three chiral-structured superconductors, , RhGe4, IrGe4, and IrSi4, synthesized under high pressure, with Tc values of about 1.6 K, 1.1 K, and 2.5 K, respectively.Using atomic resolution Cs-corrected scanning transmission electron microscopy (STEM) combined with X-ray diffraction characterizations, we directly confirm their chiral structure (space group P3121). This real space imaging approach overcomes ambiguities in traditional diffraction based methods. These materials exhibit type-II superconductivity, and the enhancement of spin-orbit coupling (SOC) leads to the emergence of mixed parity pairing. Calculations also reveal symmetry protected Weyl points near the Fermi level, which is robust against the SOC. Our work not only expands the family of chiral-structured superconductors but also demonstrates the indispensable role of STEM in directly determining chiral crystal structures. These materials thus offer a clean platform to explore the interplay among structural chirality, SOC, mixed parity superconductivity, and topological quantum phenomena.

### [169] [Microscopic theory of the lower critical field in superconducting thin-film strips](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05890)
*Takayuki Kubo*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文通过求解二维 Usadel 方程，从微观理论出发计算了窄超导薄膜条的下临界场 \(B_{c1}\)，无需引入唯象涡旋核心截断，并发现涡旋自能高于标准的 Pearl–London 估计，且无法用单一宽度无关的 London 对数形式表示。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准 Pearl–London 估计需要引入一个唯象的涡旋核心截断（vortex-core cutoff），因为 London 理论无法分辨涡旋核心结构。本文旨在建立一个无需截断的微观理论，以更准确地预测窄超导薄膜条（narrow superconducting thin-film strip）在垂直磁场（perpendicular magnetic field）中的下临界场 \(B_{c1}\)。

Method: 通过求解薄膜平面内二维 Usadel 方程（Usadel equations）建立微观理论，将外加场直接纳入规范不变动量（gauge-invariant momentum）中。在固定磁场下计算自洽的涡旋解与 Meissner 解，并通过两者的 Gibbs 自由能差（Gibbs-energy difference）得到 \(B_{c1}\)。计算直接解析涡旋核心及其有限宽度形变，无需引入截断参数。

Result: 计算得到的涡旋自能（vortex self-energy）高于朴素 Pearl–London 估计值，且一般无法用一个单一宽度无关的 London 对数（London logarithm）形式来表征。

Conclusion: 该微观理论适用于任意 \(T < T_c\) 的温度范围，为预测超导纳米条（superconducting nanostrips）及相关薄膜器件中的 \(B_{c1}\) 提供了微观基础。

Abstract: The lower critical field \(B_{c1}\) of a narrow superconducting thin-film strip sets the thermodynamic scale for vortex-free operation in a perpendicular magnetic field. The standard Pearl--London estimate requires a phenomenological vortex-core cutoff, because the London theory does not resolve the core. We formulate a microscopic theory for a dirty strip by solving the two-dimensional Usadel equations in the film plane, with the applied field included directly in the gauge-invariant momentum. Self-consistent vortex and Meissner solutions are computed at fixed field, and \(B_{c1}\) is obtained from their Gibbs-energy difference. The calculation resolves the vortex core and its finite-width deformation without introducing a cutoff. The resulting vortex self-energy is larger than the naive Pearl--London estimate and cannot, in general, be represented by a London logarithm with a single width-independent cutoff. The formulation applies at any \(T<T_c\) and provides a microscopic basis for predicting \(B_{c1}\) in superconducting nanostrips and related thin-film devices.

</details>


### [170] [Decoupling Josephson Coupling and Supercurrent Nonreciprocity in Twisted NbSe2/NbSe2 van der Waals Junctions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06304)
*Seung-Gi Lee,Kwon-Neong Jung,Jae-Kuen Kim,Jae-Chun Jeon,Jiho Yoon,Stuart S. P. Parkin,Kun-Rok Jeon*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文通过实验研究扭转NbSe2/NbSe2垂直约瑟夫森结中的超导输运，发现超电流整流效率与扭转角无关，而是源于界面无序，而非扭转角控制的动量匹配。界面退化可将整流效率提升至近30%，表明超电流非互易性的主导起源是界面无序。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 范德华约瑟夫森结（van der Waals Josephson junctions）中超电流非互易性（supercurrent nonreciprocity）的微观起源尚存争议，尤其是扭转角（twist-angle）工程在层状超导体（layered superconductors）中的作用尚未厘清。本文旨在通过系统的实验研究区分扭转角控制与界面无序对超电流二极管效应的贡献。

Method: 采用干法转移（dry transfer）制备具有可控晶向对准和化学洁净界面的扭转NbSe2/NbSe2垂直约瑟夫森结；利用高分辨透射电子显微镜（high-resolution transmission electron microscopy, HRTEM）直接确定扭转角并评估界面质量；通过对比强耦合与弱耦合结，并结合人为界面退化处理，系统研究超电流整流行为。

Result: 约瑟夫森耦合强度显著依赖于扭转角，特征电压在等效晶向附近最大，在中间角度受到抑制；但超电流二极管效率（supercurrent diode efficiency）极小且无系统性的扭转角依赖。弱耦合结表现出增强的二极管响应，且界面退化可将其提升至近30%；非互易性随磁场强度呈不规则变化。

Conclusion: 约瑟夫森耦合（Josephson coupling）与超电流非互易性在扭转NbSe2/NbSe2结中实现了明确解耦（decoupling）。界面无序（interface disorder）是超电流二极管响应的主导起源，而非扭转角控制的动量匹配（momentum matching）。该结果为解释范德华约瑟夫森器件中的非互易超导输运提供了关键基准。

Abstract: The microscopic origin of supercurrent nonreciprocity in van der Waals Josephson junctions remains under active debate, particularly regarding the role of twist-angle engineering in layered superconductors. Here, we investigate superconducting transport in twisted NbSe2/NbSe2 vertical Josephson junctions fabricated by dry transfer with controlled crystallographic alignment and chemically clean interfaces. High-resolution transmission electron microscopy is employed to directly determine the twist angle and assess interface quality. While the Josephson coupling strength exhibits a pronounced dependence on twist angle, with characteristic voltages maximized near crystallographically equivalent orientations and suppressed at intermediate angles, the supercurrent diode efficiency remains negligibly small and shows no systematic twist-angle dependence. In contrast, enhanced diode-like responses emerge only in weakly coupled junctions exhibiting interfacial disorder and reduced transparency. Deliberate interface degradation further amplifies the apparent nonreciprocity, yielding diode efficiencies approaching 30% together with an irregular magnetic-field-strength dependence. These results establish a clear decoupling between Josephson coupling and supercurrent nonreciprocity in twisted NbSe2/NbSe2 junctions. Our findings identify interface disorder, rather than twist-angle-controlled momentum matching, as the dominant origin of the observed diode response and provide a critical benchmark for interpreting nonreciprocal superconducting transport in van der Waals Josephson devices.

</details>


### [171] [Anomalously high quasiparticle thermal conductivity in the underdoped cuprate superconductor HgBa$_{2}$CuO$_{4+δ}$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06332)
*Jordan Baglo,Quentin Barthélemy,Étienne Lefrançois,Anne Forget,Dorothée Colson,Cyril Proust,Louis Taillefer*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 通过对欠掺杂HgBa₂CuO₄₊δ (Hg1201) 单层铜氧化物超导体的极低温面内纵向热导率测量，提取了节状准粒子速度比 v_F/v_Δ = 23 ± 3，该值异常大于同类掺杂的其他铜氧化物。结合正常态准粒子比热异常，表明费米面上有超过一个能带穿过节线，暗示存在量子振荡观测到的单个小电子口袋之外的其他费米面结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Hg1201 是研究铜氧化物超导体（cuprate superconductor）的理想体系，因其单层 CuO₂ 结构且无序度极低。本文旨在通过测量其极低温热导率，提取节状准粒子速度比（nodal quasiparticle velocity ratio）v_F/v_Δ，以揭示其费米面（Fermi surface）拓扑的非常规特征。

Method: 在稀释制冷机温度下测量欠掺杂 Hg1201（T_c = 76 K，p = 0.11）的面内纵向热导率（in-plane longitudinal thermal conductivity）κ，并假设费米面每个象限仅存在一条线节点（line node），从热导率数据提取准粒子速度比 v_F/v_Δ。

Result: 提取的 v_F/v_Δ = 23 ± 3，该值相比同类掺杂的其他铜氧化物异常偏大。结合此前报道的 Hg1201 在正常态准粒子比热（quasiparticle specific heat）的异常高值，表明有超过一个费米面能带（Fermi surface sheet）穿越节线，暗示存在比量子振荡（quantum oscillations）所探测到的单个小电子口袋（small electron pocket）更复杂的费米面结构。

Conclusion: Hg1201 中异常大的 v_F/v_Δ 和正常态比热数据共同指向其费米面拓扑存在多个能带穿过节线，暗示可能存在量子振荡未直接观测到的额外费米面结构。这一发现对理解铜氧化物超导体的低能电子态和配对对称性具有重要启示。

Abstract: The single-layer cuprate superconductor HgBa$_{2}$CuO$_{4+δ}$ (Hg1201) is an ideal candidate for investigating many properties of cuprates with minimal disorder and without the complication of multiple CuO$_2$ layers. Here we measure the in-plane longitudinal thermal conductivity $κ$ of underdoped Hg1201 ($T_c$ = 76 K, $p$ = 0.11) at dilution refrigerator temperatures to extract the nodal quasiparticle velocity ratio $v_F/v_Δ$. Assuming contributions from only a single line node per quadrant on the Fermi surface leads to a value of $v_F/v_Δ$ = $23 \pm 3$, anomalously large compared to other cuprates at similar dopings. In conjunction with the anomalously high quasiparticle specific heat of Hg1201 in the normal state reported previously at a similar doping, this points to more than one Fermi surface sheet crossing the nodal line, suggesting the presence of more than the single small electron pocket detected by quantum oscillations.

</details>


### [172] [Effect of charge-imbalance potential relaxation on the high-frequency vortex dynamics and kinetic inductance of superconducting circuits](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06390)
*R. I. Kinzibaev,V. S. Stolyarov,A. S. Mel'nikov*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文从含时金茨堡-朗道方程（time-dependent Ginzburg-Landau equations）出发，推导了考虑耗散（dissipation）和延迟（retardation）效应的阿布里科索夫涡旋（Abrikosov vortex）运动方程，发现电荷不平衡势（charge-imbalance potential）的弛豫在涡旋延迟动力学中起关键作用，且延迟效应在接近超导临界温度 $T_{c}$ 时发散的时标下显现，进而显著影响超导电路在高频范围的动能电感（kinetic inductance）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 揭示电荷不平衡势的弛豫过程如何影响第二类超导体（type-II superconductor）中阿布里科索夫涡旋的延迟动力学（retarded dynamics），并解释该效应对超导电路高频特性中动能电感的磁场依赖性。

Method: 以含时金茨堡-朗道方程为起点，推导同时包含耗散与延迟效应的涡旋运动方程；其中延迟项由电荷不平衡势的动力学控制。

Result: 发现了电荷不平衡势的弛豫是涡旋延迟动力学的关键因素，延迟效应在接近超导临界温度 $T_{c}$ 时特征时标发散；该延迟效应显著影响超导电路的动能电感，进而导致高频范围内各类超导器件特性对磁场的依赖性。

Conclusion: 涡旋动力学中的延迟效应（由电荷不平衡势弛豫引起）是理解超导器件高频磁场依赖特性的重要机制，对超导电路设计具有潜在影响。

Abstract: We show that relaxation of the charge-imbalance potential plays a key role in the retarded dynamics of Abrikosov vortices in a type-II superconducting sample carrying a microwave current. Starting from the time-dependent Ginzburg--Landau equations we derive the vortex equation of motion accounting both the dissipation and retardation effects. The retardation is governed by the dynamics of the charge-imbalance potential and reveals itself at characteristic timescales diverging near the superconducting critical temperature $T_{c}$. These retardation effects in vortex dynamics strongly affect the kinetic inductance of superconducting circuits being, thus, responsible for the magnetic field dependence of characteristics of different superconducting devices in the high frequency range.

</details>


### [173] [Multi-Knob Switchable Chiral Superconductivity Quartet in Rhombohedral Graphene](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.06520)
*Zhenqi Hua,Shenyong Ye,Phatthanon Pattanakanvijit,Gang Shi,Tonghang Han,Emily Aitken,Jixiang Yang,Junseok Seo,Haoyang Liu,Ran Hao,Kaitai Xiao,Jiaxing Guo,Vo Tien Phong,Kenji Watanabe,Takashi Taniguchi,Chunli Huang,Cyprian Lewandowski,Long Ju,Peng Xiong,Zhengguang Lu*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文报道在菱方六层石墨烯（R6G）中发现了可由面外磁场诱导的新型超导态（SCH），它与手性超导态（CSC）共存，并可从全部四种自旋-谷同位旋味（spin-valley isospin flavors）实现超导电性，建立起可切换的手性超导体四重态（chiral-superconductor quartet）。该工作将菱方石墨烯确立为用于不同同位旋极化超导电性的多调控平台，可用于可编程超导网络及可能的马约拉纳零模（Majorana modes）器件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 手性超导体（chiral superconductors）破坏轨道时间反演对称性（orbital time-reversal symmetry），可能承载具有非阿贝尔统计（non-Abelian statistics）的拓扑准粒子。菱方石墨烯中的超导电性源自自旋-谷极化四分之一金属（quarter-metal, QM）母态，并展现出独特的电阻磁滞现象，指示轨道时间反演对称性破缺。探索并调控此类超导电性的完整自旋-谷味（spin-valley flavors）对于实现新型超导和拓扑器件至关重要，但此前尚属空白。

Method: 对菱方六层石墨烯（R6G）进行了输运测量（transport measurements），系统扫描了磁场 $H_\perp$、载流子密度 $n$ 和栅极位移场 $D$ 构建的完整参数空间。通过量子振荡（quantum oscillations）和反常霍尔测量（anomalous Hall measurements）表征了母态的性质。

Result: 发现了一种由面外磁场诱导的新型超导态（SCH），在 0.8 T 以上出现并持续至 1.6 T，可通过磁场、载流子密度和位移场开关。SCH 源自场诱导的四分之一金属（QM'）母相，其轨道磁化方向与零场 QM 相反。在完整的 $(n, D, H_\perp)$ 参数空间中，可从全部四种自旋-谷同位旋味实现超导电性，建立了可切换的手性超导体四重态。

Conclusion: 将母态切换解释为 Kane-Mele 型自旋-谷分裂（Kane-Mele-like spin-valley splitting）与磁场耦合到自旋-谷依赖磁矩之间的竞争。菱方石墨烯成为一个多调控旋钮（multi-knob）平台，可用于不同同位旋极化超导电性，实现可编程超导网络以及沿畴壁（domain walls）可能存在的马约拉纳模（Majorana modes）。

Abstract: Chiral superconductors break orbital time-reversal symmetry and may host topological quasiparticles with non-Abelian statistics. In rhombohedral graphene, superconductivity develops from a spin-valley-polarized quarter-metal (QM) parent state and features unique magnetic hysteresis of resistance that indicates orbital time-reversal-symmetry-breaking. Exploring and controlling the full spin-valley flavors of such superconductivity could enable novel superconducting and topological devices, but have remained unexplored. Here we report transport measurements on rhombohedral hexalayer graphene (R6G), which reveal a new superconducting state (SCH) that is induced by an out-of-plane magnetic field, in addition to chiral superconductivity (CSC) similar to those observed in thinner layers. This SCH state emerges above 0.8 T, persists up to 1.6 T and can be switched on/off by magnetic field $H_\perp$, carrier density $n$, and gate displacement field $D$. Quantum oscillations and anomalous Hall measurements show that SCH stems from a field-induced quarter-metal (QM$'$) parent phase, which carries orbital magnetization opposite to that of the zero-field QM. Across the full $(n, D, H_\perp)$ parameter space, superconductivity can be realized from all four spin-valley isospin flavors, establishing a switchable chiral-superconductor quartet in R6G. We interpret the parent-state switching as arising from competition between a Kane-Mele-like spin-valley splitting and magnetic-field coupling to spin-valley-dependent magnetic moments. Our work establishes rhombohedral graphene as a multi-knob platform for different isospin-polarized superconductivities, which enables programmable superconducting networks with possible Majorana modes along domain walls.

</details>

# cs.SE [[Back]](#toc)

### [174] [Articulating Assumptions in AI-Generated Scientific Analyses through Task Decomposition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05762)
*Ahmed Hammad,Mihoko Nojiri*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 提出了一种基于量纲的语义差分（quantity grounded semantic differencing）多智能体框架，用于分析和比较由大语言模型（LLM）生成的科学程序。该框架通过将代码生成、执行、追踪和验证分配给不同智能体，重构关键输出量的计算过程、识别预期分析与实现代码之间的差异，并在代码生成前检测用户指令中的歧义。在对撞机物理分析上的验证表明，模块化任务分解相比单一提示词（single prompt）方法显著提升了透明性和可靠性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM生成的科学分析代码必须可理解且可复现，但由于自然语言规范（natural language specification）和生成实现（generated implementation）中均存在不确定性，即使可执行代码也无法清晰说明正在计算哪些量或哪些假设决定了最终结果。现有方法缺乏对上述不确定性的系统性处理。

Method: 提出量纲语义差分（quantity grounded semantic differencing）多智能体框架，将代码生成、执行、追踪和验证分配给各自独立的智能体（agent）；引入指令歧义检测模块，在代码生成前建议用户改写；采用模块化设计，可通过替换领域特定资源（domain-specific resources）适配不同科学领域。

Result: 在对撞机物理分析的验证中，模块化任务分解相较于之前的单一提示词方法显著提升了透明性和可靠性，并使更小规模的模型也能完整执行整个工作流。

Conclusion: 该多智能体框架通过结构化分解和歧义预检，增强了LLM生成科学代码的可理解性与可复现性，具备跨领域应用的潜力。

Abstract: Scientific results produced by LLM generated analysis code must be understandable and reproducible. However, uncertainty can arise at different stages of the process, both in the original natural language specification and in the generated implementation. As a result, even executable code may not provide a clear understanding of which quantities are being computed or which assumptions determine the final results. To address this challenge, we introduce quantity grounded semantic differencing, a multi-agent framework for analyzing and comparing scientific programs generated by LLMs. The framework assigns code generation, execution, tracing, and validation to separate agents, allowing it to reconstruct how key output quantities are produced and to identify differences between the intended analysis and the implemented code. We also introduce a module that inspects ambiguities in the initial user instruction and suggests alternative rewrites before code generation. Its modular design enables application to different scientific domains by replacing domain specific resources while preserving the same workflow. We validate the framework on representative collider physics analyses. The results demonstrate that the modular task decomposition enhances both transparency and reliability relative to the previous single prompt approach, while enabling substantially smaller models to execute the complete workflow.

</details>
